# RGE Handoff Document

> **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 pass-record-integration **sub-γ: docs-only post-depth measurement-gap acknowledgment, IMPLEMENTED — chapter close**): closes the Phase 6 pass-record-integration chapter at the docs-honest layer. **No new perf number, no harness change, no architecture change.** Per user direction "If the existing Gate A harness only hits the old gfx/pre-depth route, don't update BASELINE.md from that data. In that case, scope a tiny post-depth measurement harness or halt and reframe." combined with pre-dispatch inspection-first verdict that the existing harness DOES only hit the pre-depth gfx path, sub-γ takes the third path (docs-only acknowledgment) — explicitly acknowledges the post-depth production-path measurement gap rather than fabricating a synthetic perf claim or scoping a non-tiny harness chapter. **Pre-dispatch inspection-first verdict**: existing Gate A harness at `crates/gfx/tests/gate_a_simple_scene_60fps.rs:128-185` uses `LitMeshPipeline::new(...)` (no depth-state) + `record_lit_mesh_pass(.., None)` (no depth attachment) — exercises NEITHER the sub-α `LitMeshPipeline::new_with_depth(.., Some(...))` additive constructor API NOR the sub-β `build_resource_map(...)` substrate consumption over `CompiledFrameGraph`-driven `TexturePool` NOR the `editor-shell::render_path::render_frame` production path that sub-β wired. The 0.112 ms claim from 2026-05-11 (NVIDIA GeForce RTX 4060 Ti / Vulkan / DiscreteGpu / 1280×720 / shared PSO; commit `35e5078`) is therefore VALID for the pre-depth gfx path and structurally SILENT about the post-depth production path; updating `BASELINE.md` from existing harness data would falsely certify the post-depth path the harness doesn't measure. **Three options surfaced** (A — extend Gate A harness with a depth-attached second fn, ~80-120 LoC of additive setup, still gfx-level synthetic NOT editor-shell-integrated; B — true editor-shell post-depth harness, requires non-winit "headless render mode" — substantial multi-dispatch chapter; C — docs-only acknowledgment, ~20 LoC across 5 docs); user chose **Option C** as the honest chapter close per "No synthetic perf number, no new harness right now. The useful discovery is that Gate A still measures the pre-depth gfx path and says nothing about `editor-shell::render_path::render_frame`; pretending otherwise would make the chapter look more certified than it is." **Docs delta** (5 files, 0 source): (a) `plans/IMPLEMENTATION.md:468` Gate A marker softened — original `[CLOSED 2026-05-11 on recorder host only: ...]` annotation core text preserved (clarification: now reads "on recorder host AND pre-depth gfx path only" with explicit `LitMeshPipeline::new(...)` / `record_lit_mesh_pass(.., None)` configuration enumeration in the certification scope) + appended new annotation block `[POST-DEPTH PRODUCTION-PATH MEASUREMENT GAP — sub-γ docs-only 2026-05-12: ...]` explicitly stating the 0.112 ms claim is VALID for the pre-depth gfx path and structurally SILENT about the post-depth production path, with re-measurement DEFERRED until one of three concrete paths exists (synthetic depth-attached gfx harness OR non-winit editor-shell perf harness OR manual user report); cross-references `BASELINE.md §6.3` for the gap-note details. > **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 pass-record-integration **sub-β: production depth wire, IMPLEMENTED**): production `editor-shell::render_path` now consumes the frame-graph transient-texture substrate end-to-end — `TexturePool` + `BufferPool` + `CompiledFrameGraph` constructed at `init_render_state`; `build_resource_map` drives per-frame transient depth-texture acquisition via the dispatch-122 builder-layer discipline (NO direct `TexturePool::acquire` from the pass-record site, preserving ADR-118 L213's load-bearing lifetime rule); `Some(&depth_view)` flows through the inline `RenderPassDepthStencilAttachment` literal in `render_frame`; the shared `LitMeshPipeline` is constructed via the sub-α additive `new_with_depth(.., Some(DepthStateKey::new(Depth24Plus, false, LessEqual)))` path with the existing depth-state choice ratified by the user direction "Keep depth format tied to the acquired texture format and `LessEqual`, `depth_write_enabled: false` per the existing future note". **Honest scope (per user direction "Treat 'no visible behavior change' claim carefully in docs")**: this dispatch consumes the transient substrate and prevents a depth-state regression that adding a populated depth buffer would otherwise introduce (without the `depth_write_enabled: false` choice, identical cuboid+overlay positions would Z-fight against the populated buffer); but does NOT prove a user-visible Z-fight fix — that claim requires sub-γ measurement or a visual harness, neither of which exists yet. **Pre-dispatch inspection-first verdict**: substrate-disciplined path (`FrameGraph` + `ResourceMap`) is workable but heavy for one transient resource (3 new `Option<T>` state fields on `EditorShell` — `texture_pool` / `buffer_pool` / `compiled_frame_graph` — and per-frame builder-layer ceremony of `tex_pool.begin_frame() + buf_pool.begin_frame() + build_resource_map() + map.texture_map[&rid].clone() + create_view()` before the existing inline render-pass body); direct `TexturePool::acquire` would be cleaner but is explicitly forbidden by the dispatch-122 substrate-discipline rule ("pass-record sites must NOT call `pool.acquire` directly"). Per user guardrail "If TexturePool / ResourceMap ownership makes per-frame acquire awkward, halt and re-scope rather than creating a second resource lifetime path", the heavy path was chosen — bypassing creates a "second resource lifetime path" inconsistent with the substrate design. **Substrate consumption flow (per dispatch-122 recipe)**: (a) `init_render_state` step-5 upgrades `LitMeshPipeline::new(.., format)` to `LitMeshPipeline::new_with_depth(.., format, Some(lit_mesh_depth_state()))` — the additive sub-α constructor; (b) new step-5b constructs `TexturePool::new()` + `BufferPool::new()` (the latter unused but required by `build_resource_map`'s signature; future transient-buffer consumers populate `map.buffer_map` from the same builder pass with no further plumbing churn) + builds a single-pass `FrameGraph` declaring one write of `DEPTH_RESOURCE_ID` at format `Depth24Plus` with `RENDER_ATTACHMENT` usage + compiles to `CompiledFrameGraph` via the new `build_lit_mesh_compiled_frame_graph(width, height)` helper; (c) step-7 stashes all three new state objects alongside existing fields; (d) `render_frame` opens with a scoped block containing `tex_pool.begin_frame() + buf_pool.begin_frame()` (ADR-118 D4 ring rotation) + `build_resource_map(compiled, device, &mut tex_pool, &mut buf_pool)` (Err → warn + `window.request_redraw()` + return true, mirroring existing `get_current_texture` failure handling) + `Arc::clone(map.texture_map.get(&DEPTH_RESOURCE_ID).expect(...))` (`expect` justified — well-formed single-pass FrameGraph guarantees descriptor presence; `MissingDescriptorForGroup` cannot arise) + `depth_arc.create_view(&Default::default())`, then proceeds with the existing immutable borrows on neighbouring state — the only delta to the inline render-pass body is the `depth_stencil_attachment: Some(RenderPassDepthStencilAttachment { view: &depth_view, depth_ops: Some(Operations { load: Clear(1.0), store: Store }), stencil_ops: None })` literal in-place (NO refactor of the inline render pass into a `record_lit_mesh_pass(...)` call per user direction "Do not refactor the whole inline render pass into the helper unless it is the smallest way to pass depth cleanly"); (e) `resize_render_path` rebuilds `compiled_frame_graph` via `build_lit_mesh_compiled_frame_graph(new_w, new_h)` because `TextureDescriptor` is keyed on width/height and the descriptor flows verbatim into `TexturePool`'s free-list identity. **Depth-state choice rationale**: both the cuboid draw and the highlight-overlay draw share the single `LitMeshPipeline`; with `depth_write_enabled: false` on both, the depth buffer stays at the `Clear(1.0)` value for the entire frame, every fragment passes `LessEqual` against 1.0, render order determines visibility (overlay drawn second wins where it draws) — pre-sub-β no-depth visual behavior is preserved EXACTLY while the transient substrate is consumed end-to-end. The Z-fight that a `depth_write_enabled: true` shared pipeline would otherwise produce (identical cuboid+overlay positions racing for the depth-test winner) is structurally prevented — regression prevention, NOT a user-visible Z-fight fix from a today-broken baseline (today's baseline doesn't have Z-fight either because there's no depth attachment). **Borrow-flow design**: `render_frame` does the pool work in a scoped block FIRST (`&mut self.texture_pool` + `&mut self.buffer_pool` + immutable borrow of `self.gfx_ctx` via `gfx_ctx.device()`; all on distinct fields, accepted by Rust's borrow checker via struct-field-level borrow splitting) before re-acquiring the existing immutable borrows on neighbouring state at the function continuation — keeps borrow lifetimes non-overlapping WITHOUT introducing `RefCell` / `Mutex` (no `Mutex` for `Send + 'static` reasons; `RefCell` would change the field-borrow story for `gfx_ctx` patterns elsewhere). **Acceptable bounded leak on resize**: when surface size changes, the new `CompiledFrameGraph` carries a new `TextureDescriptor`; old textures keyed on the previous descriptor drain through the ring rotation and accumulate in `free_lists` as stale entries (bounded by `FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT=2` allocations per resize event — at most 2 stale textures of the old size per resize). Acceptable for v0; pool-level free-list pruning is out of scope (would surface as its own substrate-level dispatch if scale pressure demands). **New `EditorShell` state fields (3 total, all `pub(crate) Option<T>`)**: `texture_pool: Option<TexturePool>` / `buffer_pool: Option<BufferPool>` / `compiled_frame_graph: Option<CompiledFrameGraph>`. Initialized to `None` in both `EditorShell::new` (delegates to `with_world`) and `EditorShell::with_world`. **New constants in `render_path.rs`**: `DEPTH_FORMAT: wgpu::TextureFormat = Depth24Plus` (wgpu portable depth format); `DEPTH_RESOURCE_ID: ResourceId = ResourceId::from_bytes([b'r', b'g', b'e', b'.', b'e', b'd', b's', b'h', b'.', b'd', b'e', b'p', b't', b'h', 0, 1])` (ASCII prefix informational; opaque-ness preserved per `ResourceId` contract); `build_lit_mesh_compiled_frame_graph(surface_width, surface_height) -> CompiledFrameGraph` helper (single-pass graph with one depth-texture write at given dims); `lit_mesh_depth_state() -> DepthStateKey` (`Depth24Plus, depth_write_enabled: false, LessEqual`). **Highlight-overlay future-note rewrite**: the comment at the highlight-overlay site previously read "NOTE for future depth-buffer landing: ... When a depth attachment is added, this pipeline will need its `DepthStencilState` set to `LessEqual` with `depth_write_enabled = false` — out of sub-ε scope." Now reads "Post sub-β: the depth attachment is now populated ... The Z-fight that a `depth_write_enabled: true` pipeline would produce here is structurally prevented." Reflects the post-sub-β architectural state without claiming visible behavior change. **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: NO change to `crates/gfx/src/**` (substrate complete; sub-α landed the consumer API; sub-β just consumes); NO `LitMeshPipeline::new_with_depth` / `new_cached_with_depth` / `record_lit_mesh_pass` signature change (sub-α shape preserved); NO change to `crates/gfx/src/pso_cache.rs` / `frame_graph/**`; NO Gate A marker update at `plans/IMPLEMENTATION.md:468` / `BASELINE.md` (sub-γ scope when post-depth perf is measured); NO new ADR / new lint / new exemption / new doctrine doc / new §18 companion; NO pipeline splitting (single shared `LitMeshPipeline` for cuboid + overlay; one `DepthStateKey`); NO refactor of the inline render pass into a `record_lit_mesh_pass(...)` call (kept inline per user direction; smallest delta is the inline `depth_stencil_attachment` literal); NO direct `TexturePool::acquire` bypassing `FrameGraph + build_resource_map` (substrate-discipline rule preserved); NO `Cargo.toml` / `Cargo.lock` change (`rge-gfx` already re-exported every type needed); NO `tools/architecture-lints/**` change; NO `unsafe`; NO new integration test (Gate C boundary test at `crates/editor-shell/tests/render_input_boundary.rs` exercises the `RenderHandoff` invariant and passes unchanged — regression coverage at the editor-shell production surface). **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo +nightly fmt --check -p rge-editor-shell --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-editor-shell` apply normalizing a `let-expect` wrap style in `build_lit_mesh_compiled_frame_graph`); `cargo build -p rge-editor-shell --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` clean (4.43s — full editor-shell + transitive recompile); `cargo test -p rge-editor-shell --no-fail-fast --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` 108/108 PASS (67 lib + 3 camera_picker_smoke + 6 editor_coord_face_selection + 4 pie_round_trip + 13 render_input_boundary + 6 snapshot_correctness + 6 time_scale_test + 3 timing_baseline + 1 ignored release-only `editor_frame_idle` timing harness; byte-identical to pre-sub-β; Gate C invariant via `render_input_boundary::gate_c_held_snapshot_stable_across_subsequent_publishes` confirmed); `cargo test --workspace --no-fail-fast --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` = **2429 passed / 0 failed / 19 ignored** (was 2429 post-sub-α; +0 net — sub-β is wire only, no new explicit tests by design); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary PASS, byte-identical exemption count). Files modified (2 source + 3 docs): `crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs` (3 new `pub(crate)` `Option<T>` state fields on `EditorShell` struct + `None` initializers in both `EditorShell::new` and `EditorShell::with_world`); `crates/editor-shell/src/render_path.rs` (new `rge_gfx` imports: `build_resource_map`, `BufferPool`, `CompiledFrameGraph`, `DepthStateKey`, `FrameGraph`, `ResourceClassDescriptor`, `ResourceId`, `TextureDescriptor`, `TexturePool` + new `DEPTH_FORMAT` / `DEPTH_RESOURCE_ID` constants + new `build_lit_mesh_compiled_frame_graph` / `lit_mesh_depth_state` helpers + `init_render_state` step-5 pipeline upgraded to `new_with_depth(.., Some(lit_mesh_depth_state()))` + new step-5b pool/graph construction + step-7 stash extended with 3 new fields + `render_frame` opens with pool-begin-frame + `build_resource_map` + depth view extraction in a scoped block + inline `RenderPassDepthStencilAttachment` literal + post-sub-β rewrite of the highlight-overlay future-note comment; existing pipeline / camera / light / material / mesh borrows + the inline render-pass body otherwise byte-identical); `Status.md` (snapshot prepend); `change.md` (entry); `HANDOFF.md` (this entry). **Phase 6 pass-record-integration chapter status (Path B)**: sub-α + sub-β both LANDED — consumer-API shape AND substrate consumption end-to-end in production; sub-γ scope (Gate A re-measurement on the post-depth path — `BASELINE.md` updated with post-depth perf claim + `IMPLEMENTATION.md:468` marker softened with both pre-depth + post-depth perf claims) remains OPEN with no commitment. Visual harness for the Z-fight-fix claim (separate scope; would let the regression-prevention claim graduate to a user-visible-fix claim) also OPEN. **NEXT**: TBD by user.

> **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 pass-record-integration **sub-α: `LitMeshPipeline` + `record_lit_mesh_pass` depth-readiness, IMPLEMENTED**): opens the Phase 6 pass-record-integration chapter (Path B per pre-dispatch inspection) — `record_lit_mesh_pass` consuming transient resources from the frame-graph substrate (dispatches 119-123) — with sub-α as the bounded immediate dispatch: API-shaping without production change. **NO production wire**; no transient texture allocation; no Gate A marker change. **Pre-dispatch inspection-first verdict**: `record_lit_mesh_pass` is TEST-ONLY today (production `crates/editor-shell/src/render_path.rs:244-294` inlines a byte-identical 50-LoC render-pass body); no existing transient consumer in the workspace (all GPU resources currently owned — Camera/Light/Material UBOs, MeshLit vertex/index buffers, Material texture); natural first transient consumer is a depth buffer (Z-fight bug documented at `render_path.rs:281-285` for the highlight overlay); adding depth-testing trips Gate A re-validation per HANDOFF.md dispatch 123 ("runtime-perf re-validation against Gate A's recorder-host CLOSED marker is deferred until real pass-record sites grow transient-resource consumers"). Path B (full depth-buffer chapter) opened with sub-α only as immediate dispatch — sub-β (production wire + Z-fight fix) and sub-γ (Gate A re-measurement) DEFERRED with no commitment; sub-α stands alone if priorities shift. **API shape (additive — `LitMeshPipeline::new` / `new_cached` byte-identical signatures preserved per user direction "preserves production `render_path.rs` and makes sub-β a clean upgrade rather than a surprise signature churn")**: NEW `LitMeshPipeline::new_with_depth(.., depth_state: Option<DepthStateKey>) -> Result<Self, _>` (borrows `ctx.pso_cache()` and delegates to `new_cached_with_depth`); NEW `LitMeshPipeline::new_cached_with_depth(.., depth_state: Option<DepthStateKey>, cache: &mut PipelineCache) -> Result<Self, _>` (builds `PsoKey` with `depth_state` passed through — the 4th slot was already shaped in the bc51cc0 PSO cache landing, previously hardcoded to `None`); existing `new` body now reads `Self::new_with_depth(.., None)`; existing `new_cached` body now reads `Self::new_cached_with_depth(.., None, cache)` — byte-identical behavioral preservation at the existing API. `build_pipeline` gains a `depth_state: Option<DepthStateKey>` param; when `Some`, populates `wgpu::DepthStencilState { format: d.format, depth_write_enabled: Some(d.depth_write_enabled), depth_compare: Some(d.depth_compare), stencil: StencilState::default(), bias: DepthBiasState::default() }` (the `Some(...)` wrap on `depth_write_enabled` and `depth_compare` is a wgpu 29.0.3 API shape — caught at the first build attempt and corrected); when `None`, `depth_stencil: None` byte-identical pre-sub-α. **`record_lit_mesh_pass` signature change**: final param `depth_view: Option<&wgpu::TextureView>` added; when `Some`, populates `depth_stencil_attachment` with `wgpu::RenderPassDepthStencilAttachment { view, depth_ops: Some(Operations { load: LoadOp::Clear(1.0), store: StoreOp::Store }), stencil_ops: None }` (no `depth_slice` field on the depth-stencil attachment — that's color-attachment-only in wgpu 29; corrected at first build attempt). **Pipeline-vs-attachment matching is caller's responsibility**: pipeline from `new(..)` / `new_cached(..)` (depth_state=None) requires `record_lit_mesh_pass(.., None)`; pipeline from `new_with_depth(.., Some(_))` requires `Some(&depth_view)`. Mismatch is a wgpu validation error at record time — documented in the `record_lit_mesh_pass` doc-comment. **Tests (+3 net inline in `lit_mesh_pipeline::tests`, all GPU-gated via `ctx_or_skip!`)**: `lit_mesh_pipeline_new_with_depth_none_matches_new_via_pso_cache` — `new(..)` and `new_with_depth(.., None)` produce pipelines aliasing the same `Arc<wgpu::RenderPipeline>` via the context-owned PSO cache (delegation invariant proven via `Arc::ptr_eq`); `lit_mesh_pipeline_new_with_depth_some_produces_distinct_pso_cache_entry` — `Some(depth_state)` produces a distinct cache entry from `None` (silent-pipeline-collision boundary pinned at the LitMeshPipeline level; the boundary that `PsoKey`'s 4th slot was designed to prevent now actively enforced at the LitMesh consumer); `record_lit_mesh_pass_with_depth_attachment_succeeds` — full path proves the API shape end-to-end: `new_with_depth(.., Some(Depth24Plus / depth_write_enabled=true / Less))` + `Depth24Plus` texture creation + `record_lit_mesh_pass(.., Some(&depth_view))` + `device.poll(wait_indefinitely)` — reaching past the poll without a wgpu validation panic IS the proof per user direction "API-shaped proofs only, NO visual assertion (Z-fight claim belongs to sub-β)". **Test call site updates (4 byte-identical `None` additions across the 4 existing `record_lit_mesh_pass` consumers)**: `lit_mesh_pipeline.rs::tests` (2 sites at L817 / L982); `crates/gfx/tests/gate_a_simple_scene_60fps.rs` (1 site at L176 — Gate A test stays byte-identical at the perf level, `depth_view=None` preserves the pre-allocator triangle path Gate A certified on commit `35e5078`); > **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 frame-graph chapter — **dispatch 122: `ResourceMap` builder + `AliasingGroup::max_descriptor` analytical helper, IMPLEMENTED**): lands the per-frame `ResourceId → Arc<wgpu::{Texture,Buffer}>` mapping that consumes dispatches 120 (`e050e06`) + 121 (`c356f32`) and structurally enforces ADR-118's `acquire()` dedup contract. NEW `crates/gfx/src/frame_graph/resource_map.rs` (~330L total — ~50L module doc + impl + 5 unit tests). Two new public types: **`ResourceMap`** = `{ texture_map: BTreeMap<ResourceId, Arc<wgpu::Texture>>, buffer_map: BTreeMap<ResourceId, Arc<wgpu::Buffer>> }` per ADR-118 D2 (pools separate at the allocator level; class discrimination happens at the builder boundary based on each group's max descriptor); **`ResourceMapError::MissingDescriptorForGroup(AliasingGroupId)`** — diagnostic-only failure mode for partial / hand-built `CompiledFrameGraph`s. **`build_resource_map(compiled, device, &mut tex_pool, &mut buf_pool)`** iterates `CompiledFrameGraph::aliasing_groups()` exactly once, computes the max descriptor per group via the new `AliasingGroup::max_descriptor` analytical helper, calls each pool's `acquire(...)` exactly ONCE per group, then fans the returned `Arc` to every `ResourceId` member of the group. This is THE structural enforcement of ADR-118 L213's load-bearing dedup contract — no internal pool dedup is needed because the iteration discipline at the builder makes intra-group acquires impossible by construction. **`AliasingGroup::max_descriptor` helper** (~30L delta in `compile.rs`): `filter_map(|rid| descriptors.get(rid)).max_by_key(|d| d.byte_size_estimate())` over the group's `ResourceId`s; returns `None` for empty groups or groups whose members have no descriptors registered (the precondition that surfaces as `MissingDescriptorForGroup` at the builder boundary). **Re-exports**: `frame_graph/mod.rs` adds `pub mod resource_map;` + `pub use resource_map::{ResourceMap, ResourceMapError, build_resource_map};`; `lib.rs` adds the three idents to the existing `frame_graph::` re-export. **ADR-118 wording softening (single bullet L213)**: "Dispatch 122 — `FrameRecorder` integration. Wires the pools to the existing `record_lit_mesh_pass` surface…" → "Dispatch 122 — `ResourceMap` builder + `AliasingGroup::max_descriptor` analytical helper. > **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 frame-graph chapter — **dispatch 121: BufferPool MVP per ADR-118 D2+D3+D4+D5, IMPLEMENTED**): lands the descriptor-keyed transient-buffer pool as a clean mirror of dispatch 120's TexturePool (commit `e050e06`). NEW `crates/gfx/src/frame_graph/buffer_pool.rs` (268L: ~50L module doc + impl + 5 unit tests) introduces a single public type **`BufferPool`** owning `[SlotState; 2]` ring + `current_slot: usize` (identical shape to `TexturePool`). Per-slot state: `free_lists: HashMap<(BufferDescriptor, AliasingGroupId), Vec<Arc<wgpu::Buffer>>>` (keyed per ADR-118 D3) + `active: Vec<(BufferDescriptor, AliasingGroupId, Arc<wgpu::Buffer>)>` (flat triple — descriptor carried alongside Arc because wgpu 29's `Buffer` does not expose original descriptor for free-list routing at slot reset; identical rationale to TexturePool). **Three public methods**: `new()` / `default()` start at slot 0; `begin_frame()` rotates slot + drains the new slot's `active` back to `free_lists` (D4 N=2 ring); `acquire(device, descriptor, group)` peeks free-list `(descriptor, group)`, falls back to `device.create_buffer(...)` via internal `allocate_buffer` helper (label = None per D1; `mapped_at_creation = false` per D1; size + usage from descriptor), pushes triple into `active`, returns `Arc<wgpu::Buffer>`. **`AliasingGroupId` REUSED from `texture_pool` via `use super::texture_pool::AliasingGroupId;`** — graph-time identity is shared across both pool kinds (ADR-118 D2 separates pool *types*, not *identities*); NO redefinition. **`FRAMES_IN_FLIGHT` duplicated as 1-LOC const** rather than hoisted (churn exceeds payoff at this dispatch's scope; both pools amend together if N changes). **`texture_pool.rs` BEHAVIORAL byte-identical** — only reference gained is by name via `AliasingGroupId` import. **Re-exports**: `frame_graph/mod.rs` adds `buffer_pool` module + `BufferPool` export; `lib.rs` adds `BufferPool` (formatter regrouped re-export line; semantically identical). **ADR-118 wording correction (single line L212)**: "Dispatch 120 — TexturePool + BufferPool MVP" → "Dispatch 120 — TexturePool MVP; dispatch 121 — BufferPool MVP (clean mirror)"; records the dispatch-120/121 split at the moment BufferPool makes the split true. Filenames updated to `texture_pool.rs` / `buffer_pool.rs` from `allocator.rs` placeholder. Not scope creep. **Tests (+5 net; workspace 2403 → 2408)**: BP-1 structural slot rotation; BP-2 GPU acquire returns Arc with strong_count=2; BP-3 GPU free-list-reuse via `Arc::as_ptr` equality after full ring round-trip — the load-bearing reuse proof; BP-4 GPU distinct groups, same descriptor → distinct allocations (D3 key includes group); BP-5 GPU distinct descriptors (size 4096 vs 8192), same group → distinct allocations. **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: NO `wgpu::Queue` interaction / uploads / `write_buffer` / `map_async` / `unmap` / staging workflows (D1 keeps those outside allocator); NO manual barriers (D6 trusts wgpu auto-tracking); NO `FrameRecorder` integration (dispatch 122); NO `TexturePool` BEHAVIORAL change; NO `GfxContext` mutation; NO async/fence ownership; NO serialized-graph support; NO `Cargo.toml` / `Cargo.lock`; NO `tools/architecture-lints/**`; NO `unsafe`; NO new ADR/lint/exemption; NO other gfx modules touched. **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-gfx` exit 0; `cargo build -p rge-gfx` clean; `cargo test -p rge-gfx --lib buffer_pool` 5/5 PASS; `cargo test --workspace --no-fail-fast` = **2408 passed / 0 failed** (was 2403; +5 exact target); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9+1 PASS, byte-identical). Files modified: NEW `crates/gfx/src/frame_graph/buffer_pool.rs` (268L); `crates/gfx/src/frame_graph/mod.rs` (+2L re-export delta); `crates/gfx/src/lib.rs` (+1 ident, formatter-regrouped); `docs/adr/ADR-118-frame-graph-transient-resource-allocator.md` (1-line L212 wording fix); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md`. **Phase 6 frame-graph chapter transition**: dispatch 120 TexturePool (`e050e06`) → **dispatch 121 BufferPool (THIS)** → dispatch 122 = `FrameRecorder` wiring → Phase 6 umbrella exit gate (60fps simple-scene). **DISPATCH 122 LOAD-BEARING CONTRACT — `acquire()` dedup**: caller MUST map each `AliasingGroupId` to one `Arc<wgpu::{Texture,Buffer}>` per frame. If two pass-record sites within the same aliasing group both call `pool.acquire(...)` independently, they receive DISTINCT allocations (free-list is per-key, not per-id) — defeating the D5 aliasing-group reuse promise. Concrete dispatch-122 FrameRecorder shape: build a `ResourceMap: BTreeMap<ResourceId, Arc<wgpu::Texture|Buffer>>` ONCE per frame (after `begin_frame()` calls) by iterating `CompiledFrameGraph::aliasing_groups()`, calling `acquire(...)` exactly once per group with the group's pre-computed max-descriptor (D5), and inserting each `ResourceId` in the group with a `clone()` of that single `Arc`. Pass-record code reads from the `ResourceMap` only — never calls `acquire` directly. Both pools have the identical `acquire(device, descriptor, group) -> Arc<wgpu::{Texture,Buffer}>` surface, so a single `ResourceMap`-build helper dispatches on `ResourceClassDescriptor::{Texture,Buffer}` to route to the appropriate pool. Next focus: **dispatch 122 `FrameRecorder` integration** — wires both pools to `record_lit_mesh_pass` via the ResourceMap pattern above.

> **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 frame-graph chapter — **dispatch 119: `ResourceDescriptor` types + frame-graph descriptor flow, IMPLEMENTED**): implements ADR-118 D7's first code step. NEW `crates/gfx/src/frame_graph/descriptor.rs` (~350L) introduces three public types: **`TextureDescriptor`** (9 wgpu-29 fields per ADR-118 D1 — `width / height / depth_or_array_layers / mip_level_count / sample_count / format / usage / dimension / view_dimension`; `label` + `mapped_at_creation` deliberately omitted per D1 to prevent pool over-fragmentation), **`BufferDescriptor`** (`size_bytes + usage` per D1), and **`ResourceClassDescriptor::{Texture(TextureDescriptor), Buffer(BufferDescriptor)}`** as the graph-time routing discriminator (pools remain separate at allocator level per D2). All three derive `Clone + Copy + Debug + PartialEq + Eq + Hash` — wgpu-types 29 already derives `Hash + Eq` on the underlying `TextureUsages` / `BufferUsages` / `TextureFormat` / `TextureDimension` / `TextureViewDimension`, so no hand-rolled wrapping needed. Helper `byte_size_estimate()` returns approximate bytes (via `wgpu::TextureFormat::block_copy_size(None)` + 4/3 mip-pyramid upper bound) for dispatch 120's D5 "max descriptor in group" comparison. **API extension (option-(a) descriptor-on-write)**: `FrameGraph::add_pass(name, reads: Vec<ResourceId>, writes: Vec<(ResourceId, ResourceClassDescriptor)>)` — writes carry descriptors; reads remain bare `ResourceId`. **Sidecar `FrameGraph::descriptors: BTreeMap<ResourceId, ResourceClassDescriptor>`** collects descriptors as `add_pass` observes writes; deliberately kept OFF `PassNode` to preserve content-derived `NodeId` stability under descriptor variation. **Descriptor consistency**: `add_pass` validates `descriptors.get(rid) == new_desc` before mutating the sidecar; conflict → new `FrameGraphError::DescriptorMismatch { resource, first_decl, conflicting }` (mid-vector conflict leaves no partial state — validation precedes any insert). **Compile-side**: `compile_passes(passes, descriptors)` clones the map verbatim into `CompiledFrameGraph::descriptors` (a new `#[serde(skip)]` field — wgpu types don't derive serde in the workspace's feature set; substrate-honest given dispatch 119 ships no compiled-graph serialization path). NEW accessors `CompiledFrameGraph::descriptors() -> &BTreeMap<…>` + `descriptor(id) -> Option<&ResourceClassDescriptor>`. **Descriptors are NOT factored into `structural_hash`** — analytical determinism remains orthogonal to descriptor metadata. **Optional `AliasingGroup::largest_descriptor` helper deferred** to dispatch 120 (lives next to the pool that consumes it). **`tests/frame_graph_smoke.rs` updated**: existing 3-pass `geometry / shadow / lighting` smoke now passes realistic descriptors (1920×1080 `Depth32Float` depth, 1920×1080 `Rgba8Unorm` color, 2048×2048 `R32Float` shadow map) + asserts the 4 descriptors round-trip through compile + recompile. > **Snapshot**: 2026-05-12 (Phase 6 frame-graph chapter — **ADR-118 transient-resource allocator policy pinned**, docs-only design dispatch): authors `docs/adr/ADR-118-frame-graph-transient-resource-allocator.md` (237L). D3 — pool key is `(Descriptor, AliasingGroupId)` (NOT descriptor-only, NOT descriptor+frame-index) so analytical `AliasingGroup` from `compile.rs` is the reuse contract; D4 — **ring-buffered N frames-in-flight, initial N=2** lifetime policy (NOT per-frame reset, NOT LRU, NOT explicit-release) directly realizes `GFX_RENDER_TIER.md:234`'s "allocator pressure stabilises"; D5 — greedy `AliasingGroup → physical mapping` using max descriptor size per group; D6 — **trust wgpu's auto-tracked hazard barriers** (NOT manual barrier emission); D7 — **dispatch 119 = `ResourceDescriptor` types + descriptor-flow through `add_pass` / `compile`** (smallest first; Independent of `rge_gfx::Camera` (which is GPU-only and not CPU-readable). **NDC convention LOAD-BEARING**: `view_proj` assumed wgpu/Vulkan/D3D (Z ∈ 0..1, 0=near 1=far), matching `glam::Mat4::perspective_rh()` (NOT `_gl` variants which use Z ∈ -1..+1). **Y-flip**: `screen_pos` in winit top-left convention; NDC Y flipped on the way in. **Algorithm**: screen → NDC, `view_proj.inverse()` with finiteness check (returns None on non-invertible / NaN-inf), unproject NDC near (Z=0) and far (Z=1) clip points, perspective-divide on `w` (returns None if either w is zero), build Ray with `direction = far - near` (NOT normalised — matches the picker's contract). **Layering — editor-shell is editor-tier (NOT renderer-tier)**: `forbidden-dep` rule 6 (RENDERER_CRATES → game-domain forbidden) does NOT apply, so editor-shell gains `rge-cad-projection` as a PRODUCTION dep (Tier-2 editor → Tier-2 game-domain via the picker module's Ray re-export). `glam = "0.30"` added as production dep matching gfx's existing version (no `bytemuck` feature — editor-shell never touches GPU buffers). 7 unit tests in `camera.rs::tests` + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs`. Test 3 (`camera_view_composes_into_face_selection_set`) demonstrates the full `CameraView → Ray → pick_face → FaceSelection → EditorCoord.face_selection` chain. The second piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter (active 2026-05-10) — turns "screen pixel + camera state → world ray" from a pen-and-paper formula into a callable, tested, headless primitive. **Does NOT bring up rendering**: no GPU, no winit event handler, no surface, no `gfx::Camera` modification, no `EditorShell::window_event` modification (mouse-event wiring is sub-δ). With sub-α + sub-β both in place, the chapter has the full **headless** chain: caller composes `view_proj` → `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` → `pick_face` → `FaceSelection`. Sub-γ onwards put it on screen. +10 net workspace tests = 7 unit + 3 integration; 2261 → **2271 tests**; 241 → 242 binaries (+1 for camera_picker_smoke.rs); editor-shell 75 → 85; cad-core unchanged at 471; cad-projection unchanged at 116; brep-render unchanged at 11. Implementation footprint unchanged at 44 IMPLEMENTED / 8 PARTIAL / 42 EMPTY-STUB (camera is a new module inside an already-IMPLEMENTED editor-shell crate). Continuation pointer for the next session. Prior: post brep-render-sub-α — `crates/brep-render/src/lib.rs` rewritten from 4-line stub to a CPU-side flat-shaded vertex-tripled mesh-conversion substrate. Public API: `RenderMesh { positions: Vec<[f32; 3]>, normals: Vec<[f32; 3]>, indices: Vec<u32>, face_labels: Option<Vec<u64>> }` + `RenderMesh::from_buffers(positions: &[[f32; 3]], indices: &[u32], face_labels: Option<&[u64]>) -> RenderMesh`. **Buffer-typed input — LOAD-BEARING deviation from spec**: `brep-render` is in the `forbidden-dep` lint's `RENDERER_CRATES` set, and PLAN.md §1.3 rule 6 forbids renderer crates from depending on game-domain crates (`rge-cad-core` is game-domain via `rge-cad-` prefix). The substrate consumes raw `&[[f32; 3]]` positions / `&[u32]` indices / opaque `&[u64]` per-triangle face-label slice instead of `rge_cad_core::Tessellation` directly. A caller in `cad-projection` (or similar Tier-2 bridge crate) that owns both `Tessellation` and a `RenderMesh` consumer composes the conversion in two lines. `TopologyFaceId(pub u64)` is wire-compatible — `face_id.0` is a lossless u64 round-trip. Cargo.toml gains zero production deps. Flat shading (vertex-tripled, 3× vertex count vs. input); each output triangle is independent and carries the triangle's face normal; degenerate triangles (`|cross| < 1e-6`) emit `[0, 0, 0]` normal rather than NaN. face_labels preserved 1:1 with input order (NO skip / reorder / filter — desync would break sub-ε selection-feedback). Output `indices` are dense `[0, 1, 2, ..., 3n-1]`. `//! Failure class: snapshot-recoverable` added to `brep-render/src/lib.rs`; the corresponding `failure-class` exemption for `crates/brep-render/Cargo.toml` REMOVED from `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` (rollout-debt count 31 → 30; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0). 8 unit tests in `lib.rs::tests` (empty / single-triangle / cuboid / PosZ-normal / face_labels-preserved-1:1 / unlabeled / degenerate-zero-not-NaN / dense-indices) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/brep-render/tests/render_mesh_smoke.rs` (cuboid 6-axis face-normal verification; extrude n=4 triangle-count match per D-projection-β contract `4n - 4 = 12`; revolve partial n=4 segments=8 face_labels count round-trip per D-projection-γ contract `2*n*segments + 2*(n-2) = 68`). ## What just shipped (this session — completed work)

0. **gfx PSO cache call-site routing follow-up to bc51cc0** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`, 2026-05-11). The PSO cache substrate landed in bc51cc0 with additive `*::new_cached(..., &mut PipelineCache<…>)` constructors, but existing `*::new(...)` call sites bypassed the cache (rationale at the time: avoid `GfxContext` interior-mut). This follow-up takes the **Approach 1 (Preferred)** path the original spec proposed: `GfxContext` now owns a `pso_cache: RefCell<PipelineCache<wgpu::RenderPipeline>>` field + `pso_cache()` / `pso_cache_mut()` accessors; `TrianglePipeline::new` / `MeshPipeline::new` / `LitMeshPipeline::new` are refactored to internally route through their `new_cached` companions against `ctx.pso_cache().borrow_mut()`. **All existing call sites stay byte-identical at the source level**; identical inputs now share `Arc<wgpu::RenderPipeline>` allocations transparently. `RefCell` (not `Mutex`) is justified by the empirically-verified single-threaded use of `GfxContext` across the workspace — no `spawn` / `Arc<GfxContext>` / explicit `Sync` requirement appears anywhere. `RefCell` preserves `Send` (the bound `PluginContext::take<GfxContext>` requires) since `wgpu::RenderPipeline: Send + Sync` and `Arc<T>` of `Send + Sync` is `Send + Sync`. **Workspace tests 2334 / 2334 byte-identical to bc51cc0** (this is a wiring change, not a feature; test count is unchanged by design). **No new public API beyond `pso_cache()` / `pso_cache_mut()` accessors** (forced by the chosen approach: pipeline constructors live in different modules and need to reach the interior-mut cache through a shared `&` borrow). **ZERO Cargo.toml diff** (verified `git diff --stat -- '*.toml'` empty). **material-runtime stays a 4-line stub; gfx-ir stays a 4-line stub** — both genuinely untouched. No snapshot/PIE integration (`recoverable` per `SCENE_EXTRACTION_CONTRACT.md` §5.4). No eviction. Files modified: `crates/gfx/src/context.rs` (+~50L: `RefCell` field + module-doc PSO-cache section + `use std::cell::RefCell` + `use crate::pso_cache::PipelineCache` + `pso_cache()` / `pso_cache_mut()` accessors); `crates/gfx/src/pipeline.rs` / `crates/gfx/src/mesh_pipeline.rs` / `crates/gfx/src/lit_mesh_pipeline.rs` (each: `new()` body rewritten 5L → 2L; doc-comment rewritten from "does NOT use a cache — every call builds a fresh pipeline" to "routes through the context-owned PipelineCache held inside GfxContext"); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md`. **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-gfx -p rge-editor-shell --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` exit 0; `cargo build -p rge-gfx -p rge-editor-shell -p rge-editor --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` 0 errors / 0 new warnings; `cargo test -p rge-gfx --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` PASS (121 unit + 14 integration); `cargo test --workspace --no-fail-fast --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` = **2334 / 2334 pass** byte-identical to bc51cc0; `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS). 1. **cad-projection sub-ζ — smoke integration test, CHAPTER CLOSE-OUT for the Render-backed face-selection chapter** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+3 net workspace tests** = 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_selection_smoke.rs` exercising the load-bearing chain `Ray → CadProjection::pick_face → CadProjection::face_triangle_indices` end-to-end at the cad-projection layer, in CI, with no editor-shell dep, no winit, no wgpu):
   - **The dispatch's job** is to lock the user-clicks-exercise chain into CI without touching production code. Sub-α through sub-ε already shipped the production primitives + wiring + visual feedback; sub-ζ adds CI coverage at the cad-projection seam so the chain cannot silently regress.
   - **Dep-cycle constraint observed (LOAD-BEARING design rule)**: `editor-shell` already depends on `cad-projection` in production (the picker's `Ray` type re-exported, `CadProjection::pick_face` consumed by `pick_face_at`). Cargo rejects a `cad-projection → editor-shell` dev-dep edge as a cycle. Consequence — `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` cannot be called from this smoke test. The canonical math is mirrored inline as a ~30-line `screen_to_world_ray` helper with a `// MIRROR OF editor-shell::camera::CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` comment + module-level doc-comment noting the canonical version is unit-tested in `editor-shell::camera::tests` (7 unit tests pin the math; this mirror is kept synced manually given its small surface — glam Mat4 inversion + NDC unprojection, ~15 lines of actual logic).
   - **3 tests delivered**:
     1. `cuboid_face_clicks_pick_and_yield_six_highlight_indices` — 3 screen positions `[400.0, 300.0]` / `[400.0, 250.0]` / `[450.0, 320.0]` under a perspective camera at `(4.0, 3.0, 4.0)` looking at the world origin (viewport 800×600, FOV 45°, aspect 4/3, near 0.1, far 100.0; `Mat4::look_at_rh` + `Mat4::perspective_rh` — wgpu/Vulkan/D3D NDC convention Z ∈ [0.0, 1.0]). For each click: `screen_to_world_ray` produces a `Ray`, `pick_face` returns a `FacePick`, `face_triangle_indices` returns exactly 6 dense vertex indices in the `[3i, 3i+1, 3i+2]` shape all within `[0, 36)` (the cuboid's 36-vertex flat-shaded buffer). After the three clicks, the picker has resolved at least 2 distinct `BRepFaceId`s — the unique-count guard `unique_count >= 2` prevents degenerate camera setups from silently masking chain failures.
     2. `empty_space_click_misses` — top-left corner pixel `[50.0, 50.0]` (well outside the cuboid's projected silhouette under the test camera) constructs a `Ray` then `pick_face` returns `None`. The miss path is part of the chain contract — the click handler must distinguish "hit no face" from "the pick is `None` for some other reason".
     3. `pick_then_highlight_indices_consistent_for_same_ray` — same `Ray` called twice on the same `(graph, projection, world)` snapshot returns byte-identical `face_id` + `entity` + `Vec<u32>` indices across calls. The substrate-honest "no hidden state" contract that downstream caching code can rely on; mirrors the `face_triangle_indices` doc-comment "Neither caches; each call runs the full enumeration".
   - **Cargo.toml: 1 new dev-dep edge**. `glam = "0.30"` added to `crates/cad-projection/Cargo.toml` `[dev-dependencies]` with a multi-line rationale comment (mirrors `editor-shell`'s production version pin). glam is utility/runtime (not in any `is_game_domain` / `is_renderer_crate` prefix in `forbidden-dep`), so this dev-edge does NOT trip rule 6; `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 with `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` byte-identical to pre-dispatch.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance): no edits to `cad-projection/src/lib.rs` / `picking.rs` / `render_adapter.rs` (production source untouched — sub-ζ is CI-only); no edits to `editor-shell/src/*` (the Option-2 "introduce editor-shell test seam" route was rejected explicitly in the dispatch spec); no edits to `gfx/src/*` or `brep-render/src/*`; no refactor lifting `screen_to_world_ray` out of editor-shell into cad-projection (out of scope); no new ADRs / new lints / new exemptions; no modification to `Ray` semantics / `face_triangle_indices` return shape / `RenderMesh` layout; no wgpu / winit / GPU dep; no new public API on `CadProjection`.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_selection_smoke.rs` (NEW, ~310L); `crates/cad-projection/Cargo.toml` (+1 dev-dep edge with multi-line rationale comment); `Status.md`, `change.md`, `HANDOFF.md`.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-cad-projection --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` exit 0; `cargo build --tests -p rge-cad-projection --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` exit 0; `cargo test --test face_selection_smoke -p rge-cad-projection --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` 3/3 pass; `cargo test -p rge-cad-projection --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` 131 tests pass (128 prior + 3 new); `cargo test --workspace --no-fail-fast --manifest-path A:\RCAD\RGE\Cargo.toml` = **2320 / 2320 pass** (was 2317; +3 net = the 3 new smoke tests; 0 failures; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement lints all PASS, snapshot-participate supplementary unchanged).
   - **Public API delta**: ZERO. No new `pub` items, no new types, no new methods — sub-ζ is pure CI coverage.
   - **Chapter status**: the Render-backed face-selection chapter (sub-α `brep-render::RenderMesh` → sub-β `editor-shell::CameraView` → sub-γ `render_mesh_for` → sub-δ.1.A gfx surface → sub-δ.1.B first-triangle-on-screen → sub-δ.2 click → sub-ε highlight overlay → sub-ζ smoke integration) is **CLOSED**. Post-chapter cohesion-debt cleared 2026-05-11 by the lifecycle.rs split into lifecycle / render_path / pick_path (item 0 above). Next focus pointer: **material-runtime PSO cache** (Phase 6.3) per user direction.

0. **editor-shell sub-δ.2 — mouse click → picker → coord.face_selection** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+4 net workspace tests** = 4 unit tests in `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs::tests` for the new `pick_face_at` free function (`pick_face_at_returns_face_selection_for_screen_center_on_cuboid` / `pick_face_at_returns_none_for_off_axis_screen_pos_far_from_cuboid` / `pick_face_at_returns_none_when_camera_view_unprojection_fails` / `pick_face_at_composes_into_face_selection_set`). The sixth piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter — **pure wiring**; no new substrate, no new deps, no new types beyond the `pick_face_at` free function and the `cursor_pos: Option<[f32; 2]>` field on `EditorShell`. Closes the click→select chain end-to-end: mouse click → CameraView → screen_to_world_ray → pick_face → FaceSelection → coord.face_selection. **Manual click verification** (running `cargo run -p rge-editor` on a workstation with a display, clicking on the visible Lambert+Phong-shaded cuboid, observing the `rge::editor-shell::pick` tracing log emit `picked entity=... face_id=...`) is the **load-bearing test** for this dispatch and is the **user's responsibility**; the agent did NOT run the binary because there's no display in CI.):
   - **Phase 1 — `pick_face_at` free function** in `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs`. Public API:
     ```rust
     #[must_use]
     pub fn pick_face_at(
         camera_view: &CameraView,
         screen_pos: [f32; 2],
         projection: &CadProjection,
         world: &World,
         graph: &OperatorGraph,
     ) -> Option<FaceSelection>;
     ```
     Composes `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` + `CadProjection::pick_face` + `FaceSelection { entity, owner, face_id }` construction in one call; returns `None` when either the unprojection or the picker returns `None`. Extracted as a free function (NOT an inherent method) so it's directly testable without constructing a full `EditorShell` (which requires a real winit `Window`); `EditorShell::handle_left_click` is the production-side caller. Re-exported at crate root: `pub use camera::{pick_face_at, CameraView, EditorCameraState}`.
   - **Phase 2 — `cursor_pos: Option<[f32; 2]>` field on `EditorShell`** in `crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs`. Initialised to `None` in both `EditorShell::new` and `EditorShell::with_world_projection_graph`. Tracks the most recent winit `WindowEvent::CursorMoved.position` in **physical pixels** (winit 0.30 convention; matches `SurfaceConfiguration.width / height` directly so no DPI conversion is needed).
   - **Phase 3 — `WindowEvent::CursorMoved` and `WindowEvent::MouseInput` arms** in `EditorShell::window_event`. The existing `_ => {}` catch-all is preserved for unhandled winit events. CursorMoved updates `cursor_pos`; MouseInput dispatches to `handle_left_click` when `state == ElementState::Pressed && button == MouseButton::Left`. Other buttons / Released events / scroll / drag / hover / right-click / middle-click / touch / stylus / keyboard are no-ops in v0.
   - **Phase 4 — `EditorShell::handle_left_click` private method** (~70L). Defensive guards no-op when `cursor_pos` / `surface_ctx` / `projection` / `cad_world` / `cad_graph` is `None`; then builds `editor_camera.to_camera_view([surface.config().width, surface.config().height])`, calls `pick_face_at(...)` with `cad_graph.graph()` as the `&OperatorGraph` argument, and routes the resulting `Option<FaceSelection>` into `coord.face_selection`. **v0 single-select clear-on-miss semantics** (matches Fusion 360 / Onshape / FreeCAD convention): a click clears the existing face_selection set unconditionally and adds the new selection iff the picker resolves a hit. Multi-select via shift / ctrl is a future dispatch. Tracing logs at `target: "rge::editor-shell::pick"`.
   - **`cad_graph: Option<CadGraph>` field's `#[allow(dead_code, reason = "held for sub-δ.2 picker; not consumed in sub-δ.1.B")]` removed** — sub-δ.2 actively reads `cad_graph.graph()` now.
   - **`// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:`-annotation added to `crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs`** (1085 lines, +85 over the 1000-line cap from sub-δ.1.B's render-path additions + sub-δ.2's click handler). Justification: cohesive `EditorShell` lifecycle file aggregating W03 PIE state machine + sub-δ.1.B render path + sub-δ.2 click handler + the `winit::ApplicationHandler` impl that dispatches between them; splitting now would interleave with pending sub-ε / sub-ζ dispatches and obscure the `EditorShell` mutable-self boundary (every method touches `&mut self` over a different field set; a helper-module split would require either pub-ifying internals or duplicating the `Option<…>`-guard scaffolding). Module extraction queued for a dedicated post-chapter refactor dispatch when the shape stabilises (after sub-ζ). Inline `// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation, NOT a `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` entry (substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0).
   - **No new deps**: editor-shell already had every dep it needed (`rge-cad-projection`, `rge-cad-core`, `rge-editor-state`, `rge-kernel-ecs`, `winit`); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 with byte-identical pass count vs. pre-dispatch.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance): no visual feedback / selection highlight (sub-ε); no multi-select (shift / ctrl / drag-select / box-select); no hover / mouseover / cursor-leave handling beyond what's required to track cursor_pos; no right-click / middle-click / scroll / touch / stylus / keyboard handling; no camera controls (orbit / pan / zoom / fly-cam); no rendering-path modification (existing `RedrawRequested` arm byte-identical); no new deps; no ADR / lint / doctrine doc / FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md modification; no PLAN / IMPLEMENTATION / fileandfolderstructure / versions edits; no `cargo +nightly fmt --all` reformat (used `-p rge-editor-shell` on one mid-dispatch break); no persistence of `coord.face_selection` to `WorldSnapshot` (selection state is editor coordination, never in WorldSnapshot per `lifecycle.rs:48` — that boundary has been load-bearing across the entire chapter).
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs` (added 6 new imports + `pick_face_at` free function + 4 unit tests in existing `mod tests`); `crates/editor-shell/src/lib.rs` (`pub use camera::{pick_face_at, CameraView, EditorCameraState};` re-export updated); `crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs` (`// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation + `cursor_pos: Option<[f32; 2]>` field + initialise in both constructors + `WindowEvent::CursorMoved` and `WindowEvent::MouseInput` arms in `window_event` match + `handle_left_click` helper method + dropped `#[allow(dead_code)]` on `cad_graph` field); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md`.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` exit 0; `cargo build -p rge-editor --release -j 2` exit 0; `cargo test -p rge-editor-shell --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (94 / 94 tests; was 90; +4 net = 4 unit); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2296 / 2296 pass** (was 2292; +4 net workspace; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch break on the `let selection = ...` call); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` byte-identical to pre-dispatch since no new deps; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 30).
   - **Public API delta** (`rge-editor-shell`): + `pub fn pick_face_at(...)` free function in `camera.rs` + `pub use camera::pick_face_at;` re-export at crate root. **No** new types; **no** new traits; the `cursor_pos` field is private; `handle_left_click` is private. The user-visible behaviour change is left-click in the editor window now updates `EditorShell.coord.face_selection`.

1. **editor-shell + rge-editor sub-δ.1.B — first triangle on screen** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+5 net workspace tests** = 5 unit tests in `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs::tests` for `EditorCameraState` (`editor_camera_state_default_eye_at_3_3_3` / `editor_camera_view_proj_identity_aspect_produces_finite_matrix` / `editor_camera_view_proj_aspect_change_affects_x_axis_only` / `editor_camera_to_camera_view_threads_viewport_size` / `editor_camera_view_proj_consistent_with_camera_view_screen_center`). The fifth piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter — pure integration/wiring; no new substrate beyond `EditorCameraState`. Composes the prior chapter primitives (`RenderMesh`, `CameraView`, `render_mesh_for`, `SurfaceContext`, `LitMesh::from_render_mesh`, `LitMeshPipeline`, `record_lit_mesh_pass`-style render path) into the visual moment "first triangle on screen". **Manual visual verification** (running `cargo run -p rge-editor` on a workstation with a display and inspecting that a single Lambert+Phong-shaded cuboid appears against a dark gray background) is the **load-bearing test** for this dispatch and is the **user's responsibility**; the agent did NOT run the binary because there's no display in CI.):
   - **Phase 1 — `EditorCameraState` (CPU editor-runtime camera intent)** in `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs`. Public API:
     ```rust
     #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
     pub struct EditorCameraState {
         pub eye: glam::Vec3,
         pub target: glam::Vec3,
         pub up: glam::Vec3,
         pub fov_y_radians: f32,
         pub near: f32,
         pub far: f32,
     }
     impl Default for EditorCameraState {
         fn default() -> Self;          // (3,3,3) → origin, +Y up, π/4, 0.1, 100.0
     }
     impl EditorCameraState {
         #[must_use] pub fn view_proj(&self, aspect: f32) -> glam::Mat4;
         #[must_use] pub fn to_camera_view(&self, viewport: [f32; 2]) -> CameraView;
     }
     ```
     **NDC convention LOAD-BEARING preserved**: uses `Mat4::look_at_rh` + `Mat4::perspective_rh` (wgpu / Vulkan / D3D Z ∈ `[0.0, 1.0]`), matching sub-β's `CameraView` contract — NOT the `_gl` variants which use Z ∈ `[-1.0, +1.0]`. Re-exported at crate root: `pub use camera::{CameraView, EditorCameraState};`.
   - **Phase 2 — 13 new fields on `EditorShell`** in `crates/editor-shell/src/lifecycle.rs` (all `Option<…>` except `editor_camera`):
     ```rust
     editor_camera: EditorCameraState,
     cad_world: Option<rge_kernel_ecs::World>,
     projection: Option<rge_cad_projection::CadProjection>,
     cad_graph: Option<rge_cad_core::CadGraph>,    // held for sub-δ.2 picker
     cad_entity: Option<rge_kernel_ecs::EntityId>,
     window: Option<Arc<winit::window::Window>>,
     gfx_ctx: Option<rge_gfx::GfxContext>,
     surface_ctx: Option<rge_gfx::SurfaceContext>,
     pipeline: Option<rge_gfx::LitMeshPipeline>,
     gfx_camera: Option<rge_gfx::Camera>,         // GPU UBO
     material: Option<rge_gfx::Material>,
     light: Option<rge_gfx::DirectionalLight>,
     cuboid_mesh: Option<rge_gfx::LitMesh>,
     ```
     All existing call sites of `EditorShell::new` / `EditorShell::with_world` see byte-identical lifecycle behaviour: with no `cad_world` attached, `init_render_state` bails fast and the existing W03 PIE plumbing (PlayState gating, WorldSnapshot capture/restore, AuditLedger, etc.) runs unchanged. **All previously-passing tests remain green** (90 / 90 in editor-shell; was 85 → +5 from EditorCameraState unit tests; rest of the editor-shell tests untouched).
   - **Phase 3 — NEW `EditorShell::with_world_projection_graph(cad_world, projection, cad_graph)` constructor** for `rge-editor`'s scene-load path. Captures the single `BRepHandle`-carrying entity by `world.query::<BRepHandle>().next()`; panics if zero or more-than-one match (sub-δ.1.B is single-cuboid only — multi-entity rendering is a later dispatch and the panic is the substrate-honest contract).
   - **Phase 4 — `init_render_state(&mut self, &ActiveEventLoop)`** helper. Composes (in order): `event_loop.create_window(WindowAttributes::default().with_title("RGE Editor").with_inner_size(LogicalSize::new(1024, 768)))` → `Arc::new(window)` → `GfxContext::new_headless()` → `SurfaceContext::new(&ctx, Arc::clone(&window))` (negotiates color format via `Surface::get_default_config(adapter, w.max(1), h.max(1))`) → `Camera::new(&ctx)` + `Camera::update(view_proj(initial_aspect), Mat4::IDENTITY)` → `Material::new(&ctx, &WHITE_1X1_RGBA, 1, 1)` (1×1 white texture; default phong factors `(0.1, 1.0, 0.5, 32.0)`) → `DirectionalLight::new(&ctx)` + `light.update(direction = (-1,-1,-1).normalize(), color = Vec3::ONE)` → `LitMeshPipeline::new(&ctx, camera_layout, light_layout, material_layout, surface_ctx.config().format)` (color format negotiated by surface — typically `Bgra8UnormSrgb` on Win32 / Vulkan / Metal) → `projection.render_mesh_for(entity, &cad_world)` → `LitMesh::from_render_mesh(&ctx, &render_mesh)` → `window.request_redraw()` to kick off the first frame. All errors map to `String` and are logged via `tracing::error!` in `resumed`; the existing W03 ready banner still emits afterwards.
   - **Phase 5 — `render_frame()`** helper (called from `WindowEvent::RedrawRequested`). Acquires the next surface texture via `wgpu::CurrentSurfaceTexture` enum match (wgpu 29 changed `get_current_texture` from `Result` to enum: `Success(SurfaceTexture)` / `Suboptimal(SurfaceTexture)` lift the texture; `Timeout` / `Occluded` / `Outdated` / `Lost` / `Validation` cause a `tracing::warn!` + `request_redraw` skip). Begins a single render pass with `LoadOp::Clear(wgpu::Color { r: 0.12, g: 0.12, b: 0.14, a: 1.0 })` (dark neutral gray; high enough contrast for shading variation), `depth_stencil_attachment: None` (**depth buffer AVOIDED** — see Phase 7 below). Sets `pipeline()` + binds `Camera` at `@group(0)` + `DirectionalLight` at `@group(1)` + `Material` at `@group(2)`, sets vertex/index buffers (the cuboid mesh is always indexed per `LitMesh::from_render_mesh` → `LitMesh::from_indexed`), `draw_indexed(0..36, 0, 0..1)`. Submits, presents, schedules next redraw.
   - **Phase 6 — `resize_render_path(new_w, new_h)`** helper (called from `WindowEvent::Resized`). Skips on `0×0` (mobile minimisation no-op); calls `surface_ctx.resize(&gfx_ctx, w, h)` to reconfigure; recomputes `view_proj` from the new aspect ratio and uploads to the camera UBO via `Camera::update`.
   - **Phase 7 — Depth buffer status: AVOIDED** (preferred). The existing `LitMeshPipeline::new` declares `depth_stencil: None`; sub-δ.1.B preserves that. For a single Lambert+Phong-shaded cuboid: back-face triangles compute Lambert dot ≤ 0 (the directional light from `(-1,-1,-1)` lights the +X / +Y / +Z faces; the −X / −Y / −Z faces fall to ambient-only ≈ `(0.1, 0.1, 0.1) × white` per the default phong factors), and the camera at `(3, 3, 3)` looking at origin has the front-facing triangles drawn over the back-facing ones in submission order. Visual verification will confirm the three visible faces show distinct shading variations from the directional light's three-axis component. No `gfx` modification was required — staying within the strict "no gfx modification" non-goal.
   - **Phase 8 — `editor/rge-editor/src/main.rs` full rewrite** (from 5-line stub to ~85L). Builds the cuboid scene from scratch using the same construction pattern as `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs` and `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs`: `CadGraph::new()` → `begin_operation()` → `add_operator(OperatorNode::Cuboid(CuboidOp { width: 1.0, height: 1.0, depth: 1.0 }))` → `set_root(...)` → `commit("rge-editor demo cuboid")` → `CadProjection::new()` → `World::new()` → `world.register_snapshot_component::<BRepHandle>()` → `projection.spawn_brep_entity(&mut world, cuboid_node)` → mutate `BRepHandle.brep_owner = Some(BRepOwnerId::from_bytes([0x42; 16]))` → `projection.tick(&mut world, &graph, Tolerance::new(0.001).expect("tol"))` → `EditorShell::with_world_projection_graph(world, projection, graph)` → `EventLoop::new().run_app(&mut shell)`. Uses `tracing_subscriber::fmt::try_init()` (best-effort; wrapped in `drop(...)` per clippy `let_underscore_drop`). `ExitCode::SUCCESS` on clean exit; `ExitCode::FAILURE` on `run_app` error.
   - **Layering verification (rule-6-checked)**: 4 new dep edges. `editor-shell → rge-gfx` + `editor-shell → rge-brep-render` + `editor-shell → wgpu` + `editor-shell → rge-cad-core` (the last promoted from dev-dep to production because `with_world_projection_graph` takes `CadGraph` by value); `rge-editor → rge-editor-shell + rge-cad-core + rge-cad-projection + rge-kernel-ecs + winit + tracing-subscriber`. **All pass `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)`** — editor-shell is editor-tier (NOT in `RENDERER_CRATES`), so rule 6 (RENDERER_CRATES → game-domain forbidden) does NOT fire; editor → renderer is permitted.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion): no `gfx` source modification (depth buffer was avoided → no `LitMeshPipeline` change required); no `brep-render` / `cad-core` / `cad-projection` / `editor-state` / `editor-ui` / `components-*` / `gfx-ir` / `material-runtime` source modification; no picker / `RenderMesh` / `LitMesh::from_render_mesh` / `SurfaceContext` / `CameraView` / `editor_state::FaceSelection` modification; no mouse event handling, click-to-select, picking integration, selection highlight, gizmos, viewport widgets (sub-δ.2 onwards); no camera controls (orbit / pan / zoom / fly-cam / keyboard); no multiple-object scene composition (single hardcoded cuboid only); no editor UI panels, dock, menus, egui integration; no animation, time-based update, frame timing logic beyond winit's redraw schedule; no asset loading, hot reload, file watching; no headless-mode toggle for rge-editor (always opens a window); no ADRs / lints / doctrine docs / `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` modification; no `PLAN.md` / `IMPLEMENTATION.md` / `fileandfolderstructure.md` / `versions.md` modification; no `HashMap<EntityId, LitMesh>` mesh cache or any multi-entity rendering scaffold (single `Option<LitMesh>` per chapter scope); no deps beyond the MAY-list (no nalgebra, no rayon, no tokio, no eyre/anyhow, no pollster — `GfxContext::new_headless` already wraps pollster internally).

   - **Phase 1 — `crates/gfx/src/surface.rs`** (NEW). Public API:
     ```rust
     pub struct SurfaceContext {
         surface: wgpu::Surface<'static>,
         config: wgpu::SurfaceConfiguration,
         _window: Arc<Window>,
     }
     impl SurfaceContext {
         pub fn new(ctx: &GfxContext, window: Arc<Window>) -> Result<Self, SurfaceError>;
         pub fn resize(&mut self, ctx: &GfxContext, width: u32, height: u32);
         pub fn surface(&self) -> &wgpu::Surface<'static>;
         pub fn config(&self) -> &wgpu::SurfaceConfiguration;
     }
     ```
     **Window-handle ownership LOAD-BEARING** for wgpu 29 / winit 0.30: `Surface<'static>` requires an owned-handle pattern; `Arc<Window>` is the canonical satisfier. The `_window: Arc<Window>` field's leading underscore signals it's held only to keep the underlying window handle alive for the surface's lifetime — the lifetime safety comes from the `Arc`, not from accessing the field.
   - **Phase 2 — `LitMesh::from_render_mesh`** (NEW inherent method on existing `LitMesh` in `lit_mesh_pipeline.rs`):
     ```rust
     pub fn from_render_mesh(
         ctx: &GfxContext,
         render_mesh: &rge_brep_render::RenderMesh,
     ) -> Result<Self, BufferError>;
     ```
     Vertex format mapping: `VertexLit { position, normal, uv: [0.0, 0.0] }` — UV is **placeholder** for sub-δ.1.A (the Lambert+Phong lit pipeline consumes UV only for optional texture sampling; the default material does not exercise it; real UV generation is a future dispatch). face_labels are NOT uploaded to GPU (CPU-side metadata for the future selection-highlight path).

0. **cad-projection sub-γ — `render_mesh_for` adapter (ProjectedMesh → RenderMesh)** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+8 net workspace tests** = 5 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/src/render_adapter.rs::tests` (`render_mesh_for_returns_none_when_entity_has_no_brep_handle` / `render_mesh_for_returns_none_when_entity_has_no_projected_mesh` / **`render_mesh_for_yields_some_when_no_brep_owner_set` LOAD-BEARING for the "doesn't gate on owner" contract** / `render_mesh_face_labels_some_for_labeled_cuboid_projection` / `render_mesh_face_labels_none_for_unlabeled_filleted_output`) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/render_adapter_smoke.rs` (**`render_mesh_face_labels_resolve_consistently_with_picker` LOAD-BEARING chain-consistency** verifying the renderer-side opaque u64 → resolver round-trip matches picker-side `brep_face_id_for_triangle` for all 12 cuboid triangles / `cuboid_render_mesh_triangle_count_matches_d_projection_alpha_contract` 36 positions/normals/indices / `extrude_square_render_mesh_triangle_count_matches_d_projection_beta_contract` n=4 36 positions/normals/indices). The third piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter — bridges sub-α's `RenderMesh::from_buffers` to sub-β's headless picker via the projection cache. Public API: `impl CadProjection { pub fn render_mesh_for(&self, entity: EntityId, world: &World) -> Option<RenderMesh> }`. With sub-α + sub-β + sub-γ all in place, the chapter has the **complete headless** chain: `world.query::<BRepHandle>()` + `render_mesh_for(entity)` produces RenderMesh per entity, AND `screen_to_world_ray + pick_face` produces FaceSelection — all referring to the SAME face-identity space (the chain-consistency test verifies this empirically). Sub-δ onwards put it on screen.):

   - **Phase 1 — `crates/cad-projection/src/render_adapter.rs`** (NEW, ~400L incl. 5 unit tests). Public API:
     ```rust
     impl CadProjection {
         #[must_use]
         pub fn render_mesh_for(
             &self,
             entity: EntityId,
             world: &World,
         ) -> Option<RenderMesh>;
     }
     ```
     **Two-gate semantics LOAD-BEARING**: returns `None` iff `entity` has no `BRepHandle` component (gate 1: CAD-entity scope) OR has no projected mesh in the cache (gate 2: geometry validity). **Does NOT gate on `BRepHandle.brep_owner`** — owner-presence is a *selection-identity* concern (used by the picker to scope `BRepFaceId` resolution), not a *geometry-rendering* concern; an entity with `BRepHandle` + projected mesh but `brep_owner == None` still produces `Some(RenderMesh)` (geometry renders; only its faces aren't pickable). The orthogonality between geometry-vs-selection is documented inline in the rustdoc and verified by unit test 3 (the LOAD-BEARING `render_mesh_for_yields_some_when_no_brep_owner_set` test). **Adapter mechanics**: `mesh.face_labels.as_ref().map(|v| v.iter().map(|t| t.0).collect())` flattens `Vec<TopologyFaceId>` → `Vec<u64>` (lossless via `TopologyFaceId.0`); `RenderMesh::from_buffers(&mesh.positions, &mesh.indices, face_labels.as_deref())` does the rest. No caching: each call re-runs `from_buffers`; cost is bounded by triangle count; future caching is a separate dispatch if profiling shows it's needed.

   - **Phase 2 — `crates/cad-projection/tests/render_adapter_smoke.rs`** (NEW, ~225L; 3 integration tests). Test 1 `render_mesh_face_labels_resolve_consistently_with_picker` is the **LOAD-BEARING chain-consistency proof**: build a 1×1×1 Cuboid entity, get the RenderMesh via `render_mesh_for`, get the resolver pair-list via `brep_face_ids_for_node` ONCE, then for each of 12 triangles assert two parallel paths converge to the same `BRepFaceId`: (a) `RenderMesh.face_labels[i]` (opaque u64) → `TopologyFaceId(label)` → resolver lookup; (b) `CadProjection::brep_face_id_for_triangle(entity, i, ...)`. Without this invariant, sub-α's opaque-buffer deviation (u64 instead of TopologyFaceId for renderer-tier consumption) could silently desync the two paths. Test 2 `cuboid_render_mesh_triangle_count_matches_d_projection_alpha_contract`: 1×1×1 Cuboid → RenderMesh with 36 positions / 36 normals / 36 indices / 12 face_labels (D-projection-α: 12 triangles × 3 vertex-tripling = 36); also asserts indices are dense `[0..36]`. Test 3 `extrude_square_render_mesh_triangle_count_matches_d_projection_beta_contract`: square Polygon2D n=4 ExtrudeOp → RenderMesh with 36 positions / 36 normals / 36 indices / 12 face_labels (D-projection-β: `4n - 4 = 12` triangles for n=4).

   - **Phase 3 — Cargo.toml + lib.rs**. `crates/cad-projection/Cargo.toml`: added `rge-brep-render = { path = "../brep-render" }` to `[dependencies]` as PRODUCTION dep (Tier-2 game-domain → Tier-2 renderer-tier; this is the OPPOSITE direction from rule 6's prohibition — rule 6 forbids renderer-tier → game-domain, NOT game-domain → renderer-tier). `crates/cad-projection/src/lib.rs`: added `pub mod render_adapter;` declaration alphabetically alongside existing module declarations (single-line addition; no new crate-root re-export needed since the method is added via `impl CadProjection { ... }` extension, not a new type).

   - **Layering decision (rule-6-checked, empirical)**. **Precondition step ran BEFORE writing impl**: added the `rge-brep-render` dep to `cad-projection/Cargo.toml`, ran `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all`, observed exit 0 with `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)`. Rule 6 only fires for `RENDERER_CRATES → game-domain` (the OPPOSITE direction); `cad-projection → brep-render` is permitted. The dispatch's stated decision matched the lint's actual behavior — no exemption needed, no doctrine modification, no ADR, no new thin adapter crate.

   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-projection --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**124 / 124** tests; was 116; +8 net = 5 unit + 3 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2279 / 2279 pass** (was 2271; +8 net workspace; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-cad-projection` apply on three trailing-format breaks); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the new cad-projection → brep-render production dep, confirming game-domain → renderer-tier is NOT rule 6 territory; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 30).

   - **Public API delta** (`rge-cad-projection`): + `CadProjection::render_mesh_for(&self, entity: EntityId, world: &World) -> Option<RenderMesh>` inherent method on existing `CadProjection` struct + `pub mod render_adapter;` module declaration. No new types; no new traits. Re-exports the `rge_brep_render::RenderMesh` type implicitly via the method signature; no explicit re-export added at crate root (callers either reach `RenderMesh` through `rge_brep_render` directly or through inferred return type).

   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: no caching / memoization (future dispatch territory); no multi-entity batch / iteration helper (caller composes via `world.query::<BRepHandle>().filter_map(...)`); no `winit` / `wgpu` / GPU upload / surface integration; no mouse / event / window / lifecycle wiring (sub-δ); no highlight / selection-feedback rendering (sub-ε); no `CameraView` / view math helpers (sub-β's domain); no ADR / lint / doctrine doc / `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` modification; no `PLAN.md` / `IMPLEMENTATION.md` / `fileandfolderstructure.md` / `versions.md` edits; no deps beyond `rge-brep-render` (no glam, serde, nalgebra additions); no modification of `ProjectedMesh` shape / `BRepHandle` shape / `CadProjection`'s existing methods (`projected_mesh`, `brep_face_id_for_triangle`, `face_resolves_in_projection`, `pick_face`, etc. byte-identical); no picker modification; no `gfx` / `editor-shell` / `editor-state` / `cad-core` / `gfx-ir` / `material-runtime` source modification; no `cargo +nightly fmt --all` reformat across unrelated files (used `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-cad-projection` once mid-dispatch); no `panic!` / `unimplemented!` / `todo!` in production paths (`Option<RenderMesh>` contract handles all None paths explicitly via the two gates).

   > **Render-backed face-selection chapter** (active 2026-05-10): sub-α brep-render mesh substrate (shipped); sub-β CPU camera/ray contract (shipped); **sub-γ cad-projection ↔ brep-render adapter (this dispatch)**; sub-δ window/event wiring (mouse click → headless picker → `EditorCoord.face_selection`); sub-ε visual feedback (selected-face highlight); sub-ζ smoke integration (cuboid rendered → clicked → selected → highlighted).
