0. **editor-shell sub-β — `CameraView` CPU-only screen→world ray contract** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+10 net workspace tests** = 7 unit tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs::tests` (`identity_view_proj_screen_center_yields_ray_through_origin` / `identity_view_proj_top_left_corner_ray_origin_at_top_left_ndc` / `viewport_y_flip_correctness` / `perspective_camera_origin_at_5_screen_center_ray_through_origin` / `direction_is_not_normalized_per_picker_ray_contract` / `degenerate_zero_view_proj_returns_none` / `near_plane_z_is_zero_per_wgpu_convention`) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs` (`camera_view_screen_center_picks_cuboid_top_face` / `camera_view_off_axis_screen_pos_misses_centered_cuboid` / `camera_view_composes_into_face_selection_set`). The second piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter — turns "screen pixel + camera state → world ray" from a pen-and-paper formula into a callable, tested, headless primitive that returns the existing `cad_projection::picking::Ray` shape directly. With sub-α (brep-render) + sub-β (this dispatch) both in place, the chapter has the full **headless** chain: caller composes `view_proj` → `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` → `CadProjection::pick_face` → `editor_state::FaceSelection` → `EditorCoord.face_selection`. Sub-γ onwards put it on screen.):

   - **Phase 1 — `crates/editor-shell/src/camera.rs`** (NEW, ~265L incl. 7 unit tests). Public API:
     ```rust
     #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
     pub struct CameraView {
         pub view_proj: glam::Mat4,
         pub viewport_size: [f32; 2],
     }
     impl CameraView {
         #[must_use]
         pub fn screen_to_world_ray(
             &self,
             screen_pos: [f32; 2],
         ) -> Option<rge_cad_projection::picking::Ray>;
     }
     ```
     Re-exported at crate root as `pub use camera::CameraView`. **NDC convention LOAD-BEARING**: `view_proj` assumed wgpu/Vulkan/D3D (Z ∈ 0..1 with 0=near and 1=far), matching `glam::Mat4::perspective_rh()` (NOT the `_gl` variants which use Z ∈ -1..+1). Documented in the module-level docstring; verified inline by test 7 (`near_plane_z_is_zero_per_wgpu_convention`). **Y-flip**: `screen_pos` in winit top-left convention; `ndc_y = 1.0 - 2.0 * (screen_y / viewport_height)` flips on the way in. Verified inline by test 3 (`viewport_y_flip_correctness`). **Algorithm**: (1) screen → NDC with the Y-flip; (2) `view_proj.inverse()` with finiteness check (returns None on non-invertible / NaN-inf entries — glam's `inverse()` returns NaN/inf for non-invertible inputs rather than `Option`); (3) construct NDC near (Z=0) + far (Z=1) clip points (wgpu convention); (4) unproject by multiplying by inverse view_proj; (5) perspective-divide on `w` (returns None if either w is exactly zero — degenerate unprojection); (6) build `Ray { origin = near, direction = far - near }`. The direction is NOT normalised per the picker's existing contract (`Ray.direction need NOT be unit-length; the reported t is in units of direction.length()`). **Substrate-honest `Option<Ray>` rationale**: editor-shell already operates on the "snapshot-recoverable" failure class — panicking on a degenerate camera would force the editor host to either crash or wrap every CameraView call in `catch_unwind`. `Option<Ray>` is the lighter contract; callers at editor runtime are expected to supply a sane camera (the editor never constructs `Mat4::ZERO` view_proj in practice); the `None` arm is a defensive contract for the truly-degenerate case.

   - **Phase 2 — `crates/editor-shell/tests/camera_picker_smoke.rs`** (NEW, ~210L; 3 integration tests). Test 1 `camera_view_screen_center_picks_cuboid_top_face`: synthetic camera at `(0, 0, 5)` looking at origin (45° FOV, 800×600 viewport, wgpu-convention `Mat4::perspective_rh` × `Mat4::look_at_rh`); screen center pixel → ray hits the unit cuboid's `+Z` face; asserts `pick.face_id == BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face(owner, CuboidFaceTag::PosZ)`. Test 2 `camera_view_off_axis_screen_pos_misses_centered_cuboid`: screen pixel `[50, 50]` (top-left corner-ish) → ray points off into the corner of the view frustum; for the small `[-0.5, 0.5]^3` cuboid this should miss; asserts `pick.is_none()`. Test 3 `camera_view_composes_into_face_selection_set`: full chain `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray → pick_face → FaceSelection → EditorCoord.face_selection`; demonstrates sub-β's place in the chapter end-to-end. The integration tests construct `CadGraph` / `CadProjection` / `World` / `BRepHandle` mirroring the pattern in `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs`.

   - **Phase 3 — Cargo.toml + lib.rs**. `crates/editor-shell/Cargo.toml`: added `rge-cad-projection = { path = "../cad-projection" }` as PRODUCTION dep (Tier-2 editor → Tier-2 game-domain; rule 6 of `forbidden-dep` only forbids RENDERER_CRATES → game-domain, and editor-shell is NOT a renderer crate); added `glam = "0.30"` as production dep matching gfx's existing version (no `bytemuck` feature — editor-shell never touches GPU buffers). `crates/editor-shell/src/lib.rs`: added `pub mod camera;` declaration alphabetically alongside existing module declarations + `pub use camera::CameraView;` re-export alphabetically alongside existing re-exports (single-line additions, no removals).

   - **Layering decision (rule-6-checked)**. `editor-shell` is editor-tier — NOT in the `forbidden-dep` lint's `RENDERER_CRATES = ["rge-gfx", "rge-gfx-ir", "rge-brep-render"]`. Therefore rule 6 (renderers cannot depend on game-domain crates) does NOT apply to the editor-shell → cad-projection edge. Empirical confirmation: `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 with `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)`. The dispatch's stated decision matched the lint's actual behavior — no exemption needed, no doctrine modification, no ADR.

   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-editor-shell --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**85 / 85** tests; was 75; +10 net = 7 unit + 3 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2271 / 2271 pass** (was 2261; +10 net workspace; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-editor-shell` apply on two trailing-format breaks); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the new editor-shell → cad-projection production dep, confirming editor-tier → game-domain is NOT rule 6 territory; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 30).

   - **Public API delta** (`rge-editor-shell`): + `CameraView` struct (2 public fields: `view_proj`, `viewport_size`) + `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` method + `pub mod camera` declaration + `pub use camera::CameraView` re-export. The crate-root re-export is also reachable via `rge_editor_shell::camera::CameraView` for callers that want to disambiguate.

   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: no `winit` event handling / `WindowEvent::CursorMoved` parsing (sub-δ); no `EditorShell::window_event` modification; no camera state tracking over time / orbit / pan / zoom / fly-cam (editor camera control is UI concern, not substrate); no view-math helpers (LookAt, perspective_rh, FOV constructors — caller composes); no `gfx::Camera` modification (renderer-tier; sub-β stays headless); no `nalgebra` / `cgmath` / other matrix library beyond glam; no UV coords / normals helpers / tessellation-related work; no `EditorCoord` struct shape change (no new fields); no edge picking / Fillet output identity / GPU readback / new doctrine / ADR; no PLAN / IMPLEMENTATION / fileandfolderstructure / versions edits; no `panic!` / `unimplemented!` / `todo!` in production paths (`Option<Ray>` contract handles degeneracy explicitly).

   > **Render-backed face-selection chapter** (active 2026-05-10): sub-α brep-render mesh substrate (shipped); **sub-β CPU camera/ray contract (this dispatch)**; sub-γ render snapshot/input bridge; sub-δ window/event wiring (mouse click → headless picker → `EditorCoord.face_selection`); sub-ε visual feedback (selected-face highlight); sub-ζ smoke integration (cuboid rendered → clicked → selected → highlighted). With sub-α + sub-β both in place, the chapter has the full **headless** chain: caller composes `view_proj` → `CameraView::screen_to_world_ray` → `pick_face` → `FaceSelection`. Sub-γ onwards put it on screen. Hard chapter non-goals: no edge picking, no Fillet output identity answer, no full material runtime, no broad editor redesign, no GPU readback picking, no new doctrine/ADR unless a sub-dispatch hits a real design fork.

0. **brep-render sub-α — CPU-side flat-shaded `RenderMesh::from_buffers` mesh-conversion substrate** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+11 net workspace tests** = 8 unit tests in `crates/brep-render/src/lib.rs::tests` (full rewrite from 4-line stub) + 3 integration tests in NEW `crates/brep-render/tests/render_mesh_smoke.rs`. The first piece of the Render-backed face-selection chapter — fills the rendering-tier EMPTY-STUB with a callable, tested, headless `buffer-triple → RenderMesh` primitive. Public API: `RenderMesh { positions, normals, indices, face_labels }` + `RenderMesh::from_buffers(positions: &[[f32; 3]], indices: &[u32], face_labels: Option<&[u64]>) -> RenderMesh`. **Buffer-typed input — LOAD-BEARING deviation from spec**: the dispatch's literal API spec called for `from_tessellation(tessellation: &Tessellation) -> Self` with `rge-cad-core` as a production dep. That dep would have tripped `forbidden-dep` rule 6 (renderer crates cannot depend on game-domain crates per PLAN.md §1.3; `rge-cad-core` is game-domain via `rge-cad-` prefix; the `rule6_renderer_to_cad_prefix_fails` self-test in `forbidden_dep.rs` actively asserts this). Empirical confirmation: adding `rge-cad-core` even as `[dev-dependencies]` trips rule 6 (the lint does not filter by `DependencyKind`). The dispatch's stated gate "no new substantive exemptions" + "no new doctrine/ADR unless real design fork" forced the resolution: keep the substrate goal (flat-shaded mesh conversion) but adapt the API to ingest opaque buffer triples instead of cad-core types. `TopologyFaceId(pub u64)` is wire-compatible — caller does `tess.face_labels.as_ref().map(|v| v.iter().map(|t| t.0).collect::<Vec<u64>>())` then passes the slice. Substrate intent (per PLAN.md §1.3 line 463 "Only cad-projection may import cad-core types into ECS code") is preserved: `cad-projection` (the bridge crate that already depends on `rge-cad-core`) is the natural home for the conversion call; brep-render itself stays renderer-tier-clean. Cargo.toml gains zero production deps. **Failure-class declaration `//! Failure class: snapshot-recoverable` added** to `brep-render/src/lib.rs`; the corresponding `failure-class` exemption REMOVED from `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` (rollout-debt count 31 → 30; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0). The chapter does NOT bring up rendering — no GPU, no window, no surface, no triangle on screen; sub-α produces the data shape the eventual gfx pass will upload. **Test fixtures duplicated inline** rather than imported from cad-core because of the same rule-6 constraint; canonical Cuboid 8-vert layout / Extrude 8-vert two-ring layout / Revolve partial structurally-correct layout all reproduce the D-projection-α/β/γ contract counts within brep-render's own crate.):

   - **Phase 1 — `crates/brep-render/src/lib.rs` (full rewrite from 4-line stub, ~330L incl. 8 unit tests)**. Public types:
     ```rust
     #[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq)]
     pub struct RenderMesh {
         pub positions: Vec<[f32; 3]>,
         pub normals: Vec<[f32; 3]>,
         pub indices: Vec<u32>,
         pub face_labels: Option<Vec<u64>>,
     }
     impl RenderMesh {
         pub fn from_buffers(
             positions: &[[f32; 3]],
             indices: &[u32],
             face_labels: Option<&[u64]>,
         ) -> Self;
     }
     ```
     Each input triangle becomes 3 independent output vertices carrying the triangle's face normal (flat shading). Triangle count = `indices.len() / 3`; vertex count = `3 * triangle_count`. Per-triangle normal: `(v1-v0) × (v2-v0)` then normalized; degenerate triangles (`|cross| < DEGENERATE_AREA_EPS = 1e-6`) produce `[0.0, 0.0, 0.0]` instead of NaN (matches `cad-projection::picking::EPSILON`). `face_labels = face_labels_in.map(<[u64]>::to_vec)` — preserved 1:1 in order; output's i-th face_label corresponds to the output's i-th triangle (which produced output vertices `[3i, 3i+1, 3i+2]`). Output `indices` are dense `[0, 1, 2, ..., 3n-1]`. Panics on `indices.len() % 3 != 0` or out-of-bounds index — both indicate a caller contract violation (caller is expected to pre-validate via `Tessellation::new` / `with_labels` invariants). Inline `[f32;3]` math helpers (`sub` / `cross` / `dot` / `length`) mirror `cad-projection::picking` style (no glam dep, no bytemuck dep, no wgpu dep, no winit dep). **`#![forbid(unsafe_code)]`** at lib root. **`//! Failure class: snapshot-recoverable`** declaration in module-level docs.

   - **Phase 2 — `crates/brep-render/tests/render_mesh_smoke.rs`** (NEW, ~315L; 3 integration tests). Test 1 `cuboid_render_mesh_face_normals_match_six_axis_directions`: synthetic 1×1×1 cuboid with `CuboidOp` face emission order (`NegZ → PosZ → NegY → PosY → NegX → PosX`; `TopologyFaceId(0..6)`); group RenderMesh triangles by `face_labels[i]`, assert all 2 triangles in each group share the expected axis-aligned outward normal. Test 2 `extrude_square_render_mesh_triangle_count_matches_d_projection_beta_contract`: synthetic Extrude n=4 square buffers (8 vertices, 12 = 4n-4 triangles, 12 face_labels in `Bottom → Top → Side(0..4)` order matching `impl BRepProvider for ExtrudeOp`); assert RenderMesh has 36 positions / 36 normals / 36 indices / 12 face_labels with dense `0..36` indices and 1:1 face_label preservation. Test 3 `revolve_partial_render_mesh_round_trips_face_labels_count_per_d_projection_gamma`: synthetic Revolve Partial n=4 segments=8 buffers (`(segments+1)*N = 36` ring positions, 68 = 2*n*segments + 2*(n-2) triangles in `Side(0)..Side(n-1) ring-major + StartCap fan + EndCap fan` order); assert RenderMesh has 204 positions / 204 normals / 204 indices / 68 face_labels with the canonical face_label distribution `[Side(i): 2*segments=16 each (4 sides), StartCap: n-2=2, EndCap: n-2=2]`.

   - **Phase 3 — Cargo.toml + lints**. `crates/brep-render/Cargo.toml` deps section UNCHANGED (no new prod deps; no new dev deps; the spec's planned `rge-cad-core` dep would have tripped rule 6 even at dev-dep level). `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml`: REMOVED the `crates/brep-render/Cargo.toml` `failure-class` exemption (was Phase-1.x rollout debt; now satisfied by the in-source declaration).

   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-brep-render --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**11 / 11** tests; was 0); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2261 / 2261 pass** (was 2250; +11 net = 8 unit + 3 integration; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch nightly-fmt diff fix on the inline 4-element array literal in `synthetic_revolve_partial_buffers`); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` because brep-render still has no production OR dev deps on game-domain crates; `[failure-class] PASS (0 violations)` with the new declaration; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count 31 → 30).

   - **Public API delta** (`rge-brep-render`): + `RenderMesh` struct (4 public fields) + `RenderMesh::from_buffers` constructor. Replaces the prior 4-line empty-stub crate.

   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed**: no GPU dep; no `gfx` / `gfx-ir` / `winit` dep; no glam / wgpu / bytemuck / serde dep; no UV coordinates / tangents / bitangents / vertex colors; no normal averaging / smoothing groups (flat shading only for v0); no material assignment / texture refs / shader integration; no `gfx-ir` types defined or modified; no `gfx-compatible` vertex layouts (output is plain `Vec<[f32; 3]>` triples — let downstream sub-dispatches do the gfx adaptation); no ADR / lint / doctrine doc / `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` / any `docs/architecture/*.md` modification (the spec authorized doctrine for "real design forks" — the rule-6 fork was resolved by API shape adaptation, not new doctrine); no PLAN / IMPLEMENTATION / fileandfolderstructure / versions edits; no `cargo +nightly fmt --all` reformat across unrelated files (used `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-brep-render` once mid-dispatch); no skip / filter / reorder of triangles silently — face_labels MUST stay 1:1 with output triangles in input order.

   > **Render-backed face-selection chapter** (active 2026-05-10): sub-α brep-render mesh substrate (this dispatch); sub-β CPU camera/ray contract; sub-γ render snapshot/input bridge; sub-δ window/event wiring; sub-ε visual feedback; sub-ζ smoke integration (cuboid rendered → clicked → selected → highlighted). Hard chapter non-goals: no edge picking, no Fillet output identity answer, no full material runtime, no broad editor redesign, no GPU readback picking, no new doctrine/ADR unless a sub-dispatch hits a real design fork.

0. **Headless face-picking sub-α — CPU-only `CadProjection::pick_face` callable primitive with closest-*resolvable*-face-hit selection rule** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+13 net workspace tests** = 6 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/src/picking.rs::tests` + 7 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs`. The first GFX-side selection-substrate consumer of the D-projection-α through γδ face-ID propagation; turns "user clicks pixel → BRepFaceId → FaceSelection" from a pen-and-paper algorithm into a callable, tested primitive without assuming the renderer. Inspection of GFX/editor picking surfaces showed `gfx::Camera` is GPU-only with no CPU-readable `view_proj`, `editor/rge-editor/src/main.rs` is a 5-line stub, `Viewport` is a text-overlay placeholder per its own doc-comment ("no rendering yet — Real wgpu rendering lives in W21+"), `brep-render` and `gfx-ir` are EMPTY-STUB, `EditorShell::window_event` line 401 swallows mouse events with `_ => {}`, and `ProjectedMesh` has zero consumers outside cad-projection's own tests. The honest "smallest face-picking path" is therefore a HEADLESS substrate primitive — Option A in the design pass — that composes into the future renderer/editor when the W21+ wave lands.):
   - **Phase 1 — `crates/cad-projection/src/picking.rs` module** (NEW, ~387L incl. 6 unit tests). Two new types:
     ```rust
     #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
     pub struct Ray {
         pub origin: [f32; 3],
         pub direction: [f32; 3],
     }

     #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
     pub struct FacePick {
         pub entity: EntityId,
         pub owner: BRepOwnerId,
         pub face_id: BRepFaceId,
         pub t: f32,
         pub triangle_index: usize,
     }
     ```
     Möller–Trumbore intersection in raw `[f32; 3]` math via private `sub` / `cross` / `dot` helpers — **no glam dep added** (preserves cad-projection production deps byte-identical). Two-sided intersection (no back-face culling) per picker semantics — "the picker should be able to select either side of a face" — explicitly verified by the `ray_back_face_hits` unit test. `EPSILON = 1e-6` for both the parallel-ray-determinant rejection and the `t <= EPSILON` (origin-side / behind hits) rejection.
   - **Phase 2 — `CadProjection::pick_face(&Ray, &World, &OperatorGraph) -> Option<FacePick>`** as inherent method on the existing `CadProjection`:
     - Iterates `world.query::<BRepHandle>()` returning `(EntityId, &BRepHandle)` pairs; skips entities where `handle.brep_owner.is_none()` (transparency-by-pre-filter — no resolvable identity space, no need to do geometry work).
     - For each candidate, fetches `self.projected_mesh(entity)` (existing public API, returns `Option<&Arc<ProjectedMesh>>`); skips entities without a cached mesh.
     - Walks `mesh.indices` in 3-element chunks, looking up `mesh.positions` for each vertex, calling private `ray_triangle_intersect`. Collects every positive-`t` hit as `(EntityId, triangle_index, t)` into a `Vec`.
     - **Sorts hits ascending by `t`** via `partial_cmp` + `unwrap_or(Equal)` (NaN/inf cases already rejected upstream — parallel-to-triangle and `t<=EPSILON` branches both return None from intersect).
     - Iterates the sorted hits in order, calling `self.brep_face_id_for_triangle(entity, tri_idx, world, graph)`. **The first hit that returns `Some(face_id)` wins.** Builds and returns `FacePick { entity, owner, face_id, t, triangle_index: tri_idx }`. The owner is re-read explicitly from the picked entity's `BRepHandle.brep_owner` (guaranteed `Some` since we filtered upstream AND the resolver short-circuits on `None`).
     - Returns `None` if no hit resolves (filleted / boolean / sweep output everywhere along the ray, or no candidates, or no triangles intersected).
   - **Phase 3 — `crates/cad-projection/src/lib.rs` widening**: `pub mod picking;` declaration added alphabetically alongside existing module declarations; `pub use picking::{FacePick, Ray};` re-export added alphabetically alongside existing crate-root re-exports. Single-line additions with NO removals; no other source file modified.
   - **Selection rule LOAD-BEARING (closest *resolvable* face hit, NOT closest geometric triangle)**. The distinction matters: a front Fillet / Boolean / Sweep surface emits unlabeled tessellation (or its source operator is classified `TopologyChangingOperator`), so its triangles do NOT produce a `BRepFaceId`. Such triangles are **transparent** to the picker — they do NOT mask resolvable faces behind them. Without this rule, a user clicking near a filleted edge could fail to select an underlying labeled face that is geometrically further along the ray, which would make picking feel broken. The `pick_punches_through_unresolvable_to_resolvable_behind` integration test is the load-bearing demonstration: a 4×4×4 Cuboid → Fillet entity at the origin (front in `t`-order, unresolvable identity) and a plain 1×1×1 Cuboid entity at the origin (top at `z=+0.5`, resolvable identity); ray from `z=+5` along `-Z` hits the fillet's geometry FIRST (around `t ≈ 3.0`), then the plain cuboid's `+Z` face at `t = 4.5`. The picker MUST return the plain cuboid's hit; the fillet's unresolvable hits are walked past in the resolve loop. Asserts `pick.entity == behind_entity`, `pick.owner == SECOND_OWNER`, `pick.face_id == BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face(SECOND_OWNER, CuboidFaceTag::PosZ)`, and `(pick.t - 4.5).abs() < 1e-4` (NOT the fillet's earlier t).
   - **Six unit tests in `picking::tests`** (Möller–Trumbore correctness against a canonical XY-plane unit triangle):
     1. `ray_hits_triangle_dead_center` — ray pointing -Z from `(1/3, 1/3, +5)` hits the centroid at `t=5.0`.
     2. `ray_misses_triangle_outside` — ray pointing -Z from `(2, 2, +5)` (well outside) misses.
     3. `ray_parallel_to_triangle_misses` — ray parallel to the XY plane bails on the determinant-near-zero check.
     4. `ray_behind_origin_misses` — ray origin at `z=-5` pointing -Z, triangle behind origin → `t<0` rejected.
     5. `ray_glancing_edge_hits` — ray pointing -Z at the v0–v1 edge sample → inclusive `0..=1` u/v bounds let it hit.
     6. `ray_back_face_hits` — ray pointing +Z from `(1/3, 1/3, -5)` → no back-face culling per picker semantics; must hit.
   - **Seven integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs`** (~484L):
     1. `pick_hits_cuboid_top_face` — synthetic ray pointing -Z from `z=+5` above a 1×1×1 cuboid at origin → returns `FacePick` with `face_id == BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face(owner, PosZ)`, `t == 4.5`.
     2. `pick_returns_nearest_when_two_cuboids_along_ray` — 2×2×2 cuboid (top `z=+1.0`, ENTITY_OWNER) + 1×1×1 cuboid (top `z=+0.5`, SECOND_OWNER), both at origin so the larger envelops the smaller. Ray from `z=+5` along -Z hits the larger cuboid's top FIRST (`t=4.0`); picker MUST return the larger entity's hit (verifies `pick.entity == larger_entity`, `pick.owner == ENTITY_OWNER`, `(pick.t - 4.0).abs() < 1e-4`).
     3. `pick_returns_none_when_owner_missing` — entity has `BRepHandle` with `brep_owner == None` (mutated post-spawn); even though geometry intersects, the picker filters such entities out at iteration time → `None`.
     4. `pick_returns_none_for_filleted_only_geometry` — Cuboid → Fillet chain bound to a single entity; no triangle resolves a `BRepFaceId` (FilletOp emits unlabeled Tessellation AND resolver classifies Fillet as TopologyChangingOperator); picker walks every hit, finds no resolution → `None`. Docstring explicitly references `docs/architecture/FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` (which **STAYS PARKED** — test demonstrates the gap, does NOT close it).
     5. **`pick_punches_through_unresolvable_to_resolvable_behind`** ← **LOAD-BEARING** for the closest-resolvable rule. See selection rule discussion above.
     6. `pick_returns_none_when_ray_misses_all_geometry` — ray origin at `(10, 0, 0)` along +Y → ray never crosses the cuboid which lives in `[-0.5, 0.5]^3` → `None`.
     7. **Bonus** `pick_composes_into_face_selection` — calls picker, manually constructs `FaceSelection { entity: pick.entity, owner: pick.owner, face_id: pick.face_id }` using the existing dev-dep `rge-editor-state`, demonstrates downstream composition (production caller in future `EditorShell::window_event` will do the identical field copy without any new API).
   - **Layering preserved (LOAD-BEARING)**: cad-projection production deps byte-identical to the post-sub-β snapshot — `rge-cad-core` + `rge-kernel-{ecs,graph-foundation,diagnostics,plugin-host}` + serde + postcard + ron + thiserror + tracing + ulid only. **No `rge-editor-state` production dep added** (sub-α's "neither crate depends on the other in production" precedent honored; the bonus test 7 uses the existing dev-dep). **No `glam` added** (Möller–Trumbore in raw `[f32;3]` math). **No Cargo.toml dep changes whatsoever.** `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the unchanged dep set.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion):
     - No edge picking (face-only; edge-level selection requires per-edge labels in tessellation that don't exist; deferred).
     - No acceleration structure (BVH, grid, etc.) — iterate-all-triangles is the v0 simplification, future-dispatch territory.
     - No GPU readback path (CPU-only Möller–Trumbore is the v0 simplification).
     - No `Camera::screen_to_world_ray` (cad-projection is a self-contained primitive; caller computes the ray from whatever camera they have).
     - No `EditorShell::window_event` integration; no viewport widget; no mouse-event handler; no Camera modification anywhere in the workspace.
     - No UI feedback / selection highlight (visual feedback blocked on rendering).
     - No answer to `docs/architecture/FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md`'s parked question (test 4 demonstrates the gap; design note STAYS PARKED).
     - No `editor-state` production dep added to `cad-projection`; no `glam` dep added; no Cargo.toml dep changes whatsoever.
     - No PLAN / IMPLEMENTATION / fileandfolderstructure / versions / ADR / lint / doctrine / §18 companion modification.
     - No prior cad-projection or editor-state test files modified (sub-α's `face_selection_partition_smoke.rs` byte-identical).
     - No `cad-core` source modified; no `editor-shell` / `editor-ui` / `gfx` / `brep-render` / `gfx-ir` source modified.
     - One mid-session `cargo +nightly fmt -p rge-cad-projection` apply on `face_picking_smoke.rs` (two trailing-format breaks the dispatch missed); no `--all` reformat of unrelated files.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: NEW `crates/cad-projection/src/picking.rs` (~387L incl. 6 unit tests); `crates/cad-projection/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod picking;` + `pub use picking::{FacePick, Ray};` added; no removals); NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_picking_smoke.rs` (~484L; 7 integration tests). `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md`.

0. **Editor selection persistence sub-β — `EditorCoord` `face_selection` field integration** (single-agent bounded dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+6 net workspace tests** = 6 integration tests in NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/editor_coord_face_selection.rs`. The smallest honest production-side proof that sub-α's substrate composes into actual editor coordination state, not just synthetic test scenarios. **This concludes the editor selection persistence chapter's sub-α/β arc**; the user's stated next step is "stop and reassess."):
   - **Phase 1 — `editor-shell::EditorCoord` gains `face_selection: FaceSelectionSet` as a third public field** alongside the existing entity-only `selection` and `active_tool`. The new struct definition (verbatim):
     ```rust
     #[derive(Debug, Default, Clone)]
     pub struct EditorCoord {
         pub selection: Selection,
         pub active_tool: ActiveTool,
         pub face_selection: FaceSelectionSet,
     }
     ```
     `FaceSelectionSet` already implements `Default + Clone + Debug`, so the `#[derive]` works without changes. `EditorCoord::new()` calls `Self::default()` which now sets `face_selection: FaceSelectionSet::default() == FaceSelectionSet::new()` — no impl-block change needed. `lifecycle.rs` is transparent to the field addition; the existing `coord: EditorCoord` holder pattern works unchanged.
   - **Phase 2 — direct public-field access matches the existing `coord.selection.add(entity)` precedent**. The full `FaceSelectionSet` API (add / remove / contains / clear / len / is_empty / iter / partition) is reachable directly via `coord.face_selection.X()` with NO new `EditorCoord` wrapper methods (no `set_face_selection` / `clear_face_selection` / `iter_face_selections` etc — the field is its own API).
   - **Phase 3 — `coord.rs` re-export widened** to add `FaceSelection` and `FaceSelectionSet`: `pub use rge_editor_state::{ActiveTool, FaceSelection, FaceSelectionSet, Selection};` (alphabetical sort preserved).
   - **Phase 4 — `editor-shell` Cargo.toml gains `rge-cad-core` ONLY as `[dev-dependencies]`** (test-only, not production) for constructing `FaceSelection { entity, owner, face_id }` instances in the integration test. Production deps unchanged. `[forbidden-dep]` lint PASS for the dev-dep.
   - **Test placement decision: integration test file** (NEW `crates/editor-shell/tests/editor_coord_face_selection.rs`, ~170L, 6 tests). Rationale: the cleanest path per the dispatch spec — avoids polluting editor-shell's production deps with `rge-cad-core` while still letting tests exercise the field. Inline `mod tests` in `coord.rs` was rejected because it would have required `rge-cad-core` in `[dependencies]` (production), which violates the spec's "no production dep changes" non-goal.
   - **Six integration tests**:
     1. `editor_coord_default_has_empty_face_selection` — `EditorCoord::new()` produces a coord whose `face_selection` is empty.
     2. `editor_coord_face_selection_can_be_added` — add a `FaceSelection`, verify `len() == 1` and `contains` returns true.
     3. `editor_coord_face_selection_clear_works` — add several, then clear, verify empty.
     4. `editor_coord_face_selection_independent_from_entity_selection` — proves the two fields are decoupled state, not coupled (clearing one does not affect the other; both directions tested).
     5. `editor_coord_face_selection_partition_via_field` — **THE LOAD-BEARING TEST**: populate `coord.face_selection` with three `FaceSelection`s, call `coord.face_selection.partition(|fs| fs.face_id == target)` directly through the public field, verify the partition returns the documented `(survivors, invalidated)` shape AND that `partition` is non-mutating (the source set is unchanged afterward). Smallest end-to-end proof that the partition function is reachable via `EditorCoord` without any wrapper.
     6. `editor_coord_face_selection_set_is_constructible_via_re_export` — sanity that `FaceSelectionSet` reaches callers via the `rge_editor_shell::coord` re-export path.
   - **Test imports** use the canonical `coord` module path: `use rge_editor_shell::coord::{EditorCoord, FaceSelection, FaceSelectionSet};` mirroring the existing `tests/snapshot_correctness.rs` precedent (`use rge_editor_shell::coord::ActiveTool;`). No crate-root re-export needed (and none added).
   - **`FaceSelection` construction helper** uses the public APIs: `BRepOwnerId::from_bytes([0xab; 16])` + `BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face(owner, CuboidFaceTag::NegZ)` (verified public via `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` re-export at `pub use topology::{... BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, BRepResolveError, CuboidFaceTag, ...}`). `EntityId::new()` is used for fresh entity-IDs.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion):
     - No new `EditorCoord` wrapper API (`set_face_selection` / `clear_face_selection` / `iter_face_selections` etc rejected; the field is its own API matching `coord.selection.add(entity)` precedent).

0. **Editor selection persistence sub-α — FaceSelection substrate + caller-driven partition + face_resolves_in_projection query** (single-agent bounded substrate dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+20 net workspace tests** = 12 unit tests in NEW `crates/editor-state/src/face_selection.rs::tests` + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_selection_partition_smoke.rs`. The first cad-projection consumer of B-Rep face identity beyond the lookup-per-triangle smoke; concrete substrate shape that lifts the D-7.2-α through D-projection-γδ integration into a user-facing selection-persistence handle. **This dispatch transitions the repo OUT of the post-D-projection-γδ rest-point snapshot into the editor selection persistence chapter.**):
   - **Phase 1 — `editor-state::FaceSelection { entity: EntityId, owner: BRepOwnerId, face_id: BRepFaceId }`**: explicit owner field (decision 2a per scope discussion); self-contained selection unit that survives `BRepHandle.brep_owner` mutations on the entity (decision is to avoid inferring the owner from the entity at resolution time). Manual Serialize/Deserialize bridging EntityId via the same EntityIdSerde pattern as existing `Selection` (selection.rs); the bridge is duplicated inline rather than centralised at this stage of substrate growth. Derive `Ord` so `BTreeSet<FaceSelection>` iterates deterministically (entity ULID first, then owner bytes, then face_id bytes).
   - **Phase 2 — `editor-state::FaceSelectionSet`**: BTreeSet-backed container with manual serde (round-trips via BTreeSet of FaceSelectionSerde where FaceSelectionSerde inlines the EntityIdSerde bridge). Inherent methods: `new()` / `add` / `remove` / `contains` / `clear` / `len` / `is_empty` / `iter` (no traits). The pivotal method is `FaceSelectionSet::partition<F: Fn(&FaceSelection) -> bool>(&self, predicate: F) -> (Self, Self)` returning `(survivors, invalidated)`. **Caller-driven partition (decision D1)**; nothing automatically pruned; the projection state is data, the selection set is data, the caller composes them at decision points. Names deliberately avoid `restore_*` / `sync_*` / `persist_*` (those would imply hidden lifecycle/persistence semantics this dispatch deliberately doesn't have).
   - **Phase 3 — editor-state Cargo.toml gains `rge-cad-core` dep** (for `BRepFaceId` + `BRepOwnerId` opaque ID type imports). `[forbidden-dep] PASS`: editor-state is Tier-2, cad-core is Tier-2; rule 3 only forbids cad-core from depending OUT on other Tier-2 crates, not inbound deps. `[editor-state-ownership] PASS`: lint forbids `cad_core` (without `rge_` prefix) but our import path is `rge_cad_core::...` so the leading-segment match doesn't fire; the editor-state ID-only-from-Tier-2 contract per PLAN §1.15 is satisfied because BRepFaceId + BRepOwnerId are opaque [u8; 16] ID types (not authoritative content — same role as EntityId in coordination state).
   - **Phase 4 — `cad-projection::CadProjection::face_resolves_in_projection(entity, owner, face_id, world, graph) -> bool`**: owner-aware resolvability query; iterates the entity's projected mesh triangles, calling `brep_face_id_for_triangle` for each, returns `true` as soon as a triangle's resolved BRepFaceId matches `face_id`. Returns `false` on owner-mismatch (handle.brep_owner != Some(owner)) — including the legacy None-owner case — so a caller-driven partition uniformly classes mismatched/orphaned selections as invalidated. Lazy and per-call; nothing cached. Cost bounded by triangle count.
   - **Layering preserved**: editor-state owns FaceSelection types + partition mechanic; cad-projection owns face_resolves_in_projection; neither crate depends on the other in production; caller composes via closure at decision points. cad-projection gains `rge-editor-state` ONLY as dev-dep (for the integration test); production cad-projection still only depends on cad-core + kernel.
   - **Four load-bearing integration tests**: (1) `face_selection_partition_all_resolve_for_intact_cuboid` — substrate baseline. (2) `face_selection_partition_survives_cuboid_parameter_rebuild` — capture all 6 cuboid faces at 1×1×1, rebuild as 2×1×1 via `begin_operation`/`add_operator`/`set_root`/`remap_entity`/`tick`, partition against rebuilt projection: ALL 6 land in survivors (the D-7.2-α owner-seeded contract lifted through cad-projection). (3) `face_selection_partition_invalidates_side_selections_on_profile_count_change` — capture all 6 square Extrude faces (Bottom + Top + 4 Sides), rebuild as pentagon Extrude on the same entity: 2 survivors (Bottom + Top — categorical caps per D-7.2-β) + 4 invalidated (square Side IDs disjoint from pentagon Side IDs since profile_count is in Side tag). (4) `face_selection_partition_invalidates_all_on_filleted_output` — **THE LOAD-BEARING PRESSURE TEST**: build Cuboid → Fillet, bind entity to fillet root, build FaceSelectionSet from upstream cuboid's 6 face IDs, partition: ALL 6 land in invalidated (FilletOp emits unlabeled Tessellation AND resolver classifies Fillet as TopologyChangingOperator). The test docstring explicitly references `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` so future maintainers understand when to update it. The parked design note's "trigger 1: cad-projection integration" is now actively exercised; the substrate is honest about the gap; the design note STAYS PARKED.
   - **Other 4 integration tests**: `face_selection_partition_invalidates_on_owner_mismatch` (set built under TEST_OWNER, BRepHandle.brep_owner mutated to OTHER_OWNER, all 6 invalidated); `face_selection_partition_returns_empty_for_empty_set` (degenerate input); `face_selection_partition_returns_empty_for_unknown_entity` (selections reference an entity not in the world; all land in invalidated); `face_selection_round_trip_through_ron_preserves_partition_outcome` (RON round-trip preserves partition outcome — serde correctness extends to partition correctness).
   - **The 12 editor-state unit tests** cover: `face_selection_round_trips_via_ron` (single FaceSelection); `face_selection_set_round_trips_via_ron` (multi); partition with always-true / always-false / split / count-preserving predicates; deterministic iteration order; `add_is_idempotent` / `remove_returns_presence` / `contains_reflects_membership` / `clear_empties_set` / `default_is_empty` set scaffolding.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion): no edge selections (sub-α is face-only; edge-level selection requires per-edge labels in tessellation that don't exist; deferred); no automatic pruning (partition is caller-driven via closure; no `FaceSelectionSet` self-prunes); no WorldSnapshot integration (FaceSelectionSet is editor-coordination state, persisted via existing RON serde patterns; PIE round-trip integration is a separate dispatch); no UI integration; no GFX picking; no Fillet output identity answer (`FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` STAYS PARKED — filleted output → all selections invalidate, exactly as the design note documents); no `Selection` (entity-only) modification; no `BRepHandle` modification; no `ProjectedMesh` modification; no new substrate types beyond `FaceSelection` + `FaceSelectionSet` (no `SelectionItem` enum, no `SelectionEvent`, no `SelectionDelta`); no new traits (`FaceSelectionSet::partition` is an inherent method, not generic over a trait); no `cad-projection → editor-state` dep, no `editor-state → cad-projection` dep (both depend on cad-core for ID types only; caller composes via closure); no `Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `Tessellation` / `topo_lineage` modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion / parked-design-note modification; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior B-Rep test files modified (face/edge identity smokes, chain resolution smokes, gate-closure stress test, fillet smokes, sub-α/β/γδ projection smokes all byte-identical); no reformatting unrelated files (one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply on the new test file).
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/editor-state/Cargo.toml` (rge-cad-core dep added); NEW `crates/editor-state/src/face_selection.rs` (~415L incl. 12 unit tests); `crates/editor-state/src/lib.rs` (`pub mod face_selection;` + `pub use face_selection::{FaceSelection, FaceSelectionSet}`); `crates/cad-projection/src/lib.rs` (`face_resolves_in_projection` method on CadProjection + `BRepOwnerId` import); `crates/cad-projection/Cargo.toml` (rge-editor-state dev-dep); NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/face_selection_partition_smoke.rs` (~370L; 8 integration tests); Status.md + change.md + HANDOFF.md.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-editor-state --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**37 / 37** tests; was 25; +12 net = 12 face_selection unit tests); `cargo test -p rge-cad-projection --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**103 / 103** tests; was 95; +8 net = 8 face_selection_partition_smoke integration tests); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**471 / 471** tests; unchanged — no cad-core source modified); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2231 / 2231 pass** (was 2211; +20 net workspace; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch fmt apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS — `[forbidden-dep] PASS (0 violations)` with the new editor-state→cad-core dep, `[editor-state-ownership] PASS (0 violations)` with the new `rge_cad_core::...` imports inside editor-state; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).

   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships editor selection persistence sub-α (face-only, caller-driven partition, no automatic pruning). It does NOT ship edge selections, automatic pruning, WorldSnapshot/PIE integration, UI integration, GFX picking, or output-side FilletOp identity (FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md STAYS PARKED — the parked design note's trigger 1 cad-projection integration is now ACTIVELY EXERCISED in test code, but the question stays parked since the substrate is honest about the gap).
   - **Phase 7 catalog: still 8 operators** — this dispatch operates entirely in editor-state + cad-projection; cad-core source unchanged. **Workspace state**: **2231 tests / 16 doctests / 9 enforcement + 1 supplementary lints PASS / fmt clean / 0 substantive lint exemptions / failure-class rollout-debt 31/81 (50 cleared)**. **Workspace state-line transition**: this dispatch transitions the repo OUT of the post-D-projection-γδ rest-point snapshot into the editor selection persistence chapter; the next pressure points are edge-level selections and PIE/WorldSnapshot integration when concrete consumer needs surface.

0. **D-projection-γδ — cad-projection face-ID integration sub-γ + sub-δ (Revolve mode-driven topology + Loft two-profile projection lookup; consumer matrix CLOSED across direct providers)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+20 net workspace tests** = 2 unit tests in `cad-core/operators/revolve/tests.rs` (`evaluate_full_emits_face_labels_with_correct_per_side_count`, `evaluate_partial_emits_face_labels_with_side_and_cap_labels`) + 2 unit tests in `cad-core/operators/loft.rs::tests` (`evaluate_emits_face_labels_in_canonical_order`, `evaluate_emits_face_labels_for_pentagon`) + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/revolve_brep_face_id_lookup_smoke.rs` + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/loft_brep_face_id_lookup_smoke.rs`. Sub-γδ closes the cad-projection face-ID consumer matrix across all four direct providers — after this lands, all four (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft) emit face_labels through projection. The escape hatch did NOT fire: Revolve's actual triangle emission order matches the spec sketch precisely (full_path: ring-major outer + edge-major inner; partial_path: side walls FIRST in identical ring-major order, THEN start cap fan, THEN end cap fan). Loft is structurally identical to Extrude's sub-β construction with two-profile provenance):
   - **Phase 1 — `RevolveOp::evaluate_full` + `evaluate_partial` emit face_labels**: switched final `Tessellation::new(...)` to `Tessellation::with_labels(positions, indices, face_labels)`. **Full mode**: per-triangle `Vec<TopologyFaceId>` length is `2*n*segments`, in ring-major order matching the existing emission loop — each (ring, edge_idx) cell emits 2 triangles tagged `TopologyFaceId(edge_idx)`; each Side(i) appears `2*segments` times, **interleaved across rings (NOT contiguous)**. **Partial mode**: side-wall triangles tagged identically to Full followed by `n - 2` start-cap fan triangles all tagged `TopologyFaceId(n)` and `n - 2` end-cap fan triangles tagged `TopologyFaceId(n + 1)` — matching `impl BRepProvider for RevolveOp`'s canonical Side(0..n-1) → StartCap (Partial only) → EndCap (Partial only) order. Both paths add `debug_assert_eq!(face_labels.len(), indices.len() / 3, "face_labels length must equal triangle count")` invariants. Override `Operator::output_is_labeled` to return `true` unconditionally (cache-key contract holds in both Full and Partial modes; arity 0 so input-derived branching is irrelevant).
   - **Phase 2 — `LoftOp::evaluate` emits face_labels**: switched to `Tessellation::with_labels` with `4n - 4`-entry per-triangle `Vec<TopologyFaceId>` matching `impl BRepProvider for LoftOp`'s canonical emission order (`n - 2` Bottom-cap triangles → `TopologyFaceId(0)`; `n - 2` Top-cap triangles → `TopologyFaceId(1)`; per side `i in 0..N` 2 triangles → `TopologyFaceId(2 + i)`) — structurally identical to Extrude's sub-β construction with two-profile provenance. Inline `debug_assert_eq!`. Override `Operator::output_is_labeled` to return `true`.
   - **Substrate-honesty caveat (CW-vs-CCW for LoftOp)**: `evaluate` reverses each profile's iteration when its `signed_area < 0` (CW input gets corrected to CCW); the `BRepProvider` impl indexes Sides by stored profile order. Sub-δ labels the side walls in evaluate's emission position which matches BRepProvider's canonical order ONLY when both profiles are CCW. All sub-δ coverage uses CCW profiles, so CW divergence does not surface in coverage. Caveat documented inline (matches sub-β extrude.rs precedent).
   - **Phase 3 + 4 — cad-projection NO change needed**: the API surface from sub-α/β is sufficient for both Revolve and Loft; lazy resolution through `topology::brep_face_ids_for_node` works for any operator that implements `BRepProvider` (RevolveOp implements `BRepProvider` from sub-7.2-γ; LoftOp implements `BRepProvider` from sub-7.2-δ).
   - **Three load-bearing Revolve tests**: (1) `revolve_face_ids_stable_across_angle_changes_within_partial_mode` — capture face IDs at angle=π/2, rebuild at angle=π via `begin_operation`/`add_operator`/`set_root`/`remap_entity`/`tick`, verify same triangle indices map to same `BRepFaceId`s (angle is NOT in `RevolveFaceTag::Side` per D-7.2-γ). (2) `revolve_face_ids_change_when_mode_changes` — Full and Partial Side IDs disjoint (`mode` is in Side tag's BLAKE3 input). (3) `revolve_face_ids_change_when_segment_count_changes` — `segments=8` and `segments=16` face IDs disjoint (`segment_count` is in Side tag).
   - **Load-bearing Loft tests**: `loft_face_ids_stable_across_length_changes` (length is topology-preserving); `loft_face_ids_stable_across_coordinate_changes_with_same_n` (substrate doesn't inspect coordinates per D-7.2-δ); `loft_face_ids_change_when_profile_count_changes` (sq×sq → pen×pen; categorical Bottom/Top match across, Side IDs disjoint).
   - **Other 5 Revolve integration tests**: `revolve_full_projection_query_returns_brep_face_id_for_each_triangle` (each of 64 triangles maps to one of 4 face IDs); `revolve_partial_projection_query_returns_face_ids_for_sides_and_caps` (each of 68 triangles maps to one of 6 face IDs); `revolve_query_returns_none_for_out_of_bounds_triangle`; `revolve_query_returns_none_when_brep_owner_is_none`; `distinct_owners_produce_disjoint_face_ids_through_revolve_projection` (uses pentagon_ring + Partial mode for 86-tri coverage).
   - **Other 5 Loft integration tests**: `loft_projection_query_returns_brep_face_id_for_each_triangle` (each of 12 triangles maps to one of 6 face IDs); `loft_projection_query_canonical_face_order_for_squares` (verifies canonical Bottom 0-1 → Top 2-3 → Side(0..3) 4-11); `loft_query_returns_none_for_out_of_bounds_triangle`; `loft_query_returns_none_when_brep_owner_is_none`; `distinct_owners_produce_disjoint_face_ids_through_loft_projection`.

0. **D-projection-β — cad-projection face-ID integration sub-β (Extrude variable-N projection lookup)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+11 net workspace tests** = 2 unit tests in `cad-core/operators/extrude.rs::tests` (`evaluate_emits_face_labels_in_canonical_order`, `evaluate_emits_face_labels_for_pentagon`) + 9 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/extrude_brep_face_id_lookup_smoke.rs`. Sub-α (D-projection-α) shipped face-ID propagation through projection for Cuboid (fixed topology); sub-β extends to Extrude — the smallest variable-topology follow-up — and proves the projection consumer pattern isn't a Cuboid special case. The API surface (`ProjectedMesh.face_labels`, `BRepHandle.brep_owner`, `CadProjection::brep_face_id_for_triangle`) is byte-identical to sub-α — substrate change is purely Extrude operator's emit, with lazy resolution via `topology::brep_face_ids_for_node`. **Variable-N projection consumer pattern proven** — sub-γδ Revolve + Loft compressible if no surprises. The parked `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` design note STAYS PARKED — this dispatch supplies more consumer-pressure (variable-N projection visible), NOT an answer):
   - **Phase 1 — `ExtrudeOp::evaluate` emits face_labels**: switched final `Tessellation::new(positions, indices)` to `Tessellation::with_labels(positions, indices, face_labels)`. Per-triangle `Vec<TopologyFaceId>` length is `4n - 4` matching evaluate's triangle count, in `impl BRepProvider for ExtrudeOp`'s canonical emission order: `n - 2` Bottom-cap triangles → `TopologyFaceId(0)`; `n - 2` Top-cap triangles → `TopologyFaceId(1)`; per side `i in 0..N` 2 triangles → `TopologyFaceId(2 + i)`. Override `Operator::output_is_labeled` to return `true` unconditionally so the cache-key contract (`output_is_labeled` MUST match `evaluate(...).is_labeled()`) holds.
   - **Phase 2 — `ProjectedMesh.face_labels` propagation**: NO change needed. `project()` already propagates upstream Tessellation labels through projection; the propagation is operator-agnostic (sub-α verified for Cuboid; same code path serves Extrude inputs).
   - **Phase 3 — `CadProjection::brep_face_id_for_triangle` reuse**: NO change needed. Lazy resolution through `topology::brep_face_ids_for_node` works for any operator that implements `BRepProvider`. ExtrudeOp already implements `BRepProvider` (sub-7.2-β); the projection consumer surface is byte-identical to sub-α.
   - **Substrate-honesty caveat (CW-vs-CCW)**: `evaluate` reverses profile iteration when `signed_area < 0` (CW input gets corrected to CCW); the BRepProvider impl indexes Sides by stored profile order. Sub-β labels the side walls in evaluate's emission position which matches BRepProvider's canonical order ONLY when the input profile is CCW. All sub-β coverage uses CCW profiles (sub-α D-projection's pattern), so the CW divergence does not surface in the test suite. Caveat documented inline alongside the face_labels construction; CW handling deferred — same posture as sub-β D-Fillet's `extrude_side_outward_normal` docstring caveat.
   - **Three load-bearing tests** in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/extrude_brep_face_id_lookup_smoke.rs`: (1) `extrude_face_ids_stable_across_length_changes` — capture face IDs at length=1, rebuild at length=2 via `begin_operation` / `add_operator` / `set_root` / `remap_entity` / `tick`, verify same triangle indices map to same `BRepFaceId`s (length is topology-preserving per D-7.2-β contract). (2) `extrude_face_ids_stable_across_profile_coordinate_changes` — same vertex count + same vertex order = same topology, coordinates change but BRepFaceIds are stable per D-7.2-β (the `Side` tag includes only `edge_index` and `profile_count`). (3) `extrude_face_ids_change_when_profile_count_changes` — `n=4 → n=5` topology change; per D-7.2-β Bottom/Top IDs are categorical (no `profile_count` in tag) and SHOULD match across the topology change, but EVERY square Side ID must be disjoint from every pentagon Side ID (`profile_count` is in the Side tag). The substrate-honesty test for sub-β.
   - **Other 6 integration tests**: `extrude_projection_query_returns_brep_face_id_for_each_triangle` (each of 12 triangles maps to one of 6 face IDs); `extrude_projection_query_canonical_face_order_for_square` (verifies canonical Bottom→Top→Side(0..3) emission order); `extrude_projection_query_canonical_face_order_for_pentagon` (verifies same for `n=5`: 3 Bottom + 3 Top + 5*2 = 16 triangles); `extrude_query_returns_none_for_out_of_bounds_triangle`; `extrude_query_returns_none_when_brep_owner_is_none`; `distinct_owners_produce_disjoint_face_ids_through_extrude_projection` (owner-seeded identity preserved through projection consumer surface for variable-N topology).
   - **Adapted tests** (mechanical, documented): `extrude_output_is_labeled_returns_false` → renamed `extrude_output_is_labeled_returns_true` since the new override matches new evaluate semantics. NO other prior cad-core test required adaptation — the mechanical adaptations expected per the dispatch spec did not surface (`labeled_tessellation_pipeline.rs` doesn't use Extrude as an unlabeled fixture; `effective_hash_distinguishes_labeled_vs_unlabeled_input_state` uses Cuboid only; `topo_lineage::infer::tests::label_by_plane_extrude_triangle_yields_5_face_groups` calls `label_by_plane` which discards existing labels per its docstring; `extrude_smoke.rs` / `extrude_face_identity_smoke.rs` / `extrude_edge_identity_smoke.rs` / `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` / `phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs` / `boolean_smoke.rs::boolean_with_extrude_input` don't assert on labels).

1. **D-projection-α — cad-projection face-ID integration sub-α (Cuboid-only, lazy resolution, face-only)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+15 net workspace tests** = 6 unit tests across cad-projection (`brep_handle_default_has_no_owner`, `brep_handle_with_brep_owner_sets_owner`, `brep_handle_serde_round_trip_with_owner`, `brep_handle_no_owner_round_trips_as_none`, `projected_mesh_face_labels_default_none`, `project_propagates_cuboid_face_labels`) + 1 unit test in cad-core (`evaluate_emits_face_labels_in_canonical_order`) + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-projection/tests/brep_face_id_lookup_smoke.rs`. D-projection-α is the first cad-projection consumer of B-Rep face identity — until this dispatch landed, BRepFaceId substrate was consumed only at the operator layer (FilletOp's input-side validation). After this lands, projection becomes a real downstream consumer, and the missing output-side identity for FilletOp becomes a concrete product gap. The parked `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` design note STAYS PARKED — this dispatch supplies the pressure, NOT the answer):
   - **Phase 1 — `CuboidOp::evaluate` emits face_labels**: switched from `Tessellation::new(positions, indices)` to `Tessellation::with_labels(positions, indices, face_labels)` with the 12-entry per-triangle `TopologyFaceId` vector matching `impl BRepProvider for CuboidOp`'s canonical NegZ → PosZ → NegY → PosY → NegX → PosX emission order (TopologyFaceId(0)..(5) ↔ 2 triangles each, computed via `(0..6u64).flat_map(|f| std::iter::repeat(TopologyFaceId(f)).take(2)).collect()`). Override `Operator::output_is_labeled` to return `true` unconditionally so the cache-key prediction-vs-reality contract holds.
   - **Phase 2 — `ProjectedMesh.face_labels`**: extended struct with `face_labels: Option<Vec<TopologyFaceId>>` (additive; `#[serde(default, skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]` for back-compat); `project()` copies `tessellation.face_labels.clone()` into the new field.
   - **Phase 3 — `BRepHandle.brep_owner`**: extended struct with `brep_owner: Option<BRepOwnerId>` (additive, `#[serde(default)]`); `BRepHandle::with_brep_owner(owner)` builder method; `BRepHandle::new()` defaults `brep_owner: None`. PIE snapshot round-trip preserved (4 unit tests covering default, builder, postcard with owner, postcard no-owner).
   - **Phase 4 — `CadProjection::brep_face_id_for_triangle(entity, triangle_idx, world, graph) -> Option<BRepFaceId>`**: lazy resolution at query time via `topology::brep_face_ids_for_node`; no `BRepFaceId` baked into `ProjectedMesh` storage; owner-seeded contract from D-7.2-α preserved. Returns `None` for any of: missing handle, missing brep_owner, missing projected mesh, missing face_labels, out-of-bounds triangle, resolver error (e.g. `TopologyChangingOperator` for Fillet/Boolean/Sweep).
   - **Two load-bearing tests**: (1) `cuboid_face_ids_stable_across_parameter_rebuilds` — capture face IDs at Cuboid(1,1,1), rebuild as Cuboid(2,1,1) via `begin_operation` / `add_operator` / `set_root`, `remap_entity` to the new node, re-tick, verify same triangle indices map to same `BRepFaceId`s; the consumer-pressure validation of D-7.2-α's owner-seeded rebuild-stability contract through cad-projection. (2) **`cuboid_through_fillet_returns_none_for_all_triangles_pressure_test`** — **THE LOAD-BEARING PRESSURE TEST** that makes `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md`'s gap concrete in code. Project Cuboid → Fillet, verify EVERY triangle returns `None` because (a) `FilletOp::evaluate` uses `Tessellation::new` (unlabeled output) AND (b) the resolver classifies Fillet as `TopologyChangingOperator`. The test docstring explicitly references `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` so future maintainers understand when to update it. Both gaps are visible in this single test.

(`rge-cad-core`) UNCHANGED public surface; `CuboidOp::evaluate` now emits labeled output (additive behavior change — labeled cuboid output is more informative than unlabeled, no consumer breakage; the labeled-output cache key for a Cuboid root differs from the previous unlabeled-output key, but the `effective_hash` cache is rebuild-coherent and consumers that hit the new key from scratch see correct behavior).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships D-projection-α (cad-projection face-ID integration sub-α). **It does NOT close any IMPLEMENTATION.md gate** — no spec gate references "cad-projection must answer per-triangle face-ID queries". **It does NOT answer the parked `FILLET_OUTPUT_IDENTITY.md` question** — that note stays parked; this dispatch supplies the consumer-pressure that makes the gap concrete. **It does NOT ship sub-β/γ/δ** (Extrude/Revolve/Loft face_labels emission). **It does NOT ship edge-ID queries through projection** (sub-β at earliest, when the substrate to label per-edge / per-segment in tessellation exists; per-triangle edge IDs don't have a clean substrate today). **It does NOT ship gfx / editor / picking integration** (the API surface is supplied; consumers come later).
