1. **D-Fillet sub-δ — Add Loft support to `FilletOp` (input-side consumer contract closed)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+19 net workspace tests = 10 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/loft.rs::tests` + 9 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_fillet_smoke.rs`**. Sub-δ closes the input-side consumer contract by adding the fourth direct-provider variant: `impl FilletUpstream for LoftOp` + `FilletOp::new_for_loft`. After this lands, FilletOp consumes `BRepEdgeId` from all four direct providers (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve cap-side + Loft); the input-side consumer contract is now proven across the provider set. The next architectural conversation — output-side identity for FilletOp (`impl BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider`) — begins after this lands; it is NOT the next dispatch):
   - **Geometry**: Loft has the same Bottom + Top + N Sides face structure and 3N clean 2-endpoint edges as Extrude (sub-β); the chamfer geometry adapts Extrude's face-normal-bisector approach to Loft's two-profile vertex layout (`profile_a` at bottom ring `positions[0..N]`, `profile_b` at top ring `positions[N..2N]` per `loft.rs::evaluate`). All 3N edges are chamferable in v0; no `UnsupportedEdgeGeometry` variant is ever returned for Loft inputs (mirrors Extrude). Bottom-perimeter edge `i`: bottom face normal `(0, 0, -1)` + `profile_a`'s side normal at edge `i`; inward bisector = `-(bottom + side) / 2`. Top-perimeter edge `i`: top face normal `(0, 0, 1)` + `profile_b`'s side normal at edge `i`; inward bisector = `-(top + side) / 2`. Vertical seam (`Side(i) ∩ Side((i+1)%N)`): average of four side-normal contributions across both profiles' adjacent edges; inward bisector = `-(sum_of_four_normals) / 4`. Magnitude convention: half-bisector (~0.707) matching sub-α/β. Defensive `n_a.min(n_b)` pattern mirrors sub-7.2-ζ.δ's `BRepEdgeProvider` impl on LoftOp (LoftOp::evaluate enforces equal counts but `profile_a` / `profile_b` are pub fields; min cap removes a panic surface for mid-mutation through pub fields).
   - **Profile pairing convention (load-bearing)**: v0 inherits LoftOp's `profile_a[i]` ↔ `profile_b[i]` pairing convention exactly. **No twist matching, no rotation alignment, no coordinate-aware vertex correspondence is introduced by sub-δ**. If LoftOp ever extends to support twist or vertex correspondence, sub-δ's chamfer geometry will need to be revisited; until then, the i-to-i convention is the substrate's contract. The dispatch's commit message and `loft.rs`'s module-doc both explicitly state this invariant.
   - **Consumer matrix closure**: Cuboid (sub-α): 12 of 12 edges chamferable (fixed topology). Extrude (sub-β): 3N of 3N edges chamferable (variable profile count). Revolve (sub-γ): 2N of 3N edges chamferable in Partial mode; 0 in Full mode (circular paths reject). Loft (sub-δ): 3N of 3N edges chamferable (two-profile, i-to-i pairing). The input-side consumer contract is now proven across the provider set.
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/loft.rs`** (~402L incl. 10 unit tests). Sole modification to `fillet/mod.rs` is the single-line `mod loft;` declaration alongside existing `mod cuboid;` / `mod extrude;` / `mod revolve;`. **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_fillet_smoke.rs`** (9 integration tests).
   - **Four load-bearing sub-δ tests**: (1) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_length_changes` — proves rebuild-stability across topology-preserving length changes (edge ID captured at length=1 valid against rebuilds at length=2 and length=0.5; FilletOp structural hashes byte-identical, since Fillet's hash captures only `(owner, edges, radius)`, not upstream Loft length). (2) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_coordinate_changes_with_same_n` — proves coordinate-only changes preserve edge IDs (substrate doesn't inspect coordinates per D-7.2-ζ.δ). (3) `fillet_loft_edge_ids_invalidated_by_profile_count_change` — proves topology-change rejection across profile-count changes; LoftOp enforces equal profile counts so changing topology means changing BOTH profiles together (sq×sq → pen×pen); `FilletOp::new_for_loft` rejects with `EdgeNotInUpstream`. (4) `fillet_loft_distinct_owners_produce_disjoint_specs` — mirrors sub-α/β/γ owner-disjointness pattern.
   - **The 10 unit tests in `fillet/loft.rs::tests`** cover: validation (`new_for_loft_rejects_zero_radius`, `new_for_loft_rejects_negative_radius`, `new_for_loft_rejects_non_finite_radius`, `new_for_loft_rejects_empty_edge_list`, `new_for_loft_rejects_unknown_edge_id`); accept paths (`new_for_loft_accepts_single_bottom_perimeter_edge`, `new_for_loft_accepts_all_3n_edges`); helper-table sanity (`loft_edge_vertex_pair_table_correctness` verifies for N=4: canonical_index 0 → (0, 1), 4 → (4, 5), 8 → (1, 5)); evaluation (`evaluate_one_loft_edge_adds_2_vertices_and_2_triangles`, `evaluate_three_loft_edges_linear_growth`).
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): no twist matching / rotation alignment / coordinate-aware vertex correspondence (v0 inherits LoftOp's i-to-i profile pairing exactly); no real round-fillet kernel; no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`; no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`; no fifth operator support (after sub-δ the consumer pattern closes); no multi-edge corner-blending; no new substrate types (no `LoftFilletStrategy`, no `EdgeKindSelector`); no `FilletUpstream` trait modification (trait stays exactly as sub-γ defined it); no new public API surface (`FilletOp::new_for_loft` follows the precedent of `new_for_extrude` / `new_for_revolve`); no `Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` / `Tessellation` / `topology` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / `kernel/*` modification; no `Cargo.toml` modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior `fillet/` file modification beyond `mod loft;` in `mod.rs` (`cuboid.rs` / `extrude.rs` / `revolve.rs` byte-identical; no changes to Cuboid/Extrude/Revolve behavior); no prior test files modified (`fillet_smoke.rs` / `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` / `revolve_fillet_smoke.rs` byte-identical); `lib.rs` re-exports unchanged (`FilletUpstream` stays `pub(crate)` — no new public surface).
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/mod.rs` (single-line addition: `mod loft;`); NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/loft.rs` (~402L); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_fillet_smoke.rs` (~286L; 9 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~111 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**7 / 7 sub-α byte-identical**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test extrude_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**8 / 8 sub-β byte-identical**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test revolve_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**9 / 9 sub-γ byte-identical**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test loft_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**9 / 9 sub-δ integration**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**464 / 464** tests; was 445; +19 net = 10 unit + 9 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2165 / 2165 pass** across 233 binaries (was 2146; +19 net = exact cad-core delta; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** — all five `fillet/` files comfortably under 1000L: `mod.rs` 544L / `cuboid.rs` 336L / `extrude.rs` 352L / `loft.rs` 402L / `revolve.rs` 376L; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: + `FilletOp::new_for_loft` constructor (one new public method on existing FilletOp). Existing public surface UNCHANGED. `FilletUpstream` trait stays `pub(crate)` (no new public surface). **`impl BRepProvider` / `impl BRepEdgeProvider` counts in cad-core: still exactly 4 + 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft for both faces and edges; FilletOp deliberately does NOT implement either trait in sub-δ).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships D-Fillet sub-δ (Loft variant). **It does NOT close any IMPLEMENTATION.md gate** — no spec gate references "FilletOp must support Loft". **It does NOT ship output-side identity** (no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`, no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`). **It does NOT ship real round-fillet geometry** (chamfer approximation only). **It does NOT ship multi-edge corner-blending**. **It does NOT ship support for circular-path edges** (Revolve Full + Partial side-side adjacencies still reject). **It DOES close the input-side consumer contract**: FilletOp consumes BRepEdgeId from all four direct providers (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve cap-side + Loft); the next architectural conversation — output-side identity — begins after this lands.
   - **Phase 7 catalog: still 8 operators** (no new operator added — this dispatch extends the existing Fillet operator). D-Fillet sub-α/β/γ/δ shipped: chamfer-approximation FilletOp consuming BRepEdgeId from all four direct providers; **input-side consumer contract closed**; output-side identity, real round-fillet geometry, multi-edge corner-blending, and Revolve circular-path edge support remain explicit non-goals for the next architectural conversation. **Workspace state**: **2165 tests / 16 doctests / 9 enforcement + 1 supplementary lints PASS / fmt clean / 0 substantive lint exemptions / failure-class rollout-debt 31/81 (50 cleared)**.

2. **D-Fillet sub-γ — Add Revolve support to `FilletOp` + extract internal `FilletUpstream` trait (mode-driven topology consumer of BRepEdgeId)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+20 net workspace tests = 11 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/revolve.rs::tests` + 9 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_fillet_smoke.rs`**. Sub-γ generalizes the FilletOp consumer pattern to mode-driven topology (Revolve Full ↔ Partial — the last categorically-new topology axis among the direct-provider operators) and consolidates the per-upstream resolution behind a `pub(crate) trait FilletUpstream: BRepEdgeProvider`):
   - **Phase 1, extract `FilletUpstream` internal trait + generic constructor**: `pub(crate) trait FilletUpstream: BRepEdgeProvider` with one method `resolve_chamfer_spec(&self, canonical_index: usize) -> Result<ChamferSpec, &'static str>`. New `FilletOp::from_upstream<U: FilletUpstream>(upstream, owner, edges, radius) -> Result<Self, FilletError>` performs the shared validation pipeline (radius finiteness + non-empty edge list + per-edge upstream-presence lookup + per-upstream chamfer-spec resolution wrapping `&'static str` failures into `FilletError::UnsupportedEdgeGeometry { edge, reason }`). Substrate-doctrine validation: 3-implementation rule earned the abstraction (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve); the trait is internal architectural consolidation, not a public extension point. Visibility intentionally `pub(crate)` so external consumer plug-in is a separate ADR-level decision when (if) it surfaces.
   - **Phase 2, refactor sub-α + sub-β to use the trait (behavior-preserving)**: `impl FilletUpstream for CuboidOp` moved sub-α resolution logic (CUBOID_EDGE_TAG_PAIRS lookup + cuboid_edge_corner_indices + cuboid_face_normal bisector); `impl FilletUpstream for ExtrudeOp` moved sub-β resolution logic (extrude_chamfer_spec wrapping extrude_edge_vertex_pair + extrude_chamfer_inward_direction). Each public constructor (`FilletOp::new`, `FilletOp::new_for_extrude`) becomes a thin one-line delegate to `Self::from_upstream(...)`. Cuboid + Extrude implementations always return `Ok(spec)` for any in-range canonical index — those upstreams have no circular-path edges. **Behavior preservation invariant verified**: all 7 sub-α `fillet_smoke.rs` integration tests + all 8 sub-β `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` integration tests + all sub-α/β unit tests pass byte-identically; no test modified, no test count change, no test name change.
   - **Phase 3, FilletError enum modifications**: `#[non_exhaustive]` added to `FilletError` so future variant additions are non-breaking. NEW variant `FilletError::UnsupportedEdgeGeometry { edge: BRepEdgeId, reason: &'static str }` for known edge IDs whose geometry FilletOp cannot chamfer in v0. Existing pattern matches via `matches!(... Err(FilletError::Variant { .. }))` continue to compile unchanged (`matches!` is non-exhaustive by default). `ChamferSpec` visibility tightened from `pub(super)` to `pub(crate)` so the trait's method signature is visibility-consistent with the trait itself.
   - **Phase 4, Revolve support — `impl FilletUpstream for RevolveOp` + NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/revolve.rs`** (~349L incl. 11 unit tests). Geometry support matrix (v0): Cuboid all 12 edges supported (sub-α). Extrude all 3N edges supported (sub-β). **Revolve Full**: 0 edges supported — every `Side(i) ∩ Side((i+1) % n)` adjacency is a swept circular path through `segments` vertices in the tessellation, not a clean 2-endpoint edge; reject all canonical edges with `UnsupportedEdgeGeometry { reason: "revolve full-mode side-side edges are circular paths; not chamferable in v0" }`. **Revolve Partial**: 2N of 3N supported — cap-side adjacencies (canonical `n..3n`) are clean 2-endpoint edges; side-side adjacencies (canonical `0..n`) are circular paths and reject with `UnsupportedEdgeGeometry { reason: "revolve partial side-side edges are circular paths; only cap-side edges chamferable in v0" }`. Construction-time rejection — a constructed FilletOp can never be in a state where evaluation fails on unsupported geometry. Substrate honesty: validation works for ALL valid Revolve edges (BRepEdgeProvider lookup is upstream-agnostic), but only cap-side edges in Partial mode produce chamfer geometry in v0.
   - **Cap-side vertex layout**: at ring 0 (start cap, theta=0) or ring `segments` (end cap, theta=angle), partial-mode tessellation vertex layout is `positions[ring*N + cap_local]` / `positions[ring*N + (cap_local+1)%N]`. The per-canonical-index resolution maps `local = canonical_index - n`, `is_end_cap = local >= n`, `cap_local = if is_end_cap { local - n } else { local }`, `ring = if is_end_cap { segments } else { 0 }`. Confirmed against `partial_path::evaluate_partial`'s `for ring in 0..=segments { for [x, y] in ordered { positions.push([x*cos_t, y, x*sin_t]) } }` layout.
   - **Inward direction algorithm for Revolve cap-side — centroid-based**: substrate-honesty choice. Compute edge midpoint at ring 0 / ring `segments` (3D coordinates `[x*cos(theta), y, x*sin(theta)]`). Target = origin Y-axis projection at midpoint's Y-coord (`[0, mid_y, 0]` — RevolveOp is rotationally symmetric around Y; the centroid lies on the Y-axis). Raw direction = target - midpoint, normalized to magnitude ~0.707 (sub-α convention) so structural delta (vertex/index counts) is consistent with Cuboid + Extrude chamfers. Defensive zero-vector return for edges on the rotation axis (mag < 1e-9).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_fillet_smoke.rs`** (~221L; 9 integration tests). **Three load-bearing sub-γ tests** (the substrate-validation core): (1) `fillet_revolve_cap_side_edge_remains_valid_across_partial_angle_changes` — proves rebuild-stability across angle-within-Partial (per D-7.2-ζ.γ angle is topology-preserving within mode; cap_edge captured at angle=π/2 valid against rebuilds at angle=π and angle=3π/2; FilletOp::edges() byte-identical across all three rebuilds). (2) `fillet_revolve_cap_side_edge_invalidated_by_segment_count_change` — proves topology-change rejection for segment-count axis (segment_count hashed into Side face tag's BLAKE3 input; cap_edge from segments=8 NOT in segments=16's edge list; FilletOp::new_for_revolve rejects with EdgeNotInUpstream). (3) `fillet_revolve_cap_side_edge_invalidated_by_mode_change` — proves topology-change rejection for Full ↔ Partial mode axis (mode hashed into Side face tag; Partial cap_edge NOT in Full mode's edge list — Full has no caps and the n side-side edges have mode=Full in the tag; FilletOp::new_for_revolve rejects with EdgeNotInUpstream). **Other 6 tests**: `fillet_validates_revolve_partial_cap_side_edge` (cap-side edge accepted), `fillet_rejects_revolve_full_mode_side_side_edge` (full mode rejects with UnsupportedEdgeGeometry), `fillet_rejects_revolve_partial_side_side_edge` (partial side-side rejects with UnsupportedEdgeGeometry), `fillet_revolve_through_operator_graph_evaluates_correctly` (end-to-end Revolve(Partial) → Fillet through CadGraph evaluates to upstream + 2 verts + 6 indices), `fillet_revolve_radius_validation_unchanged`, `fillet_revolve_rejects_unknown_edge_id`.
   - **The 11 unit tests in revolve.rs::tests** cover: validation (`new_for_revolve_rejects_zero_radius`, `new_for_revolve_rejects_negative_radius`, `new_for_revolve_rejects_non_finite_radius`, `new_for_revolve_rejects_empty_edge_list`, `new_for_revolve_rejects_unknown_edge_id`); per-edge support matrix (`new_for_revolve_full_mode_all_edges_unsupported` iterates all n full-mode edges; `new_for_revolve_partial_mode_side_side_unsupported` iterates canonical `0..n`; `new_for_revolve_partial_mode_cap_side_supported` iterates canonical `n..3n`; `new_for_revolve_partial_mode_mixed_selection_rejects_first_unsupported`); evaluation (`evaluate_partial_cap_side_edge_adds_2_vertices_and_2_triangles`); geometry smoke (`revolve_chamfer_spec_centroid_geometry_smoke` verifies inward direction magnitude ~0.707 and direction toward Y-axis from +X profile vertex).
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): no fourth operator constructor (Loft is sub-δ); no real round-fillet kernel; no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`; no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`; no support for circular-path edges in v0 (side-side adjacencies in Partial mode + all edges in Full mode return `UnsupportedEdgeGeometry` rather than fabricating geometry — substrate honesty over visual completeness); no public `FilletUpstream` trait (`pub(crate)` only — abstraction earned by 3+ implementations existing today, external plug-in is a separate ADR-level decision); no `Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` / `Tessellation` / `Polygon2D` / `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` / `BRepEdgeId` / `BRepFaceId` / `BRepResolveError` / `topology` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / `kernel/*` modification; no new substrate types (no `RevolveFilletStrategy`, no `EdgeKindSelector`, no `BlendKind`); no `Cargo.toml` modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no `PLAN`, `IMPLEMENTATION`, `fileandfolderstructure`, `versions` edits; no `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` modification; no prior test files modified (`fillet_smoke.rs` + `extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` byte-identical to sub-α/β; all prior B-Rep test files unchanged); no `lib.rs` re-export change (`FilletUpstream` stays `pub(crate)` — no new public surface); no `#[non_exhaustive]` on other types beyond `FilletError`; no reformatting unrelated files (one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply was used to format the new files); no `OperatorNode::Fillet` arm added to topology resolvers (existing `_` catch-all absorbs FilletOp correctly).
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/mod.rs` (refactored to add FilletUpstream trait + from_upstream generic helper + UnsupportedEdgeGeometry variant + #[non_exhaustive] on FilletError + ChamferSpec visibility moved to pub(crate)); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/cuboid.rs` (refactored to `impl FilletUpstream for CuboidOp` + `FilletOp::new` becomes thin delegate); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/extrude.rs` (refactored to `impl FilletUpstream for ExtrudeOp` + `FilletOp::new_for_extrude` becomes thin delegate); NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/revolve.rs` (~349L); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_fillet_smoke.rs` (~221L; 9 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~111 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**7 / 7 sub-α byte-identical**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test extrude_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**8 / 8 sub-β byte-identical**); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test revolve_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**9 / 9 sub-γ integration tests** including the 3 load-bearing rebuild-stability + topology-change-rejection tests); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**445 / 445** tests; was 425; +20 net = 11 unit + 9 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2146 / 2146 pass** across 238 binaries (was 2126 / 237; +20 net = exact cad-core delta; +1 binary delta for the new integration test file; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** — all four `fillet/` files comfortably under 1000L: `mod.rs` 498L / `cuboid.rs` 309L / `extrude.rs` 329L / `revolve.rs` 349L; total directory size 1485L; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: + `FilletOp::new_for_revolve` constructor + `FilletError::UnsupportedEdgeGeometry { edge, reason }` variant + `#[non_exhaustive]` on `FilletError`. `FilletUpstream` trait stays `pub(crate)` (no new public surface). Existing public surface (`FilletOp::new`, `FilletOp::new_for_extrude`, `FilletError::{InvalidRadius, EmptyEdgeSelection, EdgeNotInUpstream}`) UNCHANGED. **`impl BRepProvider` / `impl BRepEdgeProvider` counts in cad-core: still exactly 4 + 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft for both faces and edges; Transform deliberately remains non-provider; FilletOp deliberately does NOT implement either trait in sub-γ — output-side identity is sub-δ-or-later).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships D-Fillet sub-γ (Revolve variant + FilletUpstream trait extraction). **It does NOT close any IMPLEMENTATION.md gate** — no spec gate references "FilletOp must support Revolve". **It does NOT ship sub-δ Loft**. **It does NOT ship output-side identity** (no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`, no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`). **It does NOT ship real round-fillet geometry** (chamfer approximation only; cap-side approximation only for Revolve in v0). **It does NOT ship multi-edge corner-blending**. **It does NOT ship support for circular-path edges** — Full-mode + Partial-mode side-side adjacencies all reject at construction time. **The internal `FilletUpstream` trait extraction makes the future Loft constructor (sub-δ) additive**: `impl FilletUpstream for LoftOp` + thin `FilletOp::new_for_loft` delegate, no further FilletOp surgery needed.
   - **Phase 7 catalog: still 8 operators** (no new operator added — this dispatch extends the existing Fillet operator). Sub-α/β/γ shipped: chamfer-approximation FilletOp consuming BRepEdgeId from Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve (Partial cap-side only). Sub-δ Loft remains the last direct-provider variant before the chapter is structurally complete; output-side identity and real round-fillet geometry remain explicit non-goals for the next dispatches in the D-Fillet chapter. **Workspace state**: **2146 tests / 16 doctests / 9 enforcement + 1 supplementary lints PASS / fmt clean / 0 substantive lint exemptions / failure-class rollout-debt 31/81 (50 cleared)**.

3. **D-Fillet sub-β — Add Extrude support to `FilletOp` (variable-topology consumer of BRepEdgeId)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+18 net workspace tests = 10 unit tests appended in `fillet/extrude.rs::tests` + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_fillet_smoke.rs`**. Sub-β generalizes the FilletOp consumer pattern from fixed Cuboid topology (sub-α; 12 edges always) to variable Extrude topology (`3 * N` edges for `N`-vertex profile). The substrate question this dispatch answers — "does the FilletOp consumer pattern generalize beyond fixed-topology Cuboid?" — is now end-to-end test-validated YES across both rebuild-stability across topology-preserving (length) parameter changes AND topology-change rejection across profile-count changes):
   - **Phase 1, internal refactor of `FilletOp` (behavior-preserving)**: Replaces sub-α's `edge_tags: Vec<(CuboidFaceTag, CuboidFaceTag)>` field with a unified `chamfer_specs: Vec<ChamferSpec>` carrier where `ChamferSpec { vertex_a: u32, vertex_b: u32, inward_direction: [f32; 3] }` is computed at construction time (sub-α's chamfer-offset bisector that previously computed at evaluation now precomputes during `FilletOp::new`). The Cuboid constructor `FilletOp::new` now resolves edges to ChamferSpecs via lookup against `CUBOID_EDGE_TAG_PAIRS` + `cuboid_edge_corner_indices` + `cuboid_face_normal`. **Behavior preservation invariant verified**: all 7 sub-α integration tests in `fillet_smoke.rs` pass byte-identically with same test count and names as sub-α; all 11 sub-α unit tests pass byte-identically; no sub-α test had to be adapted (no test depended on the now-removed `edge_tags` field — it was never publicly accessible).
   - **Phase 2, additive Extrude constructor**: NEW `FilletOp::new_for_extrude(upstream: &ExtrudeOp, owner: BRepOwnerId, edges: Vec<BRepEdgeId>, radius: f32) -> Result<Self, FilletError>` mirrors `FilletOp::new` for Extrude upstream. Same `FilletError` variants (InvalidRadius, EmptyEdgeSelection, EdgeNotInUpstream — no new error variant added). Resolves each `BRepEdgeId` via `upstream.brep_edge_ids(owner)` (the `BRepEdgeProvider` impl on `ExtrudeOp` emits `3 * N` edges for `N`-vertex profile in canonical `[Bottom-perimeter | Top-perimeter | Vertical-seams]` order). Maps the canonical edge index back to a `(vertex_a, vertex_b)` pair in the upstream's `2N`-vertex layout via `extrude_edge_vertex_pair`. Computes the inward chamfer-offset direction from profile-edge geometry via `extrude_chamfer_inward_direction` (which uses `extrude_side_outward_normal` rotating profile-edge vector `(dx, dy)` by -90° to get `(dy, -dx)` for CCW-wound profile; bisector with adjacent face outward normals — Bottom = `(0, 0, -1)` for bottom-perimeter, Top = `(0, 0, 1)` for top-perimeter, both Side normals for vertical-seam).
   - **Edge → vertex-pair table (concrete, for N=4)**: `extrude_edge_vertex_pair` produces canonical_index 0 → (0, 1) bottom-perimeter, 1 → (1, 2), 2 → (2, 3), 3 → (3, 0); 4 → (4, 5) top-perimeter, 5 → (5, 6), 6 → (6, 7), 7 → (7, 4); 8 → (1, 5) vertical-seam (Side(0) ∩ Side(1) shares profile-vertex p1, so the vertical edge runs from `bottom_ring[1]` to `top_ring[1]`), 9 → (2, 6), 10 → (3, 7), 11 → (0, 4). Verified concretely in `extrude_edge_vertex_pair_table_correctness` unit test against `extrude.rs::evaluate`'s `positions[0..N] = bottom ring at z=0` + `positions[N..2N] = top ring at z=length` layout.
   - **Phase 3, file split**: After Phase 2, `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet.rs` reached 1042L exceeding the 1000L split-exemption threshold; split into a `fillet/` directory following the `topology/face_id/` precedent. **`fillet/mod.rs` (409L)**: shared types (`FilletError`, `ChamferSpec` with `pub(super)` field visibility, `FilletOp` struct with `pub(super)` field visibility, accessors, `Operator` trait impl with the upstream-agnostic `evaluate` logic) + 9 cross-cutting unit tests (Operator trait dispatch + structural-hash + arity rejection + label-stripping). **`fillet/cuboid.rs` (333L)**: `impl FilletOp { pub fn new ... }` + `CUBOID_EDGE_TAG_PAIRS` constant + `cuboid_edge_corner_indices` + `cuboid_face_normal` helpers + 11 sub-α unit tests (validation, accept-all-12, evaluate, helper-table correctness). **`fillet/extrude.rs` (364L)**: `impl FilletOp { pub fn new_for_extrude ... }` + `extrude_edge_vertex_pair` + `extrude_side_outward_normal` + `extrude_chamfer_inward_direction` + `extrude_chamfer_spec` helpers + 10 sub-β unit tests (validation, accept-all-3N, helper-table correctness, evaluate). All three files comfortably under 1000L; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions**. Total directory size 1106L. The split mirrors the `topology/face_id/` precedent exactly: shared types in `mod.rs`, per-operator constructors in submodules.
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_fillet_smoke.rs`** (8 integration tests). **Load-bearing tests**: (1) `fillet_extrude_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_length_changes` — proves rebuild-stability across topology-preserving length changes; an edge ID captured at length=1 is valid for `FilletOp::new_for_extrude` against rebuilds at length=2 AND length=0.5; FilletOp structural hashes byte-identical (Fillet's structural hash captures only operator-own parameters — owner + edges + radius — not upstream Extrude length). (2) `fillet_extrude_edge_ids_invalidated_by_profile_count_change` — proves topology-change rejection; the square's edge[0] BRepEdgeId is NOT in the pentagon's 15-edge set (the BRepEdgeId derivation hashes the Side face's `profile_count` field which is 4 vs 5, so the edge IDs are disjoint sets by construction); FilletOp::new_for_extrude rejects with `EdgeNotInUpstream`. The two are the substrate-validation core — they prove the consumer pattern generalizes to variable-topology input. **Other 6 tests**: `fillet_validates_extrude_edge_ids_against_upstream` (all 12 edges of square extrude accepted; 3·N=12 for N=4); `fillet_rejects_unknown_extrude_edge_id`; `fillet_extrude_rebuild_produces_same_structural_delta_across_lengths` (linearity check, +2 verts +6 indices regardless of length); `fillet_extrude_through_operator_graph_evaluates_correctly` (end-to-end Extrude → Fillet through `CadGraph` evaluates to 10 vertices + 14 triangles + 42 indices, structurally identical to the Cuboid → Fillet result); `fillet_extrude_zero_radius_rejected`; `fillet_extrude_all_edges_pentagon` (all 15 edges of pentagon extrude → +30 verts +90 indices linear growth confirmed).
   - **Substrate-honest contract — ExtrudeOp profile orientation**: `ExtrudeOp::evaluate` reverses profile vertices when `signed_area < 0` (CW input gets corrected to CCW for evaluation), but `BRepEdgeProvider for ExtrudeOp` indexes Side faces by `i in 0..N` directly using the original profile order (no reversal at the provider layer). The sub-β `extrude_side_outward_normal` helper reads `upstream.profile.points()` in stored order to match the provider's adjacency convention. Both test polygons (`unit_square` + `small_pentagon`) are wound CCW so `signed_area > 0` and the evaluate path uses the original order — this divergence does not surface in test coverage but is documented in the helper's docstring as a known substrate-honesty caveat. **No silent re-spec'ing**: the provider's profile-vertex-indexing convention (original order, not reversed) is the authoritative substrate; the consumer follows the substrate.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): no real round-fillet kernel; no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`; no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`; no third operator support (Revolve / Loft fillet variants are subsequent dispatches — sub-γ and sub-δ); no `FilletUpstream` trait abstraction (3-implementation rule — abstraction can emerge when sub-γ + sub-δ exist; today each upstream type gets its own concrete constructor); no `Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` modification; no `Tessellation` / `Polygon2D` / `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` / `BRepEdgeId` / `BRepFaceId` / `BRepResolveError` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / `kernel/*` modification; no new substrate types (no `FilletStrategy`, no `EdgeSelector`, no `BlendKind` enum); no corner-blending across multi-edge configurations (chamfer remains per-edge independent; if two filleted edges share a vertex the geometry may be visually weird but tests use non-adjacent edges); no prior test files modified (`fillet_smoke.rs` byte-identical to sub-α; all 9 prior B-Rep test files unchanged; all 4 prior face-identity smokes unchanged; `phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs` unchanged); no `Cargo.toml` modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no `PLAN`, `IMPLEMENTATION`, `fileandfolderstructure`, `versions` edits; no `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` modification.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: REPLACED `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet.rs` with `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet/` directory containing `mod.rs` (409L) + `cuboid.rs` (333L) + `extrude.rs` (364L); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_fillet_smoke.rs` (~218L; 8 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**7 / 7 sub-α integration tests, byte-identical to sub-α** — same test count, same names, all `ok`); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test extrude_fillet_smoke --no-fail-fast` PASS (**8 / 8 sub-β integration tests** including both load-bearing rebuild-stability and topology-change-rejection); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**425 / 425** tests; was 407; +18 net = 10 unit + 8 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2126 / 2126 pass** across 237 binaries (was 2108 / 236; +18 net = exact cad-core delta; +1 binary delta for the new integration test file; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for all three new files in `fillet/` directory; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: `+ FilletOp::new_for_extrude` constructor (one new public method on existing `FilletOp`). Existing public surface UNCHANGED — `FilletOp` and `FilletError` were already re-exported from sub-α; no new types, no new variants, no new traits. **`impl BRepProvider` / `impl BRepEdgeProvider` counts in cad-core: still exactly 4 + 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft for both faces and edges; Transform deliberately remains non-provider; FilletOp deliberately does NOT implement either trait in sub-β — output-side identity is sub-γ/δ or later).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships D-Fillet sub-β (Extrude variant). **It does NOT close any IMPLEMENTATION.md gate** — no spec gate references "FilletOp must support Extrude". **It does NOT ship sub-γ Revolve or sub-δ Loft**. **It does NOT ship output-side identity** (no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`, no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`). **It does NOT ship real round-fillet geometry** (chamfer approximation only). **It does NOT ship multi-edge corner-blending**. **The internal `ChamferSpec` refactor makes future direct-provider operators additive**: Revolve/Loft constructors will follow the `new_for_extrude` pattern verbatim — same FilletError variants, same canonical-edge-index → ChamferSpec resolution, no further FilletOp surgery needed.
   - **Phase 7 catalog: still 8 operators** (no new operator added — this dispatch extends the existing Fillet operator). Sub-α/β shipped: chamfer-approximation FilletOp consuming BRepEdgeId from Cuboid + Extrude. Sub-γ Revolve / sub-δ Loft variants and output-side identity remain explicit non-goals for the next dispatches in the D-Fillet chapter. **Workspace state**: **2126 tests / 16 doctests / 9 enforcement + 1 supplementary lints PASS / fmt clean / 0 substantive lint exemptions / failure-class rollout-debt 31/81 (50 cleared)**.

4. **D-Fillet sub-α — Cuboid-only chamfer-approximation `FilletOp` (first BRepEdgeId substrate consumer)** (single-agent bounded substrate-validation dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+28 net workspace tests = 21 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet.rs::tests` + 7 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/fillet_smoke.rs`**. The dispatch validates that the `BRepEdgeId` substrate (D-7.2-ζ chapter) holds up against an actual consumer — for the first time since sub-7.2-ζ.α landed, an operator construction depends on edge identity, validates against `BRepEdgeProvider`, and uses the resolved `(CuboidFaceTag, CuboidFaceTag)` pair to drive geometric output. The substrate's premise — edge IDs identify edges across parameter rebuilds — is now end-to-end test-validated by a real consumer):
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet.rs`** (482 lines incl. 20 unit tests). `FilletOp { edges: Vec<BRepEdgeId>, edge_tags: Vec<(CuboidFaceTag, CuboidFaceTag)>, radius: f32, owner: BRepOwnerId }` arity 1 — takes the upstream Cuboid's tessellation as input. Constructor `FilletOp::new(upstream: &CuboidOp, owner: BRepOwnerId, edges: Vec<BRepEdgeId>, radius: f32) -> Result<Self, FilletError>` validates: radius is finite and `> 0` (`FilletError::InvalidRadius`), edge selection is non-empty (`FilletError::EmptyEdgeSelection`), and every supplied `BRepEdgeId` is present in `upstream.brep_edge_ids(owner)` — unknown IDs return `FilletError::EdgeNotInUpstream`. Resolution maps each accepted ID's position in the canonical 12-edge order back to its `(CuboidFaceTag, CuboidFaceTag)` pair via the static `CUBOID_EDGE_TAG_PAIRS` table (parallel to the canonical adjacency table in `cuboid.rs::impl BRepEdgeProvider`).
   - **Geometry**: chamfer approximation, NOT a real round-fillet kernel. `evaluate` clones the upstream positions and indices, then for each filleted edge: looks up the 2 endpoint corner indices via `cuboid_edge_corner_indices(tag_a, tag_b)` (a 12-arm match parallel to `CUBOID_EDGE_TAG_PAIRS`, mapping each face-tag pair to the 2 corner indices in the cuboid's 8-corner layout `0:(-,-,-) 1:(+,-,-) 2:(+,+,-) 3:(-,+,-) 4:(-,-,+) 5:(+,-,+) 6:(+,+,+) 7:(-,+,+)`); offsets each endpoint inward along the bisector of the two adjacent face normals by `radius`; appends 2 new vertices and 2 new chamfer-cap triangles. Per filleted edge: +2 vertices, +2 triangles. Linear in selection count. **Real round-fillet geometry (quarter-cylinder tessellation, face-strip removal, multi-edge corner blending, curvature continuity) is OUT OF SCOPE for sub-α**.
   - **Substrate posture**: FilletOp deliberately does NOT implement `BRepProvider` or `BRepEdgeProvider`. Output-side identity is sub-β at earliest. FilletOp falls into the `_` catch-all in `topology::resolve::resolve_step` and `topology::edge_resolve::resolve_step`, returning `BRepResolveError::TopologyChangingOperator { kind: OpKind::Fillet }` as expected — verified by integration test `fillet_node_returns_topology_changing_from_both_resolvers`. This is correct: FilletOp changes topology (adds vertices/triangles) and does not provide its own face/edge identity in sub-α.
   - **Wiring**: `OpKind::Fillet` variant added to `crates/cad-core/src/operators/mod.rs::OpKind` enum (alphabetical, between Extrude and Loft); `OperatorNode::Fillet(FilletOp)` variant added to `OperatorNode` enum (alphabetical, between Extrude and Loft); `as_operator()` arm extended; `pub mod fillet;` + `pub use fillet::{FilletError, FilletOp};` re-exports added; `op_kind_non_exhaustive_pattern_match_compiles` test extended with the `Fillet` arm. `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` re-export list extended (`FilletError, FilletOp` added alphabetically). The `op_kind_non_exhaustive_pattern_match_compiles` simulation-test now covers all 8 operator kinds plus the wildcard. Both `topology::resolve` and `topology::edge_resolve` byte-identical (no `OperatorNode::Fillet` arm added — the existing `_` catch-all absorbs the new variant correctly).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/fillet_smoke.rs`** (~7 integration tests). `fillet_validates_edge_ids_against_upstream_cuboid` (all 12 edges accepted); `fillet_rejects_unknown_edge_id` (synthetic `BRepEdgeId::from_bytes([0u8; 16])` rejected with `EdgeNotInUpstream`); **load-bearing `fillet_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_cuboid_parameter_rebuilds`** (capture an edge ID against unit cube, verify it is in the rebuilt 2×2×2 cube's edge list, construct `FilletOp` against both — proves the substrate carries weight as a real consumer; structural hashes byte-identical because they don't include upstream Cuboid dimensions); `fillet_rebuild_produces_same_structural_delta_across_sizes` (linearity check: same logical edge → same +2 verts +6 indices delta on both unit and double cube); `fillet_through_operator_graph_evaluates_correctly` (end-to-end Cuboid → Fillet through `CadGraph` evaluates to 10 vertices + 14 triangles + 42 indices); `fillet_zero_radius_rejected` (`InvalidRadius`); `fillet_node_returns_topology_changing_from_both_resolvers` (substrate-honest: both face and edge resolvers return `TopologyChangingOperator { kind: OpKind::Fillet }` for a Fillet node).
   - **The 20 unit tests in `fillet.rs::tests`**: validation (`new_rejects_zero_radius`, `new_rejects_negative_radius`, `new_rejects_non_finite_radius` covering NAN+INFINITY, `new_rejects_empty_edge_list`, `new_rejects_unknown_edge_id`, `new_accepts_valid_single_edge`, `new_accepts_all_12_edges`); operator-trait dispatch (`op_kind_is_fillet`, `arity_is_one`); structural-hash differentiation (`structural_hash_changes_with_radius`, `structural_hash_changes_with_edge_selection`, `structural_hash_includes_owner`, `structural_hash_is_deterministic`); evaluation (`evaluate_rejects_wrong_arity_zero_inputs`, `evaluate_rejects_wrong_arity_two_inputs`, `evaluate_one_edge_adds_2_vertices_and_2_triangles`, `evaluate_three_edges_adds_6_vertices_and_6_triangles`); helper-table sanity (`cuboid_edge_corner_indices_arg_order_independent` proves `f(a, b) == f(b, a)` for all 12 pairs, `cuboid_edge_corner_indices_all_pairs_in_bounds` proves all 12 pairs return distinct corner indices in [0, 8)); label-stripping (`output_is_labeled_strips` overrides default `iter().any` propagation to match `evaluate`'s actual label-stripping behavior, mirroring `TransformOp`'s precedent). Plus 1 dispatch test in `operators/mod.rs::tests::operator_node_dispatches_fillet`.
   - **Honest framing — what this dispatch is and isn't**: this dispatch ships D-Fillet sub-α. **It does NOT ship a generalized fillet kernel** — chamfer approximation only. **It does NOT ship multi-operator support** — Cuboid only; Extrude / Revolve / Loft fillet variants are subsequent sub-dispatches. **It does NOT ship output-side identity** — no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`, no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`. **It does NOT ship Boolean / Sweep composition**. **It does NOT ship `cad-projection` or `gfx` integration**. **It does NOT ship multi-edge corner-sharing geometry validation** — if two filleted edges share a Cuboid corner, the chamfer geometry may be visually weird; the substrate-validation tests do not exercise that case (use non-adjacent edges in tests). **The load-bearing `fillet_edge_ids_remain_valid_across_cuboid_parameter_rebuilds` is the central success criterion**: an edge ID minted against a unit cube is accepted by `FilletOp::new` against a 2×2×2 cube — the BRepEdgeId substrate has earned its weight against actual consumer pressure.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): no real round-fillet kernel; no `impl BRepProvider for FilletOp`; no `impl BRepEdgeProvider for FilletOp`; no `BRepEdgeId` / `BRepFaceId` / `BRepResolveError` / `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` modification (substrate from sub-7.2-α through ζ.ζ byte-identical); no `topology/face_id`, `topology/face_tag`, `topology/edge_id`, `topology/provider`, `topology/resolve`, `topology/edge_resolve` modification; no `Operator` trait modification, no `OperatorGraph` modification, no `Tessellation` modification, no `topo_lineage` modification; no `cad-projection` / `gfx` / `kernel/*` modification; no second operator's fillet support (Extrude / Revolve / Loft fillet variants are subsequent dispatches); no Boolean / Sweep composition; no multi-edge corner-sharing geometry validation; no new substrate types (no `EdgeSelector`, no `FilletStrategy`, no `BlendKind` enum, no quaternion-based offset helpers — just `FilletOp` + `FilletError`); no Cargo.toml edit; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior operator file modified (cuboid.rs / extrude.rs / loft.rs / sweep.rs / transform.rs / boolean/ / revolve/ all byte-identical); no prior integration test files modified (all 13 prior B-Rep / face-identity / edge-identity / chain-resolution / phase-7-2-gate smokes byte-identical); no `OperatorNode` shape change beyond adding the `Fillet` variant (no new methods, no `#[non_exhaustive]` annotation added); no fillet-stub doctrine doc, no fillet ADR, no fillet lint exemption, no fillet snapshot integration; no reformatting unrelated files (one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply was needed to reformat the new files plus `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` and `crates/cad-core/src/operators/mod.rs` — no unrelated files touched).
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: NEW `crates/cad-core/src/operators/fillet.rs` (482L); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/mod.rs` (added `pub mod fillet;` + re-exports + `OpKind::Fillet` + `OperatorNode::Fillet` + `as_operator()` arm + dispatch test + non-exhaustive pattern test extension); `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` (added `FilletError, FilletOp` to alphabetically-sorted operators re-export); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/fillet_smoke.rs` (~250L; 7 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**407 / 407** tests; was 379; +28 net = 21 unit + 7 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2108 / 2108 pass** across 236 binaries (was 2080 / 235 binaries; +28 net = exact cad-core delta; +1 binary delta for the new integration test file; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the new file at 482L well below the 1000L threshold; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).

4. **D-7.2-ζ.ζ Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md gate-closure stress test (100 chains × 10 random rebuilds, deterministic seeded; Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion CLOSED)** (single-agent bounded test-only dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+7 net workspace tests = 1 main gate test + 6 sanity tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs` (~720L)**. The dispatch closes the rebuild-stability spirit of the Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion — after it lands, the entire D-7.2 chapter (sub-α through ζ.ζ; 10 dispatches total) is closed and the next chapter (Boolean propagation, D-Fillet, sub-7.4 lineage at scale, etc.) opens):
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs`** (~720L; 1 main gate test + 6 sanity tests on the harness machinery). Main gate test `phase_7_2_gate_closure_100_chains_10_rebuilds_seed_0x7e5a_dead_beef_c0de` runs 100 deterministic-seeded random operator chains × 10 random parameter rebuilds per chain (1000 mutations total) over the full Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft + Transform substrate. Build path: `generate_random_chain` selects RootKind ∈ {Cuboid, Extrude, Revolve, Loft} via `rng.next_range_u32(4)`, parameterizes the root (Cuboid: width/height/depth ∈ [0.5, 5.0]; Extrude: profile_n ∈ {3..=6} as a regular polygon, profile_radius ∈ [0.5, 3.0], length ∈ [0.5, 5.0]; Revolve: profile_n ∈ {3..=6}, segments ∈ {3..=16}, mode coin-flipped Full or Partial, angle ∈ (0, 2π] — Full = exactly 2π, Partial ∈ [0.1, π·1.9]; Loft: profile_n ∈ {3..=6}, profile_radius ∈ [0.5, 3.0] for profile_a + 1.5× radius for profile_b, length ∈ [0.5, 5.0]), then wraps in 0..=2 Transform layers each with translation ∈ [-5, 5]^3 and scale ∈ [0.5, 3]^3 (identity rotation for simplicity). Build-and-resolve uses `CadGraph::new() / begin_operation / graph_mut().add_operator(OperatorNode::X(op)) / connect / set_root / commit("phase-7-2-gate-closure")` then `brep_face_ids_for_node` + `brep_edge_ids_for_node` against the topmost operator.
   - **Mutation strategy**: `generate_random_mutation` decides per-rebuild whether to apply a topology-preserving mutation (numeric-only changes that don't affect the face-tag enum's BLAKE3 input) or a topology-changing mutation (changes that DO break face IDs by construction, propagating to edges). Cuboid roots only ever receive preserving mutations (Cuboid is fixed-topology); Extrude/Revolve/Loft roots get a 50/50 coin-flip between preserving and changing. Preserving mutations: Cuboid width/height/depth resampled; Extrude length OR profile_radius resampled (NOT profile_n); Revolve angle (within current mode) OR profile_radius resampled (NOT profile_n, NOT segments, NOT mode); Loft length OR profile_radius resampled (NOT profile_n). Changing mutations: Extrude/Loft pick a different profile_n in {3..=6}; Revolve picks a different profile_n OR a different segments in {3..=16} OR flips mode (Full↔Partial). Mutations always target the root direct-provider's parameters — Transform-parameter mutations are always topology-preserving and would not exercise the topology-changing branch (sub-7.2-ε's smokes already cover those). Boolean / Sweep are NOT in the chain generator (resolver returns `TopologyChangingOperator` for those — sub-7.2-ε's smokes cover those error paths).
   - **Assertions**: For each rebuilt chain, `assert_eq!(rebuilt_faces, initial_faces)` AND `assert_eq!(rebuilt_edges, initial_edges)` for preserving mutations, and `assert_ne!(rebuilt_faces, initial_faces)` AND `assert_ne!(rebuilt_edges, initial_edges)` for changing mutations. Vector-level inequality is the substrate's guarantee — Side faces / all edges ARE disjoint when topology changes; categorical caps (Bottom/Top in ExtrudeFaceTag/LoftFaceTag) intentionally preserve identity per the contract from sub-7.2-β/δ, so full disjointness cannot be asserted. Coverage gate `assert!(topology_preserving_count >= 100)` AND `assert!(topology_changing_count >= 50)` ensures both branches exercised; **recorded counts on fixed seed `0x7E5A_DEAD_BEEF_C0DE`: 623 preserving + 377 changing = 1000 mutations**. Failure messages include chain index, rebuild index, and seed for full reproducibility.
   - **Hand-rolled `TinyRng` (xorshift64)** with primitives `next_u64` / `next_range_u32` / `next_f32_in_range` / `next_bool` is the entire random infrastructure — **no Cargo.toml change permitted**, no `rand` / `proptest` / `quickcheck` / `arbitrary` dep. xorshift64 cannot accept seed=0 so the constructor `assert_ne!(seed, 0)` defends against future maintainers changing the constant.
   - **6 sanity tests on the harness machinery** (caught no bugs but exercise the harness on small fixed inputs to catch bugs before the full 1000-mutation gate): `tiny_rng_deterministic_for_fixed_seed` (same seed → same first 10 outputs); `tiny_rng_rejects_zero_seed` (`#[should_panic(expected = "xorshift64 cannot accept seed=0")]`); `chain_generator_visits_all_root_kinds` (300 trials cover all 4 RootKinds); `apply_preserving_mutation_keeps_topology_counts` (50 preserving mutations on a fixed Extrude N=4 chain — face count stays 6, edge count stays 12, IDs byte-identical); `apply_changing_mutation_alters_topology_counts_or_breaks_ids` (50 changing mutations on the same fixed chain — count differs OR IDs differ); `cuboid_chain_only_uses_preserving_mutations` (50 Cuboid chains × 5 mutations each — all asserted `MutationCategory::TopologyPreserving`).
   - **Honest framing — `TopologyEvolution` interpretation (LOAD-BEARING; appears in test module-doc, commit message, and this entry verbatim)**: The IMPLEMENTATION.md spec text (line 505) reads "100 operator chains × 10 random parameter rebuilds with face/edge IDs preserved per `TopologyEvolution` enum". `TopologyEvolution` lives in `crate::topo_lineage::types` (D-7.4 prototype substrate from 2026-05-07; `pub enum TopologyEvolution { Preserved, Split, Merged, Deleted, Reinterpreted }` capturing operator-internal face evolution like Boolean clip output). It is orthogonal to D-7.2's identity-stability-across-parameter-rebuilds substrate. **This dispatch closes the rebuild-stability spirit of the gate; `TopologyEvolution` remains the operator-internal lineage substrate (a separate concern, preserved for future work)**. Future readers should not have to wonder why a D-7.4 enum appears in a D-7.2 gate — the framing is stated plainly here, in the test's module-doc, and in the commit message.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion): no new substrate (no new IDs, no new resolver functions, no operator changes, no `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` modifications, no enum extensions, no new traits — substrate from sub-7.2-α through ζ.ε is complete and this dispatch consumes it byte-identically); no `Cargo.toml` modification (verified via `git diff --stat 9559960..HEAD -- crates/cad-core/Cargo.toml` empty); no `OperatorGraph` / `Operator` / `OperatorNode` modification; no `Tessellation` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel/* modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits (the IMPLEMENTATION.md spec text at line 505 is what this dispatch closes — do NOT edit it; this HANDOFF entry notes "closes Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion" as a status update without modifying the source spec); no prior test files modified (all 9 prior B-Rep integration tests + 4 prior face-identity smokes + face_id directory + face_tag.rs + provider.rs + resolve.rs + edge_id.rs + edge_resolve.rs byte-identical); no `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` modification; no criterion bench / `#[ignore]` opt-in (regular `#[test]` runs in default cargo test; expected runtime well under 30s — actual: ~0.4s end-to-end); no mutation of Transform parameters as a topology-preserving test path (sub-7.2-ε already covers those; mutations always target the root direct-provider's parameters); no Boolean / Sweep in the chain generator (resolver returns `TopologyChangingOperator` for those); no additional `rand`-style helpers (no `Distribution` trait, no `SliceRandom`, no `RngCore`); no reformatting unrelated files (one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply was permitted by the spec and used to reformat 3 small format-only diffs in the new test file).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~111 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --test phase_7_2_gate_closure --no-fail-fast` PASS (7 / 7 tests in ~0.04s — single-binary timing); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**379 / 379** tests; was 372; +7 net = 1 main gate + 6 sanity); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2080 / 2080 pass** across 235 binaries (was 2073 / 234 binaries; +7 net = exact cad-core delta; +1 binary delta for the new integration test file; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the new file at ~720L well below the 1000L threshold; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: ZERO new public symbols. **`impl BRepProvider` / `impl BRepEdgeProvider` counts in cad-core after this dispatch: still exactly 4 + 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft for both faces and edges; Transform deliberately remains non-provider for both).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships sub-7.2-ζ.ζ — the Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md gate-closure stress test. **It DOES close Phase 7.2's IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion** (line 505: "100 operator chains × 10 random parameter rebuilds with face/edge IDs preserved per `TopologyEvolution` enum") — closes the **rebuild-stability spirit** of that gate per the explicit framing above. The full D-7.2 chapter (sub-α through ζ.ζ; 10 dispatches total) is now closed: α (BRepOwnerId + BRepFaceId + Cuboid face provider); β (Extrude face provider — variable N+2 topology); γ (Revolve face provider — mode + segment topology); δ (Loft face provider — two-input topology); face_id refactor (1088L → 5-file directory); ε (face resolver via Transform inheritance); ζ.α (BRepEdgeId + BRepEdgeProvider + Cuboid edge provider); ζ.β/γ/δ (Extrude + Revolve + Loft edge providers, compressed); ζ.ε (edge resolver via Transform inheritance); ζ.ζ (this stress-test gate-closure dispatch). Next chapter (Boolean propagation, D-Fillet, sub-7.4 lineage at scale, etc.) opens.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/phase_7_2_gate_closure.rs` (~720L; 1 main gate test + 6 sanity tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).

2. **D-7.2-ζ.ε Graph-level B-Rep edge-identity resolver (Transform inheritance, mirror of sub-7.2-ε for edges)** (single-agent bounded substrate dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+14 net workspace tests = 5 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_resolve.rs::tests` + 9 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/brep_edge_chain_resolution_smoke.rs`**. The dispatch closes the chain layer for edges: a parallel free function `brep_edge_ids_for_node` mirroring `brep_face_ids_for_node` exactly. After this lands, all B-Rep identity machinery is in place — direct providers (Cuboid/Extrude/Revolve/Loft) → both faces and edges; identity-inheriting (Transform) → both faces and edges via the two parallel resolvers; topology-changing (Boolean/Sweep/future) → both resolvers return `TopologyChangingOperator`):
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_resolve.rs`** (404 lines, well below the 1000L split-exemption threshold). Introduces free function `pub fn brep_edge_ids_for_node(graph: &OperatorGraph, node: NodeId, owner: BRepOwnerId) -> Result<Vec<BRepEdgeId>, BRepResolveError>` plus internal helpers `resolve_recursive` (in-flight `HashSet<NodeId>` mirroring `OperatorGraph::evaluate`'s and `topology::resolve`'s cycle-detection pattern) + `resolve_step` (the dispatch match) + `single_input_node` (walks `Graph::incoming` to extract the unique upstream NodeId for arity-1 identity-preserving operators).
   - **Match arms in `resolve_step`**: `OperatorNode::Cuboid(op) | Extrude(op) | Revolve(op) | Loft(op)` each call `op.brep_edge_ids(owner)` verbatim; `OperatorNode::Transform(_)` recurses to its single `EdgeKind::Input(0)` upstream and returns those edges unchanged (owner propagated unchanged through chains); catch-all `other => Err(BRepResolveError::TopologyChangingOperator { kind: other.as_operator().op_kind() })` absorbs Boolean / Sweep / any future variant.
   - **`BRepResolveError` reused unchanged** from sub-7.2-ε — no `#[non_exhaustive]` insurance, no new error variants. The hypothetical "operator implements `BRepProvider` but not `BRepEdgeProvider`" case has no current consumer (all four current direct face providers also implement `BRepEdgeProvider`), and the catch-all covers any future variant identically to the face resolver.
   - **`single_input_node` helper strategy: Option (a) duplicate** — duplicated locally in `edge_resolve.rs` rather than promoting visibility on `topology::resolve`'s helper. `topology/resolve.rs` stays byte-identical (zero changes). Honest about cross-module independence; ~10 line duplication accepted as the cost of decoupling.
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/brep_edge_chain_resolution_smoke.rs`** ships 9 integration tests: `resolver_against_direct_cuboid_matches_direct_provider` (proves resolver doesn't double-process direct providers; asserts 12 edges); **load-bearing `cuboid_through_transform_inherits_cuboid_edges` (Transform inheritance gate: `assert_eq!(chain_edges, direct_edges, "Transform must inherit Cuboid edges unchanged")` plus `assert_eq!(chain_edges.len(), 12)`)**; `transform_parameter_changes_do_not_change_edges` (3 transforms — pure translate / pure rotate ~40° around Y / pure scale 2.5x — all produce byte-identical edge IDs); `multi_hop_transforms_preserve_edges` (Cuboid → Transform → Transform inherits Cuboid edges at the second Transform); `different_owners_stay_disjoint_through_transform_chain` (`[0x11; 16]` vs `[0x22; 16]` produce disjoint edge identity spaces through chains); `boolean_returns_topology_changing_error`; `sweep_returns_topology_changing_error`; `unknown_node_returns_not_in_graph_error`; **cross-substrate compositional check `face_and_edge_resolvers_agree_on_transform_inheritance`** — calls both `brep_face_ids_for_node` AND `brep_edge_ids_for_node` against the same Cuboid → Transform chain; asserts `chain_faces == direct_faces` AND `chain_edges == direct_edges`. Cross-validates the two resolvers use the same chain semantics.
   - **Unit tests in `topology::edge_resolve::tests`** (5): `error_node_not_in_graph_returns_correct_variant`, `error_topology_changing_operator_carries_correct_kind` (Boolean and Sweep both correctly tagged via the catch-all), `error_unexpected_arity_when_transform_has_no_input` (Transform without incoming edge → `UnexpectedArity { expected: 1, got: 0 }`), `resolver_direct_cuboid_matches_direct_provider_call`, `resolver_direct_extrude_revolve_loft_match_direct_provider` (covers all 4 direct-edge-provider arms of the resolver match in a single comprehensive unit test).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs`**: added `mod edge_resolve;` (alphabetical position after `mod edge_id;`); added `pub use edge_resolve::brep_edge_ids_for_node;` (alphabetical position after `pub use edge_id::BRepEdgeId;`). **`crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs`**: re-export list extended from `pub use topology::{brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepEdgeId, ...};` to `pub use topology::{brep_edge_ids_for_node, brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepEdgeId, ...};` — alphabetical order preserved.
   - **Architectural posture (load-bearing)**: edge identity inheritance lives at the **graph resolver layer**, NOT inside `TransformOp`. `BRepEdgeProvider` stays "operator can mint its own local edge IDs." Transform stays semantically truthful (it changes placement, not topology) and remains a non-`BRepEdgeProvider`. Chain semantics live where the chain lives, not on the operator. This mirrors the sub-7.2-ε pattern exactly.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion): no `BRepResolveError` modification (no `#[non_exhaustive]` insurance, no new error variants); no `OperatorGraph` API additions (resolver uses only existing public `node`/`inner` + `Graph::incoming`/`edge` — verified via `git diff --stat 4b1b3b6..HEAD -- crates/cad-core/src/graph/` empty); no `BRepProvider` / `BRepEdgeProvider` / `BRepEdgeId` / `BRepFaceId` modification (all upstream substrate byte-identical); no `topology::resolve` modification (face-resolver byte-identical — Option (a) elected over Option (b)); no new direct provider impl for Boolean / Sweep / Transform (Boolean and Sweep return error; Transform is identity-inheriting); no `Operator` trait modification, no `OperatorNode` modification; no `Tessellation` / `topo_lineage` / `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel/* modification; no fillet prep, no edge graph, no `TopologyEdgeId`, no projection plumbing; no stress-test gate-closure work (sub-7.2-ζ.ζ); no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion / Cargo.toml edit; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior integration tests modified (the four face-identity smokes, four edge-identity smokes, and the face-chain-resolution smoke all byte-identical); no reformatting of unrelated files (no mid-dispatch fmt apply needed).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**372 / 372** tests; was 358; +14 net = 5 unit + 9 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2073 / 2073 pass** across 234 binaries (was 2059 / 233 binaries; +14 net = exact cad-core delta; +1 binary for the new integration test file); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (no mid-dispatch fmt apply needed); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the 2 new files at 404L + 444L well below the 1000L threshold; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).

   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships sub-7.2-ζ.ε (graph-level Transform inheritance for edges, mirror of sub-7.2-ε for faces). It does NOT close Phase 7.2's full IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion. Sub-7.2-ζ.ζ (Phase 7.2 stress-test gate-closure: 100 chains × 10 random rebuilds with face+edge IDs preserved per `TopologyEvolution`) becomes the next and final substrate dispatch before Phase 7.2 closes.
