2. **D-7.2-ζ.β/γ/δ Extrude + Revolve + Loft B-Rep edge identity (compressed dispatch)** (single-agent bounded substrate dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+21 net workspace tests = 10 unit tests across the three operators + 11 integration tests across 3 new smoke files**. Three additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider` blocks below the existing `impl BRepProvider` blocks, one per direct face provider beyond Cuboid; all use `local_ordinal = 0` literal at every `BRepEdgeId::for_face_pair` call site):
   - **`ExtrudeOp` (~50L additive impl)**: `3 * N` edges in canonical order — N bottom-perimeter (`Bottom (TopologyFaceId(0)) ∩ Side(i) (TopologyFaceId(2 + i))` for `i in 0..N`), then N top-perimeter (`Top (TopologyFaceId(1)) ∩ Side(i)` for `i in 0..N`), then N vertical-seam (`Side(i) ∩ Side((i + 1) % N)`). Square (N=4) → 12 edges; triangle (N=3) → 9; pentagon (N=5) → 15.
   - **`RevolveOp` (~70L additive impl below the existing BRepProvider impl in `revolve/mod.rs`)**: edge count and shape **depend on `is_full_revolution()`** — Full mode yields exactly `n` edges (Side-Side adjacencies only; the closed circular path swept by each profile-vertex shared between profile edges `i` and `i + 1`; no caps means no cap-perimeter edges). Partial mode yields exactly `3n` edges (n axial seams + n start-cap-perimeter `StartCap (TopologyFaceId(n)) ∩ Side(i)` + n end-cap-perimeter `EndCap (TopologyFaceId(n + 1)) ∩ Side(i)`). Mode is driven by the **same** `is_full_revolution()` discriminator the BRepProvider impl uses (1e-6 epsilon vs 2π); the BRep substrate does not recompute the boundary epsilon locally.
   - **`LoftOp` (~55L additive impl)**: `3 * N` edges, same shape as Extrude (Loft is structurally Extrude with a distinct top ring); defensive `n_a.min(n_b)` cap mirrors the BRepProvider impl above (`LoftOp::evaluate` enforces equal counts at runtime, but `profile_a` / `profile_b` are publicly assignable, so taking the minimum removes a panic surface).
   - **Compositional-honesty check load-bearing**: `revolve_full_and_partial_edge_ids_are_disjoint` in `revolve_edge_identity_smoke.rs` is the gate that proves sub-7.2-γ's mode break propagates to edges by construction — Full mode with 8 segments produces 4 edges; Partial mode with 8 segments at angle `π * 1.99` produces 12 edges; nested-loop `assert!(!partial_edges.contains(full_edge), "full-mode edge ID leaked into partial-mode set; mode break must propagate to edges")` proves the two sets are disjoint. Edge IDs differ because face IDs differ (mode is in the Side face tag's BLAKE3 input, per sub-7.2-γ); the face substrate's mode break propagates through edge derivation automatically — this test is the gate that proves it does.
   - **Unit tests at the bottom of existing `mod tests` blocks** (3 per Extrude / 4 per Revolve / 3 per Loft = 10 total; **NO modification to existing tests — additive only**): `brep_edge_provider_returns_expected_edge_count` (Extrude/Loft: 3N; Revolve: full=n, partial=3n at multiple N), `brep_edge_ids_use_local_ordinal_zero` (manual reconstruction via `BRepEdgeId::for_face_pair(.., .., 0)` proves byte equality), `brep_edge_ids_align_with_canonical_adjacency_table` (verifies 3 representative edges per operator from the documented adjacency table). Revolve gets one extra unit test: `brep_edge_provider_full_and_partial_yield_different_counts` (same profile n=4 → Full=4, Partial=12).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_edge_identity_smoke.rs`** (3 integration tests): `extrude_edge_ids_stable_across_length_changes` (3 lengths same profile → identical 12 IDs); `extrude_edge_ids_break_when_profile_count_changes` (square → pentagon: 12 vs 15 edges, all disjoint); `extrude_edge_ids_distinct_across_owners`. **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_edge_identity_smoke.rs`** (5 integration tests including the load-bearing `revolve_full_and_partial_edge_ids_are_disjoint`): `revolve_partial_edge_ids_stable_across_angle_changes_within_partial_mode`, `revolve_full_edge_ids_stable_across_shape_size_changes`, `revolve_full_and_partial_edge_ids_are_disjoint` ★ load-bearing ★, `revolve_edge_ids_break_when_segment_count_changes`, `revolve_edge_ids_distinct_across_owners`. **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_edge_identity_smoke.rs`** (3 integration tests): `loft_edge_ids_stable_across_length_changes`, `loft_edge_ids_break_when_profile_count_changes` (square×square → pentagon×pentagon: 12 vs 15 edges, all disjoint; both profiles change together since LoftOp::evaluate enforces equal counts), `loft_edge_ids_distinct_across_owners`.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion): no `BRepProvider` modification (sub-7.2-α through ε trait stays exactly as-is); no `BRepEdgeProvider` modification (sub-7.2-ζ.α trait stays exactly as-is); no `BRepEdgeId` modification (sub-7.2-ζ.α type and constructor stay byte-identical); no `local_ordinal` other than 0 in any of the three impls; no edge resolver / no graph-level `brep_edge_ids_for_node` (sub-7.2-ζ.ε at earliest); no `TopologyEdgeId` type / no per-edge labels on `Tessellation`; no edge graph / no `BRepEdgeGraph` / no `EdgeAdjacency`; no fillet prep / no edge-blend operator / no edge selection API; no `Tessellation` modification / no `OperatorNode` modification / no `Operator` trait modification; no `OperatorGraph` modification / no `cad-projection`, `gfx`, kernel/* modification; no fifth direct `BRepProvider` impl (Boolean / Sweep / Transform stay un-tagged for both faces and edges); no deriving owner from `NodeId` / `effective_hash` anywhere; no prior-dispatch substrate modified (all sub-7.2-α through ζ.α artifacts byte-identical: `face_id/`, `face_tag.rs`, `provider.rs`, `resolve.rs`, `edge_id.rs`, prior `impl BRepProvider for X` blocks, `impl BRepEdgeProvider for CuboidOp`); no prior integration tests modified; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / Cargo.toml edit; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**358 / 358** tests; was 337; +21 net = 10 unit + 11 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2059 / 2059 pass** across 233 binaries (was 2038 / 230 binaries; +21 net = exact cad-core delta; +3 binary delta for the 3 new integration test files; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the 3 new integration files; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: ZERO new public symbols. Existing public surface UNCHANGED — `BRepEdgeId` and `BRepEdgeProvider` were already re-exported at the crate root from sub-7.2-ζ.α; this dispatch only adds three new `impl BRepEdgeProvider for X` blocks. **`impl BRepEdgeProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch: exactly 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships sub-7.2-ζ.β + γ + δ together (Extrude + Revolve + Loft direct edge providers); the full Phase 7.2 IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion is NOT closed by this. Sub-7.2-ζ.ε (graph-level edge resolver, mirror of sub-7.2-ε for faces) becomes the next dispatch, and Phase 7.2 stress-test gate-closure (sub-7.2-ζ.ζ) becomes meaningful only after that.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: `crates/cad-core/src/operators/extrude.rs` (additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for ExtrudeOp` block + 3 unit tests at bottom of `mod tests`; existing `impl BRepProvider for ExtrudeOp` byte-identical); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/revolve/mod.rs` (additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for RevolveOp` block; existing `impl BRepProvider for RevolveOp` byte-identical); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/revolve/tests.rs` (4 unit tests at bottom only — no modification to existing tests); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/loft.rs` (additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for LoftOp` block + 3 unit tests at bottom of `mod tests`; existing `impl BRepProvider for LoftOp` byte-identical); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/extrude_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (3 integration tests); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/revolve_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (5 integration tests including the load-bearing compositional-honesty gate); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (3 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).

2. **D-7.2-ζ.α Minimum B-Rep edge-identity substrate (Cuboid only)** (single-agent bounded substrate dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+13 net workspace tests = 9 unit tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_id.rs::tests` + 2 unit tests in existing `crates/cad-core/src/operators/cuboid.rs::tests` mod block (additive only) + 2 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/cuboid_edge_identity_smoke.rs`**. The dispatch ships the FIRST SLICE of edge identity — minimum viable substrate to validate the identity scheme on Cuboid alone before chasing variable-topology operators):
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_id.rs`** (226 lines, well below the 1000L split-exemption threshold). Introduces `BRepEdgeId([u8; 16])` 16-byte BLAKE3-derived stable edge identity (`Clone, Copy, Debug, PartialEq, Eq, Hash, PartialOrd, Ord, Serialize, Deserialize`); `BRepEdgeId::for_face_pair(face_a: BRepFaceId, face_b: BRepFaceId, local_ordinal: u32) -> Self` constructor sorts inputs lexicographically by `[u8; 16]` so `for_face_pair(a, b, k) == for_face_pair(b, a, k)`; `BRepEdgeId::from_bytes`/`as_bytes` const accessors mirror `BRepFaceId` precedent; `Display` impl produces `"edge:abcdef01"` 4-byte hex prefix.
   - **Derivation**: `BRepEdgeId = first 16 bytes of BLAKE3(b"rge.cad.brep.edge/v1:" || sorted(face_a.as_bytes(), face_b.as_bytes()) || local_ordinal.to_le_bytes())`. **Domain separator `b"rge.cad.brep.edge/v1:"` is distinct from face-id derivation `b"rge.cad.brep.face/v1:"`** — verified by `edge_id_distinct_from_face_id_via_domain_separator` test using degenerate-but-valid `for_face_pair(f, f, 0)` input. Owner is NOT directly hashed — already baked into both face IDs (each `BRepFaceId` includes owner in its derivation), so owner disjointness is preserved transitively.
   - **`local_ordinal: u32` slot**: for all current operators (Cuboid / Extrude / Revolve / Loft v0), every edge has `local_ordinal = 0` because two adjacent faces share at most one edge in these topologies. Slot is reserved for future operators with multi-edge face pairs (e.g., faces with holes, non-convex sweeps) — extends without v2 derivation-scheme migration. The `for_face_pair_local_ordinal_distinguishes` test verifies the byte derivation respects the slot even though current operators only use `0`.
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/provider.rs`**: extended ADDITIVELY with `BRepEdgeProvider` trait alongside the unchanged `BRepProvider` trait. **Sibling trait — NOT a supertrait extension, NOT a default-method extension**; implementing one does NOT imply the other. Keeping them independent lets each operator opt in to edge identity when its edge topology has been explicitly inspected, without pressure to return half-baked edge IDs ahead of that inspection. Trait method: `fn brep_edge_ids(&self, owner: BRepOwnerId) -> Vec<BRepEdgeId>` (flat `Vec`, not `Vec<(TopologyEdgeId, BRepEdgeId)>` — `TopologyEdgeId` substrate is deferred until consumer pressure surfaces).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/operators/cuboid.rs`**: imports widened to `use crate::topology::{BRepEdgeId, BRepEdgeProvider, BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, CuboidFaceTag};`. New additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for CuboidOp` block (~70L) below the existing `impl BRepProvider for CuboidOp` returning 12 edge IDs in canonical order via a frozen 12-pair adjacency table: 4 bottom-face perimeter (NegZ ∩ NegY/PosY/NegX/PosX), 4 top-face perimeter (PosZ ∩ NegY/PosY/NegX/PosX), 4 vertical (NegY/PosY × NegX/PosX). `local_ordinal = 0` literal for every cuboid edge (no two non-opposite cuboid faces share more than one edge). `debug_assert_eq!` on `face_ids.len() == 6` defensive check. NO modification to existing `evaluate` / `validate` / `structural_hash` / `Default` / `op_kind` / `arity` / `impl BRepProvider for CuboidOp` block (all byte-identical) / existing tests.
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/cuboid_edge_identity_smoke.rs`** (~70L; 2 integration tests): `cuboid_edge_ids_stable_across_parameter_rebuilds` (3 cuboid rebuilds with different dimensions 1.0×1.0×1.0 / 2.0×1.0×1.0 / 0.5×2.0×0.5; same owner [0xed; 16]; asserts `edges_a == edges_b` and `edges_b == edges_c` and `edges_a.len() == 12`); `cuboid_edge_ids_distinct_across_owners` (owners [0x11; 16] vs [0x22; 16] produce disjoint edge identity spaces). Mirrors sub-7.2-α `brep_face_identity_smoke.rs` precedent.
   - **Unit tests in `topology::edge_id::tests`** (9 tests): `for_face_pair_deterministic`, `for_face_pair_order_independent` (3 distinct face pairs each verified swapped-args symmetry), `for_face_pair_local_ordinal_distinguishes`, `for_face_pair_distinct_for_different_pairs`, `for_face_pair_owner_disjointness_via_face_ids`, `edge_id_distinct_from_face_id_via_domain_separator` (degenerate-but-valid `for_face_pair(f, f, 0)` where `f = BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face(owner, NegZ)`; asserts `e.as_bytes() != f.as_bytes()`), `edge_id_byte_format` (`from_bytes(.) / as_bytes(&)` round-trip), `edge_id_serde_round_trip` (ron-based, mirrors face_id precedent), `edge_id_display_format` (`format!("{id}") == "edge:abcdef01"`).
   - **Unit tests in `crates/cad-core/src/operators/cuboid.rs::tests`** (2 tests added at the END of the existing `mod tests` block; no modification to existing 7 tests): `brep_edge_provider_returns_12_unique_edges` (12 pairwise-distinct ids), `brep_edge_ids_align_with_canonical_adjacency_table` (verifies positions 0/4/8 manually computed via `BRepEdgeId::for_face_pair(face_ids[a], face_ids[b], 0)` from the documented adjacency table — NegZ ∩ NegY at edge 0, PosZ ∩ NegY at edge 4, NegY ∩ NegX at edge 8).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs`**: added `mod edge_id;` (alphabetical position before `mod face_id;`); added `pub use edge_id::BRepEdgeId;` (alphabetical position before `pub use face_id::{...}`); extended `pub use provider::BRepProvider;` to `pub use provider::{BRepEdgeProvider, BRepProvider};` (alphabetical within braces).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs`**: re-export list extended from `pub use topology::{brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, BRepResolveError, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` to `pub use topology::{brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepEdgeId, BRepEdgeProvider, BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, BRepResolveError, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` — alphabetical order within type-block preserved.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion): no Extrude / Revolve / Loft / Sweep / Boolean / Transform `BRepEdgeProvider` impl (Cuboid only); no edge resolver / no `brep_edge_ids_for_node` graph-level resolver (sub-7.2-ζ.ε at earliest); no `TopologyEdgeId` type / no per-edge labels on `Tessellation` / no `edge_labels: Option<Vec<TopologyEdgeId>>` field (defer until consumer pressure surfaces); no edge graph / no `BRepEdgeGraph` / no `EdgeAdjacency` / no graph-foundation reuse for edges; no `BRepEdgeProvider: BRepProvider` supertrait bound (independent traits — partial rollout stays honest); no `BRepProvider` modification (sub-7.2-α's trait stays exactly as-is); no fillet prep / no edge-blend operator / no edge selection API / no edge round/chamfer machinery; no `Tessellation` modification / no `OperatorNode` modification / no `Operator` trait modification / no `OperatorGraph` modification; no deriving owner from `NodeId` / `effective_hash` in any new code path; no prior-dispatch substrate modified (sub-7.2-α through ε artifacts byte-identical: `face_id/` directory + `face_tag.rs` + `provider.rs`'s `BRepProvider` definition + `resolve.rs` + per-operator `impl BRepProvider` blocks); no prior integration tests modified; no `cad-projection`, `gfx`, kernel/* modification; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion / Cargo.toml edit; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no reformatting unrelated files (one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply was permitted by the spec and used to reformat one method-chain in `cuboid.rs::brep_edge_ids_align_with_canonical_adjacency_table`); no coordinate-aware identity (matches sub-7.2-β/γ/δ precedent); no raw-geometry hashing (edge IDs come from face IDs and an integer ordinal; no coordinates); no `local_ordinal` other than 0 in any current operator's edge derivation.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**337 / 337** tests; was 324; +13 net = 9 unit edge_id + 2 unit cuboid + 2 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2038 / 2038 pass** across 230 binaries (was 2025 / 229; +13 tests / +1 binary for the new integration test; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the new file at 226L well below the 1000L threshold; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: + `BRepEdgeId` + `BRepEdgeProvider` (two new public symbols at crate root). Existing public surface UNCHANGED. **`impl BRepProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch: still exactly 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft). **`impl BRepEdgeProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch: exactly 1** (Cuboid).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships sub-7.2-ζ.α (Cuboid edge identity primitive). It does NOT close Phase 7.2's full IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion. Sub-7.2-ζ.β/γ/δ (Extrude / Revolve / Loft `BRepEdgeProvider` impls), edge resolver (graph-level Transform inheritance for edges), `TopologyEdgeId` substrate, edge graph, and Phase 7.2 stress-test gate-closure all remain open as subsequent dispatches.
   - **Resisted expansion-pressure** during shaping (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): rejected second operator's `BRepEdgeProvider` impl "for completeness" (Cuboid-only by spec); rejected edge resolver `brep_edge_ids_for_node` (sub-7.2-ζ.ε at earliest); rejected `TopologyEdgeId` substrate; rejected `BRepEdgeGraph` / `EdgeAdjacency` graph-foundation reuse for edges; rejected `BRepEdgeProvider: BRepProvider` supertrait bound (independence keeps partial rollout honest); rejected `BRepProvider` modification; rejected fillet prep / edge-blend operator / edge selection API; rejected `Tessellation` / `OperatorNode` / `Operator` trait / `OperatorGraph` modification; rejected deriving owner from `NodeId` / `effective_hash`; rejected `local_ordinal` other than 0; rejected coordinate-aware identity / raw-geometry hashing.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/edge_id.rs` (226L; 9 unit tests); modified `crates/cad-core/src/topology/provider.rs` (additive `BRepEdgeProvider` trait; `BRepProvider` definition byte-identical); modified `crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs` (`mod edge_id;` + 2 re-export lines); modified `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` (re-export list extended); modified `crates/cad-core/src/operators/cuboid.rs` (additive `impl BRepEdgeProvider for CuboidOp` + 2 unit tests; existing `impl BRepProvider for CuboidOp` byte-identical); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/cuboid_edge_identity_smoke.rs` (~70L; 2 integration tests); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).

2. **D-7.2-ε Graph-level B-Rep face-identity resolver (Transform inheritance, no `TransformOp` `BRepProvider` impl)** (single-agent bounded substrate dispatch in `A:\RCAD\RGE\`. **+16 net workspace tests = 8 unit tests in `crates/cad-core/src/topology/resolve.rs::tests` + 8 integration tests in NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/brep_chain_resolution_smoke.rs`**. The dispatch answers the question "does identity propagate through Transform?" with: yes, but at the **graph resolver layer**, NOT inside `TransformOp`. `BRepProvider` stays as "operator can mint its own local face IDs"; `TransformOp` stays semantically truthful (it changes placement, not topology) and remains a non-`BRepProvider`; chain semantics live where the chain lives, not on the operator):
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/resolve.rs`** (521 lines, well below the 1000L split-exemption threshold) introduces `BRepResolveError` (4-variant `#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Error)]` enum: `NodeNotInGraph { node }` / `TopologyChangingOperator { kind: OpKind }` / `UnexpectedArity { node, expected, got }` / `CycleDetected { node }`) plus the public free function `pub fn brep_face_ids_for_node(graph: &OperatorGraph, node: NodeId, owner: BRepOwnerId) -> Result<Vec<(TopologyFaceId, BRepFaceId)>, BRepResolveError>`. Internal helpers: `resolve_recursive` (mirrors `OperatorGraph::evaluate`'s in-flight `HashSet<NodeId>` cycle-detection pattern; insert-on-entry / remove-on-exit so sibling subtrees with overlapping ancestors still resolve), `resolve_step` (the dispatch match), `single_input_node` (walks `Graph::incoming` then `Graph::edge` to extract the unique upstream `NodeId` for arity-1 identity-preserving operators).
   - **Match dispatch in `resolve_step`**: `OperatorNode::Cuboid(op) | Extrude(op) | Revolve(op) | Loft(op)` each return `Ok(op.brep_face_ids(owner))` verbatim (delegating to the existing `BRepProvider` impls — no double-processing); `OperatorNode::Transform(_)` calls `single_input_node(graph, node)?` to find its unique `EdgeKind::Input(0)` upstream and recurses (`resolve_recursive(graph, upstream, owner, in_flight)`), returning those IDs unchanged with `owner` propagated through; catch-all `other => Err(BRepResolveError::TopologyChangingOperator { kind: other.as_operator().op_kind() })` absorbs Boolean / Sweep / any future variant via the `Operator::op_kind` trait method (so future-added variants surface their accurate kind, not a hardcoded discriminant).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/brep_chain_resolution_smoke.rs`** (8 integration tests): `resolver_against_direct_cuboid_matches_direct_provider` (proves resolver doesn't double-process direct providers — direct call vs through-resolver call produce identical IDs); **load-bearing `cuboid_through_transform_inherits_cuboid_ids` (Transform inheritance gate: `assert_eq!(chain_ids, direct_ids, "Transform must inherit Cuboid IDs unchanged")` with explicit failure message)**; `transform_parameter_changes_do_not_change_ids` (3 transforms — pure translate `[5,0,0]` / pure rotate ~40° around Y / pure scale `[2.5;3]` — all produce byte-identical face IDs because Transform parameters never enter the BLAKE3 derivation); **load-bearing `multi_hop_transforms_preserve_ids` (Cuboid → Transform → Transform: resolving at the second Transform returns IDs equal to the direct Cuboid IDs)**; `different_owners_stay_disjoint_through_transform_chain` (`[0x11; 16]` vs `[0x22; 16]` produce disjoint identity spaces through chains, mirroring the direct-provider precedent); `boolean_returns_topology_changing_error` (Boolean → `Err(BRepResolveError::TopologyChangingOperator { kind: OpKind::Boolean })`); `sweep_returns_topology_changing_error` (Sweep → `Err(BRepResolveError::TopologyChangingOperator { kind: OpKind::Sweep })`); `unknown_node_returns_not_in_graph_error` (`NodeId::from_raw(u128::MAX)` → `NodeNotInGraph { node: fresh }`).
   - **Unit tests in `topology::resolve::tests`** (8 tests): `error_node_not_in_graph_returns_correct_variant` (synthesized `NodeId` against fresh graph), `error_topology_changing_operator_carries_correct_kind` (Boolean and Sweep both correctly tagged), `error_unexpected_arity_when_transform_has_no_input` (Transform with zero incoming edges → `UnexpectedArity { expected: 1, got: 0 }` — reachable through public API because `OperatorGraph::connect` does NOT validate arity at attach time, only `evaluate` does; this is structural graph-construction territory and the resolver surfaces it rather than panicking), `error_cycle_detected_unreachable_through_public_api_documented` (defensive variant; documented as unreachable through `OperatorGraph` public API, sanity-tested via `Display` + `Clone` + `PartialEq` round-trip on a synthetic value), `error_display_renders_for_all_variants` (4-variant `Display` smoke), `error_clone_partialeq_eq_round_trip` (derive bundle smoke), `resolver_direct_cuboid_matches_direct_provider_call`, `resolver_direct_extrude_and_revolve_match_direct_provider` (covers all 4 direct-provider arms of the resolver match — Extrude + Revolve through resolver match their direct `BRepProvider::brep_face_ids` calls).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs`**: `mod resolve;` added below the existing `mod face_id; mod face_tag; mod provider;` declarations; `pub use resolve::{brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepResolveError};` re-export added below the existing 3 `pub use` lines.
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs`**: re-export list extended from `pub use topology::{BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` to `pub use topology::{brep_face_ids_for_node, BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, BRepResolveError, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};`. Function listed first per the `topo_lineage` precedent at L50-52 (functions before types within a single `pub use` block); types alphabetical. Rustfmt re-ordered into a 3-line block.
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion): no `impl BRepProvider for TransformOp` (Transform stays a non-provider — that's the architectural decision); no new `BRepFaceId` constructor (no `for_transform_face` — Transform inherits, doesn't mint); no `BRepProvider` trait modification; no `OperatorGraph` API additions or modifications (`git diff --stat crates/cad-core/src/graph/` empty — resolver uses ONLY existing public methods: `OperatorGraph::node`, `OperatorGraph::inner`, `Graph::incoming`, `Graph::edge`); no `OperatorNode` modification; no `Operator` trait modification; no `Tessellation` modification, no `topo_lineage` modification; no fifth direct `BRepProvider` impl (Boolean / Sweep stay un-tagged AND the resolver returns explicit error for them — no sneaking `BRepProvider for BooleanOp` "for completeness"); no edge IDs (sub-7.2-ζ); no `cad-projection`, `gfx`, kernel/* modification; no D-Fillet prep; no new ADR / lint / doctrine doc / §18 companion / Cargo.toml edit; no PLAN, IMPLEMENTATION, fileandfolderstructure, versions edits; no prior-dispatch substrate modified (Cuboid / Extrude / Revolve / Loft `BRepProvider` impls byte-identical; the five `face_id/` files byte-identical; `face_tag.rs` byte-identical; prior integration tests `brep_face_identity_smoke.rs`, `extrude_face_identity_smoke.rs`, `revolve_face_identity_smoke.rs`, `loft_face_identity_smoke.rs` byte-identical); no deriving owner from `NodeId` or `effective_hash` in any code path (the owner is caller-supplied and propagated unchanged through Transform chains); no cleanup pass touching things outside the resolver scope; one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply was permitted by the spec and used.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (the initial unused-import warning for `Operator` was fixed before any further work — `op_kind()` is callable through `&dyn Operator` without the trait being in scope by name); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**324 / 324** tests; was 308; +16 net = 8 unit + 8 integration); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2025 / 2025 pass** across 229 binaries (was 2009 / 222 binaries; +16 tests / +7 binary delta — the 1 new integration-test binary plus 6 doc-test binary differences from refresh; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0 (after one mid-dispatch `cargo +nightly fmt --all` apply); `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; `split-exemption` lint **0 violations 0 exemptions** for the new file at 521L well below the 1000L threshold; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Public API delta**: + `brep_face_ids_for_node` free function + `BRepResolveError` error enum (two new public symbols at crate root). Existing public surface UNCHANGED. **`impl BRepProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch: still exactly 4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft — no new impls; `TransformOp` deliberately remains a non-provider).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch ships sub-7.2-ε (graph-level Transform inheritance via a new resolver function). It does NOT close Phase 7.2's full IMPLEMENTATION.md exit criterion. That criterion needs edges (sub-7.2-ζ), Boolean propagation, projection plumbing, and chain composition under coordinate-aware identity (rotation matching, etc.) — all of which are subsequent dispatches.
   - **Resisted expansion-pressure** during shaping (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): rejected `impl BRepProvider for TransformOp` (architectural posture: Transform stays non-provider; chain logic lives at graph layer); rejected `BRepFaceId::for_transform_face` constructor (Transform inherits, doesn't mint); rejected fifth direct provider impl for Boolean or Sweep "for completeness" (resolver returns explicit error instead — substrate honesty); rejected adding any public helper to `OperatorGraph` (resolver uses existing public API only); rejected sneaking edges / projection / Boolean propagation in (those are subsequent dispatches); rejected adding any visibility annotations or new modules; rejected centralizing the recursive `HashSet<NodeId>` pattern into a graph-foundation helper (cycle detection's three-implementation divergence pattern is documented in `operator_graph.rs::8-47` — the resolver uses the same pattern locally, deliberately not unifying). **`OperatorGraph` API surface confirmed UNTOUCHED**: `git diff --stat crates/cad-core/src/graph/` reports empty. **`TransformOp` `BRepProvider` impl confirmed ABSENT**: `Grep "impl BRepProvider for Transform" crates/cad-core/` returns 0 matches.
   - **API adaptation**: the spec's anticipated `OperatorNode::Cuboid(op)` payload-field call shape `op.brep_face_ids(owner)` works exactly as written (each variant payload — `CuboidOp`, `ExtrudeOp`, `RevolveOp`, `LoftOp` — implements `BRepProvider`). The `as_operator()` method exists on `OperatorNode` (operators/mod.rs line 205, returning `&dyn Operator`); `Operator::op_kind` trait method is `op_kind(&self) -> OpKind`. No mechanical adaptations needed beyond what was inlined into the spec's example code. One adaptation: rather than building `OperatorGraph` directly in tests, every integration test uses `CadGraph::new() / begin_operation / graph_mut().add_operator(OperatorNode::Cuboid(op)) / connect / commit / graph()` — the canonical chain-construction idiom from `tests/cad_smoke.rs` — because there's no `From<X> for OperatorNode` impl and no `OperatorGraph::add_operator` accepting a non-wrapped variant.
   - **Files modified (within MAY-list)**: NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/resolve.rs` (521L); NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/brep_chain_resolution_smoke.rs` (~370L; 8 integration tests); modified `crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs` (+ `mod resolve;` and re-export line); modified `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` (re-export list extended); `Status.md` + `change.md` + `HANDOFF.md` (this entry + sibling status updates).

2. **face_id refactor — pure-mechanical split for sub-7.2-ε runway** (single-agent bounded refactor cleanup in `crates/cad-core/src/topology/`. **NOT a substrate addition** — pre-emptive cleanup before sub-7.2-ε chain composition. Pure mechanics: 0 test delta / 0 byte-output change / 0 API surface change / 0 new types / 0 new tests. Establishes clean per-operator runway; sub-7.2-ε will want to touch identity construction and we want it to land on a clean per-operator layout, not on a 1088-line single file):
   - **DELETED `crates/cad-core/src/topology/face_id.rs`** (1088L; sub-7.2-δ pushed it past the 1000L split-exemption threshold + a `// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation was added to its head documenting the cohesive owner-seed + per-operator face-identity constructor module that grows by ~12 tests + 1 constructor + 1 KIND const per per-operator BRepProvider sub-dispatch).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/src/topology/face_id/`** directory with 5 files (1116L cumulative; ~28L per-file imports + module-doc overhead vs single-file 1088L):
     - `mod.rs` (195L): `BRepOwnerId` (caller-supplied opaque 16-byte owner seed) + `BRepFaceId` core type + `DOMAIN: &'static [u8] = b"rge.cad.brep.face/v1:"` const + 4 `KIND_X: &'static [u8]` consts (`b"cuboid:"` / `b"extrude:"` / `b"revolve:"` / `b"loft:"`) + `as_bytes()` accessor + module declarations (`mod cuboid; mod extrude; mod loft; mod revolve;`) + 4 cross-cutting tests (`owner_id_round_trips_through_bytes` / `owner_id_serde_round_trips` / `face_id_serde_round_trips` / `owner_zero_max_distinct`).
     - `cuboid.rs` (120L): `pub fn for_cuboid_face(owner, tag) -> Self` constructor + 5 cuboid tests (`for_cuboid_face_is_deterministic` / `for_cuboid_face_distinguishes_all_six_tags` / `for_cuboid_face_changes_when_owner_changes` / `domain_separator_makes_id_distinct_from_undecorated_blake3` / `for_cuboid_face_truncates_blake3_first_16_bytes`).
     - `extrude.rs` (177L): `pub fn for_extrude_face(owner, tag) -> Self` constructor + 5 extrude tests (`for_extrude_face_deterministic` / `for_extrude_face_distinct_across_tags` / `for_extrude_face_distinct_across_owners` / `for_extrude_face_count_change_breaks_side_id` / `for_extrude_face_distinct_from_for_cuboid_face_with_same_owner` — newer-operator placement rule: cross-operator distinctness lives with the newer operator's file).
     - `revolve.rs` (323L): `pub fn for_revolve_face(owner, tag) -> Self` constructor + 8 revolve tests (`for_revolve_face_deterministic` / `for_revolve_face_distinct_across_tag_kinds` / `for_revolve_face_distinct_across_modes` / `for_revolve_face_segments_change_breaks_side_id` / `for_revolve_face_profile_count_change_breaks_side_id` / `for_revolve_face_caps_unaffected_by_segments` / 2 cross-operator distinctness tests vs cuboid + extrude).
     - `loft.rs` (301L): `pub fn for_loft_face(owner, tag) -> Self` constructor + 8 loft tests (`for_loft_face_deterministic` / `for_loft_face_distinct_across_tag_kinds` / `for_loft_face_distinct_across_owners` / `for_loft_face_distinct_for_swapped_profile_counts` / `for_loft_face_handles_unequal_profile_counts_at_constructor_level` / 3 cross-operator distinctness tests vs cuboid + extrude + revolve).
   - **Inherent `impl BRepFaceId` block organization**: each per-operator file's `impl BRepFaceId` block holds its `for_X_face` constructor; Rust resolves these regardless of file location since they all `impl` the same type. `Self::DOMAIN` and `Self::KIND_X` constants stay in `mod.rs`'s `impl BRepFaceId` block (private to `face_id` module — accessible from `face_id::cuboid` / `extrude` / `revolve` / `loft` submodules per normal item visibility — submodules see private items of their parent module).
   - **Per-operator constructor bodies + test bodies are byte-identical to pre-refactor** (function bodies / comments / doc-strings / attribute order all preserved). The only edits permitted (and made) on moved items: imports at file head + the `mod tests` block's `use super::*;` line + (where applicable) imports for cross-operator types (`use crate::topology::face_tag::{CuboidFaceTag, ...};`).
   - **Cross-operator distinctness test placement rule observed** (newer operator's file): `for_extrude_face_distinct_from_for_cuboid_face_with_same_owner` → `extrude.rs`; `for_revolve_face_distinct_from_for_extrude_face_with_same_owner` → `revolve.rs`; `for_revolve_face_distinct_from_for_cuboid_face_with_same_owner` → `revolve.rs`; `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_extrude_face_with_same_owner` → `loft.rs`; `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_cuboid_face_with_same_owner` → `loft.rs`; `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_revolve_face_with_same_owner` → `loft.rs`. This matches the order in which each test was historically added (cross-operator tests landed with the newer operator's sub-dispatch).
   - **SPLIT-EXEMPTION marker REMOVED entirely** — no per-file marker remains in `face_id/mod.rs` or any per-operator file. Verified via `grep -r "SPLIT-EXEMPTION" crates/cad-core/src/topology/` returning empty. The split-exemption lint reports 0 violations and 0 exemptions for the new files.
   - **Files NOT touched** (validation that the refactor was strictly contained): `crates/cad-core/src/topology/{mod.rs, face_tag.rs, provider.rs}` (the existing `pub mod face_id;` in `topology/mod.rs` resolves to either `face_id.rs` OR `face_id/mod.rs` automatically — no edit needed); `crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs` (re-exports unchanged); `crates/cad-core/src/operators/` ANY file (caller code stays byte-identical); `crates/cad-core/tests/` ANY file (integration tests use the same public API); `crates/cad-core/Cargo.toml`; ANY other crate; `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` (the SPLIT-EXEMPTION was an in-file marker, not in this file); `plans/PLAN.md` / `IMPLEMENTATION.md` / `fileandfolderstructure.md` / `versions.md`; `docs/` anything; workspace `Cargo.toml`.
   - **Public API delta**: ZERO. `BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face` / `for_extrude_face` / `for_revolve_face` / `for_loft_face` — all 4 constructors callable from outside the module byte-identically. Caller code in `operators/` + `tests/` + `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel needed zero updates — the inherent `impl` block organization is invisible to consumers.
   - **Resisted expansion-pressure** during shaping (substrate IS the resistance — the dispatch's central success criterion, exactly per the spec's anti-shape directives): rejected centralizing the BLAKE3 derivation boilerplate into a `pub(crate) const DOMAIN_BYTES` + private `fn derive(owner, kind, payload)` helper (centralization is logic restructuring; pure mechanics dispatch); rejected adding any new test "while in there" (1:1 move discipline); rejected merging two tests "for clarity" (1:1 move discipline); rejected adding a `cross_operator.rs` file as a fallback split shape (not strictly necessary — per-operator placement worked); rejected adding any visibility annotations (`pub(super)` / `pub(crate)`) to the `KIND_X` consts (default-private with submodule access works); rejected re-running fmt mid-dispatch (new files came out fmt-clean by following source byte-for-byte).
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings; `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (**308 / 308** tests; zero delta from pre-refactor 308; lib still 211 + integration still 97 = 308); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2009 / 2009 pass** across 222 binaries (zero delta; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0; `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; **`split-exemption` lint reports 0 violations 0 exemptions** for the new files; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31).
   - **Honest framing of dispatch scope**: this dispatch is **NOT** a substrate addition — it is a refactor cleanup that establishes runway for sub-7.2-ε (chain composition across `OperatorGraph`). The per-operator constructor pattern adds ~12 tests + 1 constructor + 1 KIND const per operator dispatch; sub-7.2-ε will want to touch identity construction; landing it on a clean per-operator layout removes the bloat-compounding risk in a 1088-line single file.

2. **D-7.2-δ Loft B-Rep face identity (two-input local-provider)** (bounded substrate dispatch extending sub-7.2-α + sub-7.2-β + sub-7.2-γ to `LoftOp` — the fourth `BRepProvider` impl in cad-core, this time exercising the **two-input local-provider** topology axis: `LoftOp` is the first operator with two profile inputs, and the substrate handles this without leaking into chain-composition territory which is sub-7.2-ε; +19 net workspace tests = 15 lib unit + 4 integration; no new ADR / no new lint / no new doctrine doc / no new §18 companion / no `Operator` trait modification / no `Tessellation` / `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` / `topo_lineage` / `Polygon2D` / `LoftOp` API modification (only the additive `impl BRepProvider for LoftOp` block) / no `CuboidOp` / `ExtrudeOp` / `RevolveOp` modification (sub-7.2-α + sub-7.2-β + sub-7.2-γ impls byte-identical) / no `provider.rs` modification / no prior integration-test files modified / no `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel integration / no Cargo.toml modification / no D-Fillet prep / no fifth operator):
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/face_tag.rs`**: extended with `LoftFaceTag` 3-variant `#[non_exhaustive]` enum in canonical face-emission order matching `LoftOp::evaluate` — `Bottom = 0` (`-Z` cap, `profile_a` lifted to `z = 0`; categorical, no inner data, matching ExtrudeFaceTag::Bottom precedent), `Top = 1` (`+Z` cap, `profile_b` lifted to `z = length`; categorical), `Side { edge_index: u32, profile_a_count: u32, profile_b_count: u32 } = 2` (one per profile-edge pair `(profile_a[i], profile_b[i])` in canonical order Side(0)..Side(N-1)). The `Side` variant carries BOTH `profile_a_count` AND `profile_b_count` independently — this is the load-bearing substrate-honesty guardrail that ensures profile-count changes break face identity by construction (BOTH counts hashed into BLAKE3 input as 4-byte LE), even though `LoftOp::evaluate` enforces equal counts at runtime; the tag does NOT depend on that validation rule, so a hypothetical malformed in-memory `LoftOp` (mid-mutation through pub fields) cannot collide tag identity. 7-clause stability contract pinned in the `LoftFaceTag` docstring: (1) Bottom/Top stable across `length` AND shape-size changes; (2) Bottom/Top categorical (no inner data, matching ExtrudeFaceTag precedent); (3) Side stable across `length` AND coordinate-only profile changes when both counts unchanged; (4) Side breaks across either profile count changing (square → pentagon for either profile or both → disjoint Side ID sets by construction); (5) Side depends on profile-A-count vs profile-B-count ordering (swapping `profile_a` and `profile_b` produces different IDs because the resulting mesh swaps top and bottom, side winding flips); (6) substrate does NOT inspect profile coordinates (rotation / twist matching / vertex-pairing offset OUT OF SCOPE for v0; same explicit limit as ExtrudeFaceTag and RevolveFaceTag); (7) no twist-matching implied (future twist param requires new variant or field). Module-doc updated to enumerate four face-tag enums + clarify v0 NON-GOALS now exclude `BooleanOp` / `SweepOp` / `TransformOp` (Loft folded in).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/face_id.rs`**: imports widened to `super::face_tag::{CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag}`; new `KIND_LOFT: &'static [u8] = b"loft:"` const alongside existing `KIND_CUBOID` / `KIND_EXTRUDE` / `KIND_REVOLVE`; new constructor `BRepFaceId::for_loft_face(owner: BRepOwnerId, tag: LoftFaceTag) -> Self` with BLAKE3 input layout `DOMAIN || owner.as_bytes() || b"loft:" || tag.discriminant() || (Side ONLY: edge_index.to_le_bytes() (4 bytes) || profile_a_count.to_le_bytes() (4 bytes) || profile_b_count.to_le_bytes() (4 bytes))` truncated to first 16 bytes. For caps (`Bottom` / `Top`) the BLAKE3 input ends after the discriminant byte — no inner data — so cap IDs are stable across `length`, profile-coordinate, and profile-count changes (categorical caps; same explicit limit as ExtrudeFaceTag). The order of the two profile counts in the BLAKE3 input is `profile_a_count` THEN `profile_b_count`; this ordering is **load-bearing** because swapping a Loft's `profile_a` and `profile_b` produces a geometrically-different mesh, and the IDs SHOULD differ to reflect that. Documented in the `for_loft_face` docstring. `face_id.rs` reached 1078 lines so a `// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation was added to its head (single bare flag — no exemptions in `exemptions.toml` per the lint design); the rationale documents the cohesive owner-seed + per-operator face-identity constructor module that grows by ~12 tests + 1 constructor + 1 KIND const per per-operator BRepProvider sub-dispatch (sub-7.2-α/β/γ/δ landed; ε / ζ / further operators pending), and notes that splitting per-operator constructors into separate files would introduce module-boundary friction and duplicate the BLAKE3 derivation protocol across N files.
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/operators/loft.rs`**: imports widened to add `crate::tessellation::TopologyFaceId` and `crate::topology::{BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, LoftFaceTag}`; new additive `impl BRepProvider for LoftOp` block (~70L) below the existing `impl Operator for LoftOp` returning `N + 2` pairs in canonical emission order: `(TopologyFaceId(0), Bottom)`, `(TopologyFaceId(1), Top)`, then for `i in 0..n` `(TopologyFaceId(2 + u64::from(i)), Side { edge_index: i, profile_a_count: n_a, profile_b_count: n_b })`. The defensive `n_a.min(n_b)` cap defends against a hypothetical mutation through the `pub profile_a` / `pub profile_b` fields between construction and `brep_face_ids` call (Polygon2D doesn't expose interior mutability today, but the fields are publicly assignable); cost is negligible and removes a panic surface. The `n_a` / `n_b` cast pattern `u32::try_from(self.profile_x.len()).unwrap_or(u32::MAX)` mirrors the `extrude.rs` precedent. NO modification to existing `evaluate` / `validate` / `structural_hash` / `Default` / `op_kind` / `arity` / `new` / existing tests.
   - **Critical design constraints pinned in docstrings** (load-bearing): all stability properties from sub-7.2-α + sub-7.2-β + sub-7.2-γ preserved verbatim (caller-supplied opaque owner seed, NOT derived from `NodeId` / `effective_hash`; `b"rge.cad.brep.face/v1:"` domain separator; literal-byte-string operator-kind tags `b"cuboid:"` / `b"extrude:"` / `b"revolve:"` / `b"loft:"` NOT `OpKind` discriminant). The new `LoftFaceTag` 7-clause stability contract layered on top.
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/topology/mod.rs`**: re-export widened from `pub use face_tag::{CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` to `pub use face_tag::{CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};`. Module-doc updated from `(sub-7.2-α + sub-7.2-β + sub-7.2-γ)` framing to `(sub-7.2-α + sub-7.2-β + sub-7.2-γ + sub-7.2-δ)`; module-doc enumerates the new `LoftFaceTag` substrate-honesty guardrail (BOTH profile counts independently hashed) + A→B-ordering rule (swapping profiles produces different IDs).
   - **`crates/cad-core/src/lib.rs`**: re-export widened from `pub use topology::{BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` to `pub use topology::{BRepFaceId, BRepOwnerId, BRepProvider, CuboidFaceTag, ExtrudeFaceTag, LoftFaceTag, RevolveFaceTag, RevolveMode};` (alphabetical order preserved; rustfmt formatted as multi-line block).
   - **NEW `crates/cad-core/tests/loft_face_identity_smoke.rs`** (~190L; 4 integration tests): the rebuild-stability gate `loft_face_ids_stable_across_length_changes` — same square profiles, three `length` values 1.0/2.0/0.5, all 6 face IDs byte-identical via `assert_eq!(ids_a, ids_b); assert_eq!(ids_b, ids_c); assert_eq!(ids_a.len(), 6);`. The shape-size-stability gate `loft_face_ids_stable_across_shape_size_changes` — unit square (1×1) vs 3-unit square (3×3) at the same point count + length=1; asserts byte-identical IDs across all 6 faces because the substrate does NOT inspect coordinate values. The substrate-honesty integration gate `loft_face_ids_break_when_both_profile_counts_change_together` — square → pentagon (BOTH profiles change together because LoftOp::evaluate enforces equal counts at runtime); asserts `ids_sq.len() == 6` and `ids_pen.len() == 7`; asserts Bottom/Top IDs MATCH between the two (caps' BLAKE3 input does NOT hash either profile count in, so `ids_sq[0] == ids_pen[0]` and `ids_sq[1] == ids_pen[1]` are CORRECT and EXPECTED per the categorical-cap clauses 1-2 of the stability contract); then nested-loop asserts every Side ID across the two is disjoint via `for sq_side in &ids_sq[2..] { for pen_side in &ids_pen[2..] { assert_ne!(sq_side, pen_side, "Side IDs must NOT collide across profile-count change"); } }`. The owner-disambiguation gate `loft_face_ids_distinct_across_owners` — owners `[0x11; 16]` and `[0x22; 16]` produce disjoint identity spaces (mirrors cuboid / extrude / revolve precedent). Pentagon coordinates used for the integration test: regular pentagon at unit radius `[(1.0, 0.0), (0.309, 0.951), (-0.809, 0.588), (-0.809, -0.588), (0.309, -0.951)]` (5 finite CCW points; passes Polygon2D::new + LoftOp's evaluate-time convexity check).
   - **Unit tests (lib)**: `face_tag.rs` adds 4 — `loft_face_tag_serde_round_trip` (5 variants via ron: Bottom, Top, 3 Side variants including unequal-count Side {0, 4, 5} which substrate-handles cleanly even though LoftOp::evaluate would reject it), `loft_face_tag_non_exhaustive_pattern_compiles` (mirrors ExtrudeFaceTag precedent with `Side { .. }` arm + wildcard), `loft_side_distinct_for_distinct_edge_indices` (constructor-level — `Side {0, 4, 4}` vs `Side {1, 4, 4}` distinct via PartialEq; same-key equal; Bottom/Top/Side all pairwise distinct), **`loft_side_distinct_for_distinct_profile_counts` (substrate-honesty test #1 at the tag level — four combinations `(4, 4) / (5, 4) / (4, 5) / (5, 5)` produce four pairwise-distinct tags via PartialEq, pinning the BOTH-counts-independently-distinguish guarantee at the enum level)**. `face_id.rs` adds 8 — `for_loft_face_deterministic` (4 tags × 2 calls byte-identical including Side {0, 4, 4} and Side {7, 12, 12}), `for_loft_face_distinct_across_tag_kinds` (Bottom / Top / Side {0, 4, 4} pairwise distinct under same owner), `for_loft_face_distinct_across_owners` (3 tags × 2 owners), **`for_loft_face_distinct_for_swapped_profile_counts` (substrate-honesty test #2 — `Side { 0, 4, 5 }` ≠ `Side { 0, 5, 4 }` via assert_ne with explicit failure message "side IDs must differ when profile_a_count and profile_b_count are swapped"; pins the A→B-ordering load-bearing role)**, **`for_loft_face_handles_unequal_profile_counts_at_constructor_level` (substrate-honesty guardrail — exercises `Side { 0, 4, 5 }` directly, asserts the BRepFaceId's bytes length is 16 (finite), and asserts the unequal-count ID is distinct from both `Side { 0, 4, 4 }` and `Side { 0, 5, 5 }` with explicit failure messages "unequal-count Side ID must NOT collide with Side(0, 4, 4)" and "unequal-count Side ID must NOT collide with Side(0, 5, 5)"; this is THE GUARDRAIL TEST proving the substrate is genuinely self-describing and doesn't depend on `LoftOp::evaluate`'s validation rule)**, `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_extrude_face_with_same_owner` (cross-operator separator check — Bottom (discriminant 0) vs Bottom (discriminant 0) under same owner produce different IDs purely because of `b"loft:"` vs `b"extrude:"`), `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_cuboid_face_with_same_owner` (cross-operator separator check — `b"loft:"` vs `b"cuboid:"`), `for_loft_face_distinct_from_for_revolve_face_with_same_owner` (cross-operator separator check — `b"loft:"` vs `b"revolve:"`). `loft.rs` adds 3 — `brep_provider_returns_n_plus_2_pairs_for_squares` (two squares N=4 → 6 pairs), `brep_provider_returns_n_plus_2_pairs_for_pentagons` (two pentagons N=5 → 7 pairs), `brep_provider_topology_face_ids_are_canonical_emission_order` (verifies TopologyFaceId(0)=Bottom, TopologyFaceId(1)=Top, TopologyFaceId(2+i)=Side(i, 4, 4) byte-identically for i in 0..4).
   - **HARD NON-GOALS observed during shaping** (substrate IS the resistance — the spec discipline holds across all expansion-pressure points; the dispatch's central success criterion): no edges / vertices / `BRepEdgeId` / `EdgeTag` enums (sub-7.2-ζ); no fifth operator's `BRepProvider` impl — Boolean / Sweep / Transform stay un-tagged; **no coordinate-aware identity / rotation detection** — profile-vertex-order rotation at the same count produces the same `Side(i)` ID, documented as a v0 limit; **no twist-matching implied** — `LoftOp` v0 pairs `profile_a[i]` with `profile_b[i]`; future twist parameter would require a new `LoftFaceTag` variant or new field, NOT a quiet behavior change in the existing tag; **no profile-vertex-pairing offset** — shifting which `profile_a[i]` matches `profile_b[j]` is OUT OF SCOPE for v0; **no raw-geometry hashing** — neither profile coordinates nor length is hashed; **no collapsing of the two-count Side tag** to a single shared `profile_count` "since they must be equal anyway" (REJECTED — defeats the substrate-honesty guardrail this dispatch is built on; resisted explicitly); **no fourth `LoftFaceTag` variant** ("TwistedSide"? "OffsetCap"? — REJECTED, the substrate-honesty principle says three variants is enough for v0); **no chain composition** / Transform inheritance (sub-7.2-ε); no `Operator` trait modification (sibling trait); no `Tessellation` modification; no `OperatorNode` / `OperatorGraph` / `topo_lineage` / `Polygon2D` / `LoftOp` API modification; no `CuboidOp` / `ExtrudeOp` / `RevolveOp` modification (prior `BRepProvider` impls byte-identical — verified by re-reading those files); no `provider.rs` modification (trait already correct from sub-7.2-α); no prior integration-test files modified (`brep_face_identity_smoke.rs`, `extrude_face_identity_smoke.rs`, `revolve_face_identity_smoke.rs` byte-identical); no `cad-projection` / `gfx` / kernel integration; no D-Fillet prep; no new ADR / no new lint / no new doctrine doc / no new §18 companion / no PLAN edits / no IMPLEMENTATION.md edits / no version-suffix migration machinery / no Cargo.toml modifications / no `tools/architecture-lints/exemptions.toml` modification.
   - **Verification gates ALL GREEN**: `cargo build --workspace -j 2` 0 errors / 0 new warnings (~110 pre-existing ui-theme `missing_docs` warnings unchanged); `cargo test -p rge-cad-core --all-targets --no-fail-fast` PASS (308 / 308 tests; was 289; +19 net = 15 lib + 4 integration; cad-core lib goes 226 → 241, integration 63 → 67); `cargo test --workspace --all-targets --no-fail-fast -j 2` = **2009 / 2009 pass** across 222 binaries (was 1990; +19 net = exactly the cad-core delta; +1 binary for the new integration test; 3 ignored unchanged); `cargo +nightly fmt --check` exit 0; `cargo run -q -p rge-tool-architecture-lints -- all` exit 0 (9 enforcement + 1 supplementary all PASS; substantive lint exemption count unchanged at 0; rollout-debt count unchanged at 31). The split-exemption lint flagged `face_id.rs` at 1078L during the first lint run; remediated within MAY-list by adding a `// SPLIT-EXEMPTION:` annotation to the file's head (in-file comment, NOT an `exemptions.toml` entry — the lint design has `split-exemption` as a single bare flag with no .toml exemption surface).
   - **Public API delta**: + `LoftFaceTag` (one new type at crate root, alphabetically inserted into `pub use topology::{...};`) + `BRepFaceId::for_loft_face` constructor + `LoftOp: BRepProvider` impl. Existing public surface UNCHANGED (`Operator` / `OperatorNode` / `Tessellation` / `OperatorGraph` / `TopologyFaceId` / `Polygon2D` / `LoftOp` / `CuboidFaceTag` / `ExtrudeFaceTag` / `RevolveFaceTag` / `RevolveMode` / `BRepFaceId` / `BRepOwnerId` / `BRepProvider` types byte-identical; `BRepFaceId::for_cuboid_face` / `for_extrude_face` / `for_revolve_face` and `CuboidOp: BRepProvider` / `ExtrudeOp: BRepProvider` / `RevolveOp: BRepProvider` impls byte-identical).
   - **`impl BRepProvider` count in cad-core after this dispatch**: exactly **4** (Cuboid + Extrude + Revolve + Loft).
